Cease from anger, and leave rage; have no emulation to do evil.


<a id="org73cfc13"></a>

## Psalms 36:9

For evildoers shall be cut off: but they that wait upon the Lord, they shall inherit the land.


<a id="org6df7b9d"></a>

## Psalms 36:10

For yet a little while, and the wicked shall not be: and thou shalt seek his place, and shalt not find it.


<a id="orga628239"></a>

## Psalms 36:11

But the meek shall inherit the land, and shall delight in abundance of peace.


<a id="orgc9750d2"></a>

## Psalms 36:12

The sinner shall watch the just man: and shall gnash upon him with his teeth.


<a id="orgc3bc140"></a>

## Psalms 36:13

But the Lord shall laugh at him: for he foreseeth that his day shall come.


<a id="orgad66bc1"></a>

## Psalms 36:14

The wicked have drawn out the sword: they have bent their bow. To cast down the poor and needy, to kill the upright of heart.


<a id="org9c05a8c"></a>

## Psalms 36:15

Let their sword enter into their own hearts, and let their bow be broken.


<a id="org44afd20"></a>

## Psalms 36:16

Better is a little to the just, than the great riches of the wicked.


<a id="orgd1acd4f"></a>

## Psalms 36:17

For the arms of the wicked shall be broken in pieces; but the Lord strengtheneth the just.


<a id="orgbdfc719"></a>

## Psalms 36:18

The Lord knoweth the days of the undefiled; and their inheritance shall be for ever.


<a id="orgefad3d5"></a>

## Psalms 36:19

They shall not be confounded in the evil time; and in the days of famine they shall be filled:


<a id="orgf1cf456"></a>

## Psalms 36:20

Because the wicked shall perish. And the enemies of the Lord, presently after they shall be honoured and exalted, shall come to nothing and vanish like smoke.


<a id="orgf9e8b26"></a>

## Psalms 36:21

The sinner shall borrow, and not pay again; but the just sheweth mercy and shall give.


<a id="orgd865558"></a>

## Psalms 36:22

For such as bless him shall inherit the land: but such as curse him shall perish.


<a id="org95c8ab6"></a>

## Psalms 36:23

With the Lord shall the steps of a man be directed, and he shall like well his way.


<a id="org602cc1d"></a>

## Psalms 36:24

When he shall fall he shall not be bruised, for the Lord putteth his hand under him.


<a id="orgbfa4826"></a>

## Psalms 36:25

I have been young and now am old; and I have not seen the just forsaken, nor his seed seeking bread.


<a id="orgb661855"></a>

## Psalms 36:26

He sheweth mercy, and lendeth all the day long; and his seed shall be in blessing.


<a id="org51d6be7"></a>

## Psalms 36:27

Decline from evil and do good, and dwell for ever and ever.


<a id="org0536988"></a>

## Psalms 36:28

For the Lord loveth judgment, and will not forsake his saints: they shall be preserved for ever. The unjust shall be punished, and the seed of the wicked shall perish.


<a id="org847ba6e"></a>

## Psalms 36:29

But the just shall inherit the land, and shall dwell therein for evermore.


<a id="org6db666f"></a>

## Psalms 36:30

The mouth of the just shall meditate wisdom: and his tongue shall speak judgment.


<a id="org66e7a92"></a>

## Psalms 36:31

The law of his God is in his heart, and his steps shall not be supplanted.


<a id="orgac74bc1"></a>

## Psalms 36:32

The wicked watcheth the just man, and seeketh to put him to death,


<a id="org8cd8682"></a>

## Psalms 36:33

But the Lord will not leave him in his hands; nor condemn him when he shall be judged.


<a id="orga77f472"></a>

## Psalms 36:34

Expect the Lord and keep his way: and he will exalt thee to inherit the land: when the sinners shall perish thou shalt see.


<a id="org1c4ec6d"></a>

## Psalms 36:35

I have seen the wicked highly exalted, and lifted up like the cedars of Libanus.


<a id="org93ea300"></a>

## Psalms 36:36

And I passed by, and lo, he was not: and I sought him and his place was not found.


<a id="orgd7c36e6"></a>

## Psalms 36:37

Keep innocence, and behold justice: for there are remnants for the peaceable man.


<a id="org417d813"></a>

## Psalms 36:38

But the unjust shall be destroyed together: the remnants of the wicked shall perish.


<a id="org68e3fe1"></a>

## Psalms 36:39

But the salvation of the just is from the Lord, and he is their protector in the time of trouble.


<a id="org779c740"></a>

## Psalms 36:40

And the Lord will help them and deliver them: and he will rescue them from the wicked, and save them because they have hoped in him. <chapter eID=&ldquo;gen15785&rdquo; osisID=&ldquo;Ps.36&rdquo;/>


<a id="orgf9b2fb3"></a>

# Psalms 37


<a id="org11b2b65"></a>

## Psalms 37:1

A psalm for David, for a remembrance of the sabbath.


<a id="orgfbcc4ed"></a>

## Psalms 37:2

Rebuke me not, O Lord, in thy indignation; nor chastise me in thy wrath.


<a id="orgc929c89"></a>

## Psalms 37:3

For thy arrows are fastened in me: and thy hand hath been strong upon me.


<a id="orgecd5cb2"></a>

## Psalms 37:4

There is no health in my flesh, because of thy wrath: there is no peace for my bones, because of my sins.


<a id="org6f85365"></a>

## Psalms 37:5

For my iniquities are gone over my head: and as a heavy burden are become heavy upon me.


<a id="org42eb374"></a>

## Psalms 37:6

My sores are putrefied and corrupted, because of my foolishness.


<a id="org2ae1a0e"></a>

## Psalms 37:7

I am become miserable, and am bowed down even to the end: I walked sorrowful all the day long.


<a id="org14b88a4"></a>

## Psalms 37:8

For my loins are filled with illusions; and there is no health in my flesh.


<a id="org52e1504"></a>

## Psalms 37:9

I am afflicted and humbled exceedingly: I roared with the groaning of my heart.


<a id="org812727f"></a>

## Psalms 37:10

Lord, all my desire is before thee, and my groaning is not hidden from thee.


<a id="orgb355c8e"></a>

## Psalms 37:11

My heart is troubled, my strength hath left me, and the light of my eyes itself is not with me.


<a id="org9251835"></a>

## Psalms 37:12

My friends and my neighbours have drawn near, and stood against me. And they that were near me stood afar off:


<a id="orga420973"></a>

## Psalms 37:13

And they that sought my soul used violence. And they that sought evils to me spoke vain things, and studied deceits all the day long.


<a id="org337a094"></a>

## Psalms 37:14

But I, as a deaf man, heard not: and as a dumb man not opening his mouth.


<a id="org8be9fb7"></a>

## Psalms 37:15

And I became as a man that heareth not: and that hath no reproofs in his mouth.


<a id="orge496f62"></a>

## Psalms 37:16

For in thee, O Lord, have I hoped: thou wilt hear me, O Lord my God.


<a id="org9ac13be"></a>

## Psalms 37:17

For I said: Lest at any time my enemies rejoice over me: and whilst my feet are moved, they speak great things against me.


<a id="org61bd944"></a>

## Psalms 37:18

For I am ready for scourges: and my sorrow is continually before me.


<a id="org8c3c4ed"></a>

## Psalms 37:19

For I will declare my iniquity: and I will think for my sin.


<a id="org33025a6"></a>

## Psalms 37:20

But my enemies live, and are stronger than I: and they that hate me wrongfully are multiplied.


<a id="orgfb29995"></a>

## Psalms 37:21

They that render evil for good, have detracted me, because I followed goodness.


<a id="orgd6923e7"></a>

## Psalms 37:22

For sake me not, O Lord my God: do not thou depart from me.


<a id="org213d38c"></a>

## Psalms 37:23

Attend unto my help, O Lord, the God of my salvation. <chapter eID=&ldquo;gen15826&rdquo; osisID=&ldquo;Ps.37&rdquo;/>


<a id="org20cfec6"></a>

# Psalms 38


<a id="orgd0cbbc9"></a>

## Psalms 38:1

Unto the end, for Idithun himself, a canticle of David.


<a id="org4c10a95"></a>

## Psalms 38:2

I said: I will take heed to my ways: that I sin not with my tongue. I have set a guard to my mouth, when the sinner stood against me.


<a id="orgcd7f850"></a>

## Psalms 38:3

I was dumb, and was humbled, and kept silence from good things: and my sorrow was renewed.


<a id="orgf6f4d6d"></a>

## Psalms 38:4

My heart grew hot within me: and in my meditation a fire shall flame out.


<a id="org192c308"></a>

## Psalms 38:5

I spoke with my tongue: O Lord, make me know my end. And what is the number of my days: that I may know what is wanting to me.


<a id="orgd2ec7fc"></a>

## Psalms 38:6

Behold thou hast made my days measurable. and my substance is as nothing before thee. And indeed all things are vanity: every man living.


<a id="org27d92e7"></a>

## Psalms 38:7

Surely man passeth as an image: yea, and he is disquieted in vain. He storeth up: and he knoweth not for whom he shall gather these things.


<a id="org541b0b8"></a>

## Psalms 38:8

And now what is my hope? is it not the Lord? and my substance is with thee.


<a id="orgc50de2b"></a>

## Psalms 38:9

Deliver thou me from all my iniquities: thou hast made me a reproach to the fool.


<a id="org7bde790"></a>

## Psalms 38:10

I was dumb, and I opened not my mouth, because thou hast done it.


<a id="org7eb44e7"></a>

## Psalms 38:11

Remove thy scourges from me. The strength of thy hand hath made me faint in rebukes:


<a id="org8230bb8"></a>

## Psalms 38:12

Thou hast corrected man for iniquity. And thou hast made his soul to waste away like a spider: surely in vain is any man disquieted.


<a id="orga304f80"></a>

## Psalms 38:13

Hear my prayer, O Lord, and my supplication: give ear to my tears. Be no silent: for I am a stranger with thee, and a sojourner as all my fathers were.


<a id="org4f87f8b"></a>

## Psalms 38:14

O forgive me, that I may be refreshed, before I go hence, and be no more. <chapter eID=&ldquo;gen15850&rdquo; osisID=&ldquo;Ps.38&rdquo;/>


<a id="orge1ebc64"></a>

# Psalms 39


<a id="orgbe4ad95"></a>

## Psalms 39:1

Unto the end, a psalm for David himself.


<a id="org8a85dbb"></a>

## Psalms 39:2

With expectation I have waited for the Lord, and he was attentive to me.


<a id="org9d9eab7"></a>

## Psalms 39:3

And he heard my prayers, and brought me out of the pit of misery and the mire of dregs. And he set my feet upon a rock, and directed my steps.


<a id="org78f9b5f"></a>

## Psalms 39:4

And he put a new canticle into my mouth, a song to our God. Many shall see, and shall fear: and they shall hope in the Lord.


<a id="orgac3a41b"></a>

## Psalms 39:5

Blessed is the man whose trust is in the name of the Lord; and who hath not had regard to vanities, and lying follies.


<a id="orgd0a8ebb"></a>

## Psalms 39:6

Thou hast multiplied thy wonderful works, O Lord my God: and in thy thoughts there is no one like to thee. I have declared and I have spoken they are multiplied above number.


<a id="org9ca89bd"></a>

## Psalms 39:7

Sacrifice and oblation thou didst not desire; but thou hast pierced ears for me. Burnt offering and sin offering thou didst not require:


<a id="org530c4f2"></a>

## Psalms 39:8

Then said I, Behold I come. In the head of the book it is written of me


<a id="orgd3d7451"></a>

## Psalms 39:9

That I should do thy will: O my God, I have desired it, and thy law in the midst of my heart.


<a id="org96a817a"></a>

## Psalms 39:10

I have declared thy justice in a great church, lo, I will not restrain my lips: O Lord, thou knowest it.


<a id="org3332c69"></a>

## Psalms 39:11

I have not hid thy justice within my heart: I have declared thy truth and thy salvation. I have not concealed thy mercy and thy truth from a great council.


<a id="org911783c"></a>

## Psalms 39:12

Withhold not thou, O Lord, thy tender mercies from me: thy mercy and thy truth have always upheld me.


<a id="org976a206"></a>

## Psalms 39:13

For evils without number have surrounded me; my iniquities have overtaken me, and I was not able to see. They are multiplied above the hairs of my head: and my heart hath forsaken me.


<a id="org7fc1205"></a>

## Psalms 39:14

Be pleased, O Lord, to deliver me. Look down, O Lord, to help me.


<a id="org6ee2790"></a>

## Psalms 39:15

Let them be confounded and ashamed together, that seek after my soul to take it away. Let them be turned backward and be ashamed that desire evils to me.


<a id="orga1782a3"></a>

## Psalms 39:16

Let them immediately bear their confusion, that say to me: &rsquo;Tis well, &rsquo;tis well.


<a id="orgd895b53"></a>

## Psalms 39:17

Let all that seek thee rejoice and be glad in thee: and let such as love thy salvation say always: The Lord be magnified.


<a id="orgb79de5a"></a>

## Psalms 39:18

But I am a beggar and poor: the Lord is careful for me. Thou art my helper and my protector: O my God, be not slack. <chapter eID=&ldquo;gen15865&rdquo; osisID=&ldquo;Ps.39&rdquo;/>


<a id="org26aa45c"></a>

# Psalms 40


<a id="org1a5c350"></a>

## Psalms 40:1

Unto the end, a psalm for David himself.


<a id="org7bc0f27"></a>

## Psalms 40:2

Blessed is he that understandeth concerning the needy and the poor: the Lord will deliver him in the evil day.


<a id="org986aba2"></a>

## Psalms 40:3

The Lord preserve him and give him life, and make him blessed upon the earth: and deliver him not up to the will of his enemies.


<a id="org921b4c3"></a>

## Psalms 40:4

The Lord help him on his bed of sorrow: thou hast turned all his couch in his sickness.


<a id="orge41fcd8"></a>

## Psalms 40:5

I said: O Lord, be thou merciful to me: heal my soul, for I have sinned against thee.


<a id="org377f379"></a>

## Psalms 40:6

My enemies have spoken evils against me: when shall he die and his name perish?


<a id="org190f751"></a>

## Psalms 40:7

And if he came in to see me, he spoke vain things: his heart gathered together iniquity to itself. He went out and spoke to the same purpose.


<a id="org5983a96"></a>

## Psalms 40:8

All my enemies whispered together against me: they devised evils to me.


<a id="org738a292"></a>

## Psalms 40:9

They determined against me an unjust word: shall he that sleepeth rise again no more?


<a id="org64e4eab"></a>

## Psalms 40:10

For even the man of my peace, in whom I trusted, who ate my bread, hath greatly supplanted me.


<a id="orge37d41e"></a>

## Psalms 40:11

But thou, O Lord, have mercy on me, and raise me up again: and I will requite them.


<a id="orga659053"></a>

## Psalms 40:12

By this I know, that thou hast had a good will for me: because my enemy shall not rejoice over me.


<a id="org8a26374"></a>

## Psalms 40:13

But thou hast upheld me by reason of my innocence: and hast established me in thy sight for ever.


<a id="orga8c2cfd"></a>

## Psalms 40:14

Blessed be the Lord the God of Israel from eternity to eternity. So be it. So be it. <chapter eID=&ldquo;gen15884&rdquo; osisID=&ldquo;Ps.40&rdquo;/>


<a id="orge596b3e"></a>

# Psalms 41


<a id="orga0f446c"></a>

## Psalms 41:1

Unto the end, understanding for the sons of Core.


<a id="org42ca96c"></a>

## Psalms 41:2

As the hart panteth after the fountains of water; so my soul panteth after thee, O God.


<a id="orgdfda370"></a>

## Psalms 41:3

My soul hath thirsted after the strong living God; when shall I come and appear before the face of God?


<a id="org078769c"></a>

## Psalms 41:4

My tears have been my bread day and night, whilst it is said to me daily: Where is thy God?


<a id="org46f24f5"></a>

## Psalms 41:5

These things I remembered, and poured out my soul in me: for I shall go over into the place of the wonderful tabernacle, even to the house of God: With the voice of joy and praise; the noise of one feasting.


<a id="orgf64cec7"></a>

## Psalms 41:6

Why art thou sad, O my soul? and why dost thou trouble me? Hope in God, for I will still give praise to him: the salvation of my countenance,


<a id="orgdf0a595"></a>

## Psalms 41:7

And my God. My soul is troubled within my self: therefore will I remember thee from the land of Jordan and Hermoniim, from the little hill.


<a id="org1b5618f"></a>

## Psalms 41:8

Deep calleth on deep, at the noise of thy flood-gates. All thy heights and thy billows have passed over me.


<a id="orgb3db02c"></a>

## Psalms 41:9

In the daytime the Lord hath commanded his mercy; and a canticle to him in the night. With me is prayer to the God of my life.


<a id="org83695ac"></a>

## Psalms 41:10

I will say to God: Thou art my support. Why hast thou forgotten me? and why go I mourning, whilst my enemy afflicteth me?


<a id="org3aade62"></a>

## Psalms 41:11

Whilst my bones are broken, my enemies who trouble me have reproached me; Whilst they say to me day by day: Where is thy God?


<a id="org82d5a7b"></a>

## Psalms 41:12

Why art thou cast down, O my soul? and why dost thou disquiet me? Hope thou in God, for I will still give praise to him: the salvation of my countenance, and my God. <chapter eID=&ldquo;gen15899&rdquo; osisID=&ldquo;Ps.41&rdquo;/>


<a id="org59a9439"></a>

# Psalms 42


<a id="orgae71c16"></a>

## Psalms 42:1

A psalm for David. Judge me, O God, and distinguish my cause from the nation that is not holy: deliver me from the unjust and deceitful man.


<a id="org2084dbb"></a>

## Psalms 42:2

For thou art God my strength: why hast thou cast me off? and why do I go sorrowful whilst the enemy afflicteth me?


<a id="org1c4c4a1"></a>

## Psalms 42:3

Sent forth thy light and thy truth: they have conducted me, and brought me unto thy holy hill, and into thy tabernacles.


<a id="orgffb96a8"></a>

## Psalms 42:4

And I will go in to the altar of God: to God who giveth joy to my youth.


<a id="org18240f9"></a>

## Psalms 42:5

To thee, O God my God, I will give praise upon the harp: why art thou sad, O my soul? and why dost thou disquiet me?


<a id="org38d2588"></a>

## Psalms 42:6

Hope in God, for I will still give praise to him: the salvation of my countenance, and my God. <chapter eID=&ldquo;gen15912&rdquo; osisID=&ldquo;Ps.42&rdquo;/>


<a id="orgd4379a6"></a>

# Psalms 43


<a id="org7335acf"></a>

## Psalms 43:1

Unto the end, for the sons of Core, to give understanding.


<a id="org946b6fa"></a>

## Psalms 43:2

We have heard, O God, with our ears: our fathers have declared to us, The work thou hast wrought in their days, and in the days of old.


<a id="org8604966"></a>

## Psalms 43:3

Thy hand destroyed the Gentiles, and thou plantedst them: thou didst afflict the people and cast them out.


<a id="orgb2a5deb"></a>

## Psalms 43:4

For they got not the possession of the land by their own sword: neither did their own arm save them. But thy right hand and thy arm, and the light of thy countenance: because thou wast pleased with them.


<a id="org94c0af9"></a>

## Psalms 43:5

Thou art thyself my king and my God, who commandest the saving of Jacob.


<a id="orgc14aaa9"></a>

## Psalms 43:6

Through thee we will push down our enemies with the horn: and through thy name we will despise them that rise up against us.


<a id="orgbe0f392"></a>

## Psalms 43:7

For I will not trust in my bow: neither shall my sword save me.


<a id="org3351779"></a>

## Psalms 43:8

But thou hast saved us from them that afflict us: and hast put them to shame that hate us.


<a id="org564ebc5"></a>

## Psalms 43:9

In God shall we glory all the day long: and in thy name we will give praise for ever.


<a id="org2121768"></a>

## Psalms 43:10

But now thou hast cast us off, and put us to shame: and thou , O God, wilt not go out with our armies.


<a id="org971a336"></a>

## Psalms 43:11

Thou hast made us turn our back to our enemies: and they that hated us plundered for themselves.


<a id="orgfa50b2f"></a>

## Psalms 43:12

Thou hast given us up like sheep to be eaten: thou hast scattered us among the nations.


<a id="org8882f47"></a>

## Psalms 43:13

Thou hast sold thy people for no price: and there was no reckoning in the exchange of them.


<a id="orgf6fd32e"></a>

## Psalms 43:14

Thou hast made us a reproach to our neighbours, a scoff and derision to them that are round about us.


<a id="orgb773f1c"></a>

## Psalms 43:15

Thou hast made us a byword among the Gentiles: a shaking of the head among the people.


<a id="org7371765"></a>

## Psalms 43:16

All the day long my shame is before me: and the confusion of my face hath covered me,


<a id="org4d48543"></a>

## Psalms 43:17

At the voice of him that reproacheth and detracteth me: at the face of the enemy and persecutor.


<a id="orgfcc182a"></a>

## Psalms 43:18

All these things have come upon us, yet we have not forgotten thee: and we have not done wickedly in thy covenant.


<a id="org1a442f9"></a>

## Psalms 43:19

And our heart hath not turned back: neither hast thou turned aside our steps from thy way.


<a id="org40282e1"></a>

## Psalms 43:20

For thou hast humbled us in the place of affliction: and the shadow of death hath covered us.


<a id="org37e354b"></a>

## Psalms 43:21

If we have forgotten the name of our God, and if we have spread forth our hands to a strange god:


<a id="org683996f"></a>

## Psalms 43:22

Shall not God search out these things: for he knoweth the secrets of the heart. Because for thy sake we are killed all the day long: we are counted as sheep for the slaughter.


<a id="orgcfc2cec"></a>

## Psalms 43:23

Arise, why sleepest thou, O Lord? arise, and cast us not off to the end.


<a id="org16048c8"></a>

## Psalms 43:24

Why turnest thou thy face away? and forgettest our want and our trouble?


<a id="org201a17a"></a>

## Psalms 43:25

For our soul is humbled down to the dust: our belly cleaveth to the earth.


<a id="org9bc1c97"></a>

## Psalms 43:26

Arise, O Lord, help us and redeem us for thy name&rsquo;s sake. <chapter eID=&ldquo;gen15919&rdquo; osisID=&ldquo;Ps.43&rdquo;/>


<a id="orgbf16f3f"></a>

# Psalms 44


<a id="org0e8e409"></a>

## Psalms 44:1

Unto the end, for them that shall be changed, for the sons of Core, for understanding. A canticle for the Beloved.


<a id="orgc344fae"></a>

## Psalms 44:2

My heart hath uttered a good word: I speak my works to the king: My tongue is the pen of a scrivener that writeth swiftly.


<a id="org85416a1"></a>

## Psalms 44:3

Thou art beautiful above the sons of men: grace is poured abroad in thy lips; therefore hath God blessed thee for ever.


<a id="orga164a2c"></a>

## Psalms 44:4

Gird thy sword upon thy thigh, O thou most mighty.


<a id="org01c4d3d"></a>

## Psalms 44:5

With thy comeliness and thy beauty set out, proceed prosperously, and reign. Because of truth and meekness and justice: and thy right hand shall conduct thee wonderfully.


<a id="org4d45205"></a>

## Psalms 44:6

Thy arrows are sharp: under thee shall people fall, into the hearts of the king&rsquo;s enemies.


<a id="orgd8898de"></a>

## Psalms 44:7

Thy throne, O God, is forever and ever: the sceptre of thy kingdom is a sceptre of uprightness.


<a id="org76a817f"></a>

## Psalms 44:8

Thou hast loved justice, and hated iniquity: therefore God, thy God, hath anointed thee with the oil of gladness above thy fellows.


<a id="orgec977aa"></a>

## Psalms 44:9

Myrrh and stacte and cassia perfume thy garments, from the ivory houses: out of which


<a id="org39a2d37"></a>

## Psalms 44:10

The daughters of kings have delighted thee in thy glory. The queen stood on thy right hand, in gilded clothing; surrounded with variety.


<a id="org4b534d5"></a>

## Psalms 44:11

Hearken, O daughter, and see, and incline thy ear: and forget thy people and thy father&rsquo;s house.


<a id="org77b4c03"></a>

## Psalms 44:12

And the king shall greatly desire thy beauty; for he is the Lord thy God, and him they shall adore.


<a id="orgbee1f3e"></a>

## Psalms 44:13

And the daughters of Tyre with gifts, yea, all the rich among the people, shall entreat thy countenance.


<a id="orgde1dfda"></a>

## Psalms 44:14

All the glory of the king&rsquo;s daughter is within in golden borders,


<a id="org2cf9042"></a>

## Psalms 44:15

Clothed round about with varieties. After her shall virgins be brought to the king: her neighbours shall be brought to thee.


<a id="org7eb2d32"></a>

## Psalms 44:16

They shall be brought with gladness and rejoicing: they shall be brought into the temple of the king.


<a id="orga6e4bed"></a>

## Psalms 44:17

Instead of thy fathers, sons are born to thee: thou shalt make them princes over all the earth.


<a id="org8c53bdf"></a>

## Psalms 44:18

They shall remember thy name throughout all generations. Therefore shall people praise thee for ever; yea, for ever and ever. <chapter eID=&ldquo;gen15946&rdquo; osisID=&ldquo;Ps.44&rdquo;/>


<a id="orgfc8b64c"></a>

# Psalms 45


<a id="org82f1ed1"></a>

## Psalms 45:1

Unto the end, for the sons of Core, for the hidden.


<a id="org9b461c0"></a>

## Psalms 45:2

Our God is our refuge and strength: a helper in troubles, which have found us exceedingly.


<a id="org41c18d8"></a>

## Psalms 45:3

Therefore we will not fear, when the earth shall be troubled; and the mountains shall be removed into the heart of the sea.


<a id="org0e3c823"></a>

## Psalms 45:4

Their waters roared and were troubled: the mountains were troubled with his strength.


<a id="orgdc5b71c"></a>

## Psalms 45:5

The stream of the river maketh the city of God joyful: the most High hath sanctified his own tabernacle.


<a id="org0f73b5a"></a>

## Psalms 45:6

God is in the midst thereof, it shall not be moved: God will help it in the morning early.


<a id="orgf34e4e9"></a>

## Psalms 45:7

Nations were troubled, and kingdoms were bowed down: he uttered his voice, the earth trembled.


<a id="orgb64e99c"></a>

## Psalms 45:8

The Lord of armies is with us: the God of Jacob is our protector.


<a id="orgacca914"></a>

## Psalms 45:9

Come and behold ye the works of the Lord: what wonders he hath done upon earth,


<a id="orgf295b6f"></a>

## Psalms 45:10

Making wars to cease even to the end of the earth. He shall destroy the bow, and break the weapons: and the shield he shall burn in the fire.


<a id="orgc5d31cb"></a>

## Psalms 45:11

Be still and see that I am God; I will be exalted among the nations, and I will be exalted in the earth.


<a id="orgc540f1c"></a>

## Psalms 45:12

The Lord of armies is with us: the God of Jacob is our protector. <chapter eID=&ldquo;gen15965&rdquo; osisID=&ldquo;Ps.45&rdquo;/>


<a id="org869ef9a"></a>

# Psalms 46


<a id="orga73f21e"></a>

## Psalms 46:1

Unto the end, for the sons of Core.


<a id="orgb74bd3b"></a>

## Psalms 46:2

O clap your hands, all ye nations: shout unto God with the voice of joy,


<a id="org8550abc"></a>

## Psalms 46:3

For the Lord is high, terrible: a great king over all the earth.


<a id="org83441a0"></a>

## Psalms 46:4

He hath subdued the people under us; and the nations under our feet.


<a id="org455d3e8"></a>

## Psalms 46:5

He hath chosen for us his inheritance, the beauty of Jacob which he hath loved.


<a id="orga74d15f"></a>

## Psalms 46:6

God is ascended with jubilee, and the Lord with the sound of trumpet.


<a id="org77e1eef"></a>

## Psalms 46:7

Sing praises to our God, sing ye: sing praises to our king, sing ye.


<a id="orgb4f31f4"></a>

## Psalms 46:8

For God is the king of all the earth: sing ye wisely.


<a id="org24c7800"></a>

## Psalms 46:9

God shall reign over the nations: God sitteth on his holy throne.


<a id="org5a5b302"></a>

## Psalms 46:10

The princes of the people are gathered together, with the God of Abraham: for the strong gods of the earth are exceedingly exalted. <chapter eID=&ldquo;gen15978&rdquo; osisID=&ldquo;Ps.46&rdquo;/>


<a id="orgc692442"></a>

# Psalms 47


<a id="orga98c84d"></a>

## Psalms 47:1

A psalm of a canticle, for the sons of Core, on the second day of the week.


<a id="orgdf4f6f2"></a>

## Psalms 47:2

Great is the Lord, and exceedingly to be praised in the city of our God, in his holy mountain.


<a id="orgc2432e1"></a>

## Psalms 47:3

With the joy of the whole earth is mount Sion founded, on the sides of the north, the city of the great king.


<a id="orgca80049"></a>

## Psalms 47:4

In her houses shall God be known, when he shall protect her.


<a id="orgfee1927"></a>

## Psalms 47:5

For behold the kings of the earth assembled themselves: they gathered together.


<a id="org7f87442"></a>

## Psalms 47:6

So they saw, and they wondered, they were troubled, they were moved:


<a id="org659154d"></a>

## Psalms 47:7

Trembling took hold of them. There were pains as of a woman in labour.


<a id="org5cc418b"></a>

## Psalms 47:8

With a vehement wind thou shalt break in pieces the ships of Tharsis.


<a id="org8e2eafe"></a>

## Psalms 47:9

As we have heard, so have we seen, in the city of the Lord of hosts, in the city of our God: God hath founded it for ever.


<a id="org3d46334"></a>

## Psalms 47:10

We have received thy mercy, O God, in the midst of thy temple.


<a id="orgd81e2df"></a>

## Psalms 47:11

According to thy name, O God, so also is thy praise unto the ends of the earth: thy right hand is full of justice.


<a id="org93c7f5d"></a>

## Psalms 47:12

Let mount Sion rejoice, and the daughters of Juda be glad; because of thy judgments, O Lord.


<a id="org0216ac8"></a>

## Psalms 47:13

Surround Sion, and encompass her: tell ye in her towers.


<a id="org7eb65dd"></a>

## Psalms 47:14

Set your hearts on her strength; and distribute her houses, that ye may relate it in another generation.


<a id="org59b9051"></a>

## Psalms 47:15

For this is God, our God unto eternity, and for ever and ever: he shall rule us for evermore. <chapter eID=&ldquo;gen15989&rdquo; osisID=&ldquo;Ps.47&rdquo;/>


<a id="org82146da"></a>

# Psalms 48


<a id="org241e199"></a>

## Psalms 48:1

Unto the end, a psalm for the sons of Core.


<a id="org58c17bd"></a>

## Psalms 48:2

Hear these things, all ye nations: give ear, all ye inhabitants of the world.


<a id="orgb27d895"></a>

## Psalms 48:3

All you that are earthborn, and you sons of men: both rich and poor together.


<a id="orgfc32c1c"></a>

## Psalms 48:4

My mouth shall speak wisdom: and the meditation of my heart understanding.


<a id="org2b7e337"></a>

## Psalms 48:5

I will incline my ear to a parable; I will open my proposition on the psaltery.


<a id="org87f1c47"></a>

## Psalms 48:6

Why shall I fear in the evil day? the iniquity of my heel shall encompass me.


<a id="org842151c"></a>

## Psalms 48:7

They that trust in their own strength, and glory in the multitude of their riches,


<a id="orgec69c74"></a>

## Psalms 48:8

No brother can redeem, nor shall man redeem: he shall not give to God his ransom,


<a id="org1394a88"></a>

## Psalms 48:9

Nor the price of the redemption of his soul: and shall labour for ever,


<a id="org7390d39"></a>

## Psalms 48:10

And shall still live unto the end.


<a id="orge1db1d2"></a>

## Psalms 48:11

He shall not see destruction, when he shall see the wise dying: the senseless and the fool shall perish together: And they shall leave their riches to strangers:


<a id="orgfec5940"></a>

## Psalms 48:12

And their sepulchres shall be their houses for ever. Their dwelling places to all generations: they have called their lands by their names.


<a id="org14d6bb5"></a>

## Psalms 48:13

And man when he was in honour did not understand; he is compared to senseless beasts, and is become like to them.


<a id="org8aad127"></a>

## Psalms 48:14

This way of theirs is a stumblingblock to them: and afterwards they shall delight in their mouth.


<a id="orgd0d3840"></a>

## Psalms 48:15

They are laid in hell like sheep: death shall feed upon them. And the just shall have dominion over them in the morning; and their help shall decay in hell from their glory.


<a id="org7bc95c7"></a>

## Psalms 48:16

But God will redeem my soul from the hand of hell, when he shall receive me.


<a id="org787dcbd"></a>

## Psalms 48:17

Be not thou afraid, when a man shall be made rich, and when the glory of his house shall be increased.


<a id="orge600977"></a>

## Psalms 48:18

For when he shall die he shall take nothing away; nor shall his glory descend with him.


<a id="org53f9027"></a>

## Psalms 48:19

For in his lifetime his soul will be blessed: and he will praise thee when thou shalt do well to him.


<a id="orgf88248f"></a>

## Psalms 48:20

He shall go in to the generations of his fathers: and he shall never see light.


<a id="org58a2f74"></a>

## Psalms 48:21

Man when he was in honour did not understand: he hath been compared to senseless beasts, and made like to them. <chapter eID=&ldquo;gen16005&rdquo; osisID=&ldquo;Ps.48&rdquo;/>


<a id="org4b7a20a"></a>

# Psalms 49


<a id="org8d63588"></a>

## Psalms 49:1

A psalm for Asaph. The God of gods, the Lord hath spoken: and he hath called the earth. From the rising of the sun, to the going down thereof:


<a id="orgd34e58e"></a>

## Psalms 49:2

Out of Sion the loveliness of his beauty.


<a id="org1e3a4b9"></a>

## Psalms 49:3

God shall come manifestly: our God shall come, and shall not keep silence. A fire shall burn before him: and a mighty tempest shall be round about him.


<a id="orgddd41fe"></a>

## Psalms 49:4

He shall call heaven from above, and the earth, to judge his people.


<a id="org67a75bf"></a>

## Psalms 49:5

Gather ye together his saints to him: who set his covenant before sacrifices.


<a id="org48da39c"></a>

## Psalms 49:6

And the heavens shall declare his justice: for God is judge.


<a id="org61c76f3"></a>

## Psalms 49:7

Hear, O my people, and I will speak: O Israel, and I will testify to thee: I am God, thy God.


<a id="orgffb3377"></a>

## Psalms 49:8

I will not reprove thee for thy sacrifices: and thy burnt offerings are always in my sight.


<a id="org85123aa"></a>

## Psalms 49:9

I will not take calves out of thy house: nor he goats out of thy flocks.


<a id="org64dcbab"></a>

## Psalms 49:10

For all the beasts of the woods are mine: the cattle on the hills, and the oxen.


<a id="org8d85f7a"></a>

## Psalms 49:11

I know all the fowls of the air: and with me is the beauty of the field.


<a id="orga617c3a"></a>

## Psalms 49:12

If I should be hungry, I would not tell thee: for the world is mine, and the fulness thereof.


<a id="org57de01a"></a>

## Psalms 49:13

Shall I eat the flesh of bullocks? or shall I drink the blood of goats?


<a id="org05ecc78"></a>

## Psalms 49:14

Offer to God the sacrifice of praise: and pay thy vows to the most High.


<a id="orgb65a972"></a>

## Psalms 49:15

And call upon me in the day of trouble: I will deliver thee, and thou shalt glorify me.


<a id="org603bf4e"></a>

## Psalms 49:16

But to the sinner God hath said: Why dost thou declare my justices, and take my covenant in thy mouth?


<a id="orge47443b"></a>

## Psalms 49:17

Seeing thou hast hated discipline: and hast cast my words behind thee.


<a id="orgf706c5e"></a>

## Psalms 49:18

If thou didst see a thief thou didst run with him: and with adulterers thou hast been a partaker.


<a id="org1555cc3"></a>

## Psalms 49:19

Thy mouth hath abounded with evil, and thy tongue framed deceits.


<a id="org99da45a"></a>

## Psalms 49:20

Sitting thou didst speak against thy brother, and didst lay a scandal against thy mother&rsquo;s son:


<a id="orgcb610e2"></a>

## Psalms 49:21

These things hast thou done, and I was silent. Thou thoughtest unjustly that I should be like to thee: but I will reprove thee, and set before thy face.


<a id="org6cdb38b"></a>

## Psalms 49:22

Understand these things, you that forget God; lest he snatch you away, and there be none to deliver you.


<a id="orgb02cc1c"></a>

## Psalms 49:23

The sacrifice of praise shall glorify me: and there is the way by which I will shew him the salvation of God. <chapter eID=&ldquo;gen16027&rdquo; osisID=&ldquo;Ps.49&rdquo;/>


<a id="org50e1871"></a>

# Psalms 50


<a id="orgea68963"></a>

## Psalms 50:1

Unto the end, a psalm of David,


<a id="orgc184e4c"></a>

## Psalms 50:2

When Nathan the prophet came to him, after he had sinned with Bethsabee.


<a id="orga8b7c2a"></a>

## Psalms 50:3

Have mercy on me, O God, according to thy great mercy. And according to the multitude of thy tender mercies blot out my iniquity.


<a id="orga2a6a36"></a>

## Psalms 50:4

Wash me yet more from my iniquity, and cleanse me from my sin.


<a id="orgaa306ea"></a>

## Psalms 50:5

For I know my iniquity, and my sin is always before me.


<a id="org3f81f15"></a>

## Psalms 50:6

To thee only have I sinned, and have done evil before thee: that thou mayst be justified in thy words, and mayst overcome when thou art judged.


<a id="org39cb411"></a>

## Psalms 50:7

For behold I was conceived in iniquities; and in sins did my mother conceive me.


<a id="org4be7e72"></a>

## Psalms 50:8

For behold thou hast loved truth: the uncertain and hidden things of thy wisdom thou hast made manifest to me.


<a id="org2ab301e"></a>

## Psalms 50:9

Thou shalt sprinkle me with hyssop, and I shall be cleansed: thou shalt wash me, and I shall be made whiter than snow.


<a id="org2a598ca"></a>

## Psalms 50:10

To my hearing thou shalt give joy and gladness: and the bones that have been humbled shall rejoice.


<a id="org5c0d1cb"></a>

## Psalms 50:11

Turn away thy face from my sins, and blot out all my iniquities.


<a id="org67b7468"></a>

## Psalms 50:12

Create a clean heart in me, O God: and renew a right spirit within my bowels.


<a id="orgcf81321"></a>

## Psalms 50:13

Cast me not away from thy face; and take not thy holy spirit from me.


<a id="org9b08c25"></a>

## Psalms 50:14

Restore unto me the joy of thy salvation, and strengthen me with a perfect spirit.


<a id="org55b59f7"></a>

## Psalms 50:15

I will teach the unjust thy ways: and the wicked shall be converted to thee.


<a id="orgeac64a5"></a>

## Psalms 50:16

Deliver me from blood, O God, thou God of my salvation: and my tongue shall extol thy justice.


<a id="org0af1347"></a>

## Psalms 50:17

O Lord, thou wilt open my lips: and my mouth shall declare thy praise.


<a id="org3cea0b1"></a>

## Psalms 50:18

For if thou hadst desired sacrifice, I would indeed have given it: with burnt offerings thou wilt not be delighted.


<a id="orgdedbd1e"></a>

## Psalms 50:19

A sacrifice to God is an afflicted spirit: a contrite and humbled heart, O God, thou wilt not despise.


<a id="orge3a8d99"></a>

## Psalms 50:20

Deal favourably, O Lord, in thy good will with Sion; that the walls of Jerusalem may be built up.


<a id="orgd5ad00c"></a>

## Psalms 50:21

Then shalt thou accept the sacrifice of justice, oblations and whole burnt offerings: then shall they lay calves upon thy altar. <chapter eID=&ldquo;gen16051&rdquo; osisID=&ldquo;Ps.50&rdquo;/>


<a id="org7f450a9"></a>

# Psalms 51


<a id="org9240e7e"></a>

## Psalms 51:1

Unto the end, understanding for David,


<a id="org882d433"></a>

## Psalms 51:2

When Doeg the Edomite came and told Saul: David went to the house of Achimelech.


<a id="orgbf228b0"></a>

## Psalms 51:3

Why dost thou glory in malice, thou that art mighty in iniquity?


<a id="orgcc1e764"></a>

## Psalms 51:4

All the day long thy tongue hath devised injustice: as a sharp razor, thou hast wrought deceit.


<a id="org4c93ad4"></a>

## Psalms 51:5

Thou hast loved malice more than goodness: and iniquity rather than to speak righteousness.


<a id="orgcc74bc1"></a>

## Psalms 51:6

Thou hast loved all the words of ruin, O deceitful tongue.


<a id="org2d74edf"></a>

## Psalms 51:7

Therefore will God destroy thee for ever: he will pluck thee out, and remove thee from thy dwelling place: and thy root out of the land of the living.


<a id="org34a0124"></a>

## Psalms 51:8

The just shall see and fear, and shall laugh at him, and say:


<a id="orgbdd5102"></a>

## Psalms 51:9

Behold the man that made not God his helper: But trusted in the abundance of his riches: and prevailed in his vanity.


<a id="org2065b20"></a>

## Psalms 51:10

But I, as a fruitful olive tree in the house of God, have hoped in the mercy of God for ever, yea for ever and ever.


<a id="org58a8c3f"></a>

## Psalms 51:11

I will praise thee for ever, because thou hast done it: and I will wait on thy name, for it is good in the sight of thy saints. <chapter eID=&ldquo;gen16073&rdquo; osisID=&ldquo;Ps.51&rdquo;/>


<a id="orga0a2543"></a>

# Psalms 52


<a id="orgfaf4bf6"></a>

## Psalms 52:1

Unto the end, for Maeleth, understandings to David. The fool said in his heart: There is no God.


<a id="orga51bc96"></a>

## Psalms 52:2

They are corrupted, and become abominable in iniquities: there is none that doth good.


<a id="org811e1a7"></a>

## Psalms 52:3

God looked down from heaven on the children of men: to see if there were any that did understand, or did seek God.


<a id="org69b8ab3"></a>

## Psalms 52:4

All have gone aside, they are become unprofitable together, there is none that doth good, no not one.


<a id="orgce7e5b9"></a>

## Psalms 52:5

Shall not all the workers of iniquity know, who eat up my people as they eat bread?


<a id="org7a066a9"></a>

## Psalms 52:6

They have not called upon God: there have they trembled for fear, where there was no fear. For God hath scattered the bones of them that please men: they have been confounded, because God hath despised them.


<a id="orgf687bf9"></a>

## Psalms 52:7

Who will give out of Sion the salvation of Israel? when God shall bring back the captivity of his people, Jacob shall rejoice, and Israel shall be glad. <chapter eID=&ldquo;gen16085&rdquo; osisID=&ldquo;Ps.52&rdquo;/>

# Psalms 53


<a id="org44cc0b9"></a>

## Psalms 53:1

Unto the end, in verses, understanding for David.


<a id="org032de2e"></a>

## Psalms 53:2

When the men of Ziph had come and said to Saul: Is not David hidden with us?


<a id="orga670ebe"></a>

## Psalms 53:3

Save me, O God, by thy name, and judge me in thy strength.


<a id="orga9c837e"></a>

## Psalms 53:4

O God, hear my prayer: give ear to the words of my mouth.


<a id="org8f108ff"></a>

## Psalms 53:5

For strangers have risen up against me; and the mighty have sought after my soul: and they have not set God before their eyes.


<a id="org773fd78"></a>

## Psalms 53:6

For behold God is my helper: and the Lord is the protector of my soul.


<a id="org55d5582"></a>

## Psalms 53:7

Turn back the evils upon my enemies; and cut them off in thy truth.


<a id="org5619d5f"></a>

## Psalms 53:8

I will freely sacrifice to thee, and will give praise, O God, to thy name: because it is good:


<a id="org8234a8c"></a>

## Psalms 53:9

For thou hast delivered me out of all trouble: and my eye hath looked down upon my enemies. 


<a id="org0738af7"></a>

# Psalms 54


<a id="orgdccbce5"></a>

## Psalms 54:1

Unto the end, in verses, understanding for David.


<a id="org12b96bd"></a>

## Psalms 54:2

Hear, O God, my prayer, and despise not my supplication:


<a id="org358d625"></a>

## Psalms 54:3

Be attentive to me and hear me. I am grieved in my exercise; and am troubled,


<a id="orgfda9a25"></a>

## Psalms 54:4

At the voice of the enemy, and at the tribulation of the sinner. For they have cast iniquities upon me: and in wrath they were troublesome to me.


<a id="org5298991"></a>

## Psalms 54:5

My heart is troubled within me: and the fear of death is fallen upon me.


<a id="org0a0941f"></a>

## Psalms 54:6

Fear and trembling are come upon me: and darkness hath covered me.


<a id="org30d09eb"></a>

## Psalms 54:7

And I said: Who will give me wings like a dove, and I will fly and be at rest?


<a id="orgc077a51"></a>

## Psalms 54:8

Lo, I have gone far off flying away; and I abode in the wilderness.


<a id="orgf05f366"></a>

## Psalms 54:9

I waited for him that hath saved me from pusillanimity of spirit, and a storm.


<a id="org9121c3f"></a>

## Psalms 54:10

Cast down, O Lord, and divide their tongues; for I have seen iniquity and contradiction in the city.


<a id="org739f075"></a>

## Psalms 54:11

Day and night shall iniquity surround it upon its walls: and in the midst thereof are labour,


<a id="orge7975a4"></a>

## Psalms 54:12

And injustice. And usury and deceit have not departed from its streets.


<a id="org7833eee"></a>

## Psalms 54:13

For if my enemy had reviled me, I would verily have borne with it. And if he that hated me had spoken great things against me, I would perhaps have hidden my self from him.


<a id="org1a82cc1"></a>

## Psalms 54:14

But thou a man of one mind, my guide, and my familiar,


<a id="org6ebed91"></a>

## Psalms 54:15

Who didst take sweetmeats together with me: in the house of God we walked with consent.


<a id="org9fee244"></a>

## Psalms 54:16

Let death come upon them, and let them go down alive into hell. For there is wickedness in their dwellings: in the midst of them.


<a id="orgfe6d532"></a>

## Psalms 54:17

But I have cried to God: and the Lord will save me.


<a id="org73271e0"></a>

## Psalms 54:18

Evening and morning, and at noon I will speak and declare: and he shall hear my voice.


<a id="orgde26434"></a>

## Psalms 54:19

He shall redeem my soul in peace from them that draw near to me: for among many they were with me.


<a id="org926fad0"></a>

## Psalms 54:20

God shall hear, and the Eternal shall humble them. For there is no change with them, and they have not feared God:


<a id="org2d719ab"></a>

## Psalms 54:21

He hath stretched forth his hand to repay. They have defiled his covenant,


<a id="org265bd81"></a>

## Psalms 54:22

They are divided by the wrath of his countenance, and his heart hath drawn near. His words are smoother than oil, and the same are darts.


<a id="orge5503e6"></a>

## Psalms 54:23

Cast thy care upon the Lord, and he shall sustain thee: he shall not suffer the just to waver for ever.


<a id="orga26346b"></a>

## Psalms 54:24

But thou, O God, shalt bring them down into the pit of destruction. Bloody and deceitful men shall not live out half their days; but I will trust in thee, O Lord. 


<a id="org8ad8b34"></a>

# Psalms 55


<a id="org8a867d8"></a>

## Psalms 55:1

Unto the end, for a people that is removed at a distance from the sanctuary: for David, for an inscription of a title (or pillar) when the Philistines held him in Geth.


<a id="org3fc8b58"></a>

## Psalms 55:2

Have mercy on me, O God, for man hath trodden me under foot; all the day long he hath afflicted me fighting against me.


<a id="org171a908"></a>

## Psalms 55:3

My enemies have trodden on me all the day long; for they are many that make war against me.


<a id="org92f5df4"></a>

## Psalms 55:4

From the height of the day I shall fear: but I will trust in thee.


<a id="orgc6c53ab"></a>

## Psalms 55:5

In God I will praise my words, in God I have put my trust: I will not fear what flesh can do against me.


<a id="org97e2058"></a>

## Psalms 55:6

All the day long they detested my words: all their thoughts were against me unto evil.


<a id="org9340457"></a>

## Psalms 55:7

They will dwell and hide themselves: they will watch my heel. As they have waited for my soul,


<a id="org5198fd6"></a>

## Psalms 55:8

For nothing shalt thou save them: in thy anger thou shalt break the people in pieces. O God,


<a id="orgae904b2"></a>

## Psalms 55:9

I have declared to thee my life: thou hast set me tears in thy sight, As also in thy promise.


<a id="org6891f34"></a>

## Psalms 55:10

Then shall my enemies be turned back. In what day soever I shall call upon thee, behold I know thou art my God.


<a id="org36e742f"></a>

## Psalms 55:11

In God will I praise the word, in the Lord will I praise his speech. In God have I hoped, I will not fear what man can do to me.


<a id="orgf44c50d"></a>

## Psalms 55:12

In me, O God, are vows to thee, which I will pay, praises to thee:


<a id="org81a15db"></a>

## Psalms 55:13

Because thou hast delivered my soul from death, my feet from falling: that I may please in the sight of God, in the light of the living. 


<a id="orgd2eae7b"></a>

# Psalms 56


<a id="org0347059"></a>

## Psalms 56:1

Unto the end, destroy not, for David, for an inscription of a title, when he fled from Saul into the cave.


<a id="orgce01e72"></a>

## Psalms 56:2

Have mercy on me, O God, have mercy on me: for my soul trusteth in thee. And in the shadow of thy wings will I hope, until iniquity pass away.


<a id="orgb980522"></a>

## Psalms 56:3

I will cry to God the most high; to God who hath done good to me.


<a id="org765b5d4"></a>

## Psalms 56:4

He hath sent from heaven and delivered me: he hath made them a reproach that trod upon me. God hath sent his mercy and his truth,


<a id="org8d80aaf"></a>

## Psalms 56:5

And he hath delivered my soul from the midst of the young lions. I slept troubled. The sons of men, whose teeth are weapons and arrows, and their tongue a sharp sword.


<a id="org8e377b1"></a>

## Psalms 56:6

Be thou exalted, O God, above the heavens, and thy glory above all the earth.


<a id="orgd2f141b"></a>

## Psalms 56:7

They prepared a snare for my feet; and they bowed down my soul. They dug a pit before my face, and they are fallen into it.


<a id="org9c24e50"></a>

## Psalms 56:8

My heart is ready, O God, my heart is ready: I will sing, and rehearse a psalm.


<a id="orgfdf5d3e"></a>

## Psalms 56:9

Arise, O my glory, arise psaltery and harp: I will arise early.


<a id="org8616d68"></a>

## Psalms 56:10

I will give praise to thee, O Lord, among the people: I will sing a psalm to thee among the nations.


<a id="org6ed6139"></a>

## Psalms 56:11

For thy mercy is magnified even to the heavens: and thy truth unto the clouds.


<a id="orgfe2ebc7"></a>

## Psalms 56:12

Be thou exalted, O God, above the heavens: and thy glory above all the earth. 


<a id="org7765ea0"></a>

# Psalms 57


<a id="org24f0f61"></a>

## Psalms 57:1

Unto the end, destroy not, for David, for an inscription of a title.


<a id="org0f8b585"></a>

## Psalms 57:2

If in very deed ye speak justice: judge right things, ye sons of men.


<a id="org1b5915c"></a>

## Psalms 57:3

For in your heart you work iniquity: your hands forge injustice in the earth.


<a id="org3679296"></a>

## Psalms 57:4

The wicked are alienated from the womb; they have gone astray from the womb: they have spoken false things.


<a id="orgad892b9"></a>

## Psalms 57:5

Their madness is according to the likeness of a serpent: like the deaf asp that stoppeth her ears:


<a id="orgbd926ea"></a>

## Psalms 57:6

Which will not hear the voice of the charmers; nor of the wizard that charmeth wisely.


<a id="orgea550c7"></a>

## Psalms 57:7

God shall break in pieces their teeth in their mouth: the Lord shall break the grinders of the lions.


<a id="org854b39c"></a>

## Psalms 57:8

They shall come to nothing, like water running down; he hath bent his bow till they be weakened.


<a id="orgcece79d"></a>

## Psalms 57:9

Like wax that melteth they shall be taken away: fire hath fallen on them, and they shall not see the sun.


<a id="orgd047cf6"></a>

## Psalms 57:10

Before your thorns could know the brier; he swalloweth them up, as alive, in his wrath.


<a id="orgb2a644f"></a>

## Psalms 57:11

The just shall rejoice when he shall see the revenge: he shall wash his hands in the blood of the sinner.


<a id="org1b2966b"></a>

## Psalms 57:12

And man shall say: If indeed there be fruit to the just: there is indeed a God that judgeth them on the earth. 


<a id="org8288d30"></a>

# Psalms 58


<a id="orgfe0ddd7"></a>

## Psalms 58:1

Unto the end, destroy not, for David for an inscription of a title, when Saul sent and watched his house to kill him.


<a id="org223ecdd"></a>

## Psalms 58:2

Deliver me from my enemies, O my God; and defend me from them that rise up against me.


<a id="org79afc72"></a>

## Psalms 58:3

Deliver me from them that work iniquity, and save me from bloody men.


<a id="org7a656fa"></a>

## Psalms 58:4

For behold they have caught my soul: the mighty have rushed in upon me:


<a id="orge0e3d3e"></a>

## Psalms 58:5

Neither is it my iniquity, nor my sin, O Lord: without iniquity have I run, and directed my steps.


<a id="org55dfb26"></a>

## Psalms 58:6

Rise up thou to meet me, and behold: even thou, O Lord, the God of hosts, the God of Israel. Attend to visit all the nations: have no mercy on all them that work iniquity.


<a id="org0f51301"></a>

## Psalms 58:7

They shall return at evening, and shall suffer hunger like dogs: and shall go round about the city.


<a id="org9d57d28"></a>

## Psalms 58:8

Behold they shall speak with their mouth, and a sword is in their lips: for who, say they, hath heard us?


<a id="orgbd9cd4f"></a>

## Psalms 58:9

But thou, O Lord, shalt laugh at them: thou shalt bring all the nations to nothing.


<a id="orga4fcab0"></a>

## Psalms 58:10

I will keep my strength to thee: for thou art my protector:


<a id="orgfbb0603"></a>

## Psalms 58:11

My God, his mercy shall prevent me.


<a id="org66b706c"></a>

## Psalms 58:12

God shall let me see over my enemies: slay them not, lest at any time my people forget. Scatter them by thy power; and bring them down, O Lord, my protector:


<a id="orga684a9a"></a>

## Psalms 58:13

For the sin of their mouth, and the word of their lips: and let them be taken in their pride. And for their cursing and lying they shall be talked of,


<a id="org4eb36d6"></a>

## Psalms 58:14

When they are consumed: when they are consumed by thy wrath, and they shall be no more. And they shall know that God will rule Jacob, and all the ends of the earth.


<a id="orgc1f947b"></a>

## Psalms 58:15

They shall return at evening and shall suffer hunger like dogs: and shall go round about the city.


<a id="orgee05afe"></a>

## Psalms 58:16

They shall be scattered abroad to eat, and shall murmur if they be not filled.


<a id="org3b8c9d5"></a>

## Psalms 58:17

But I will sing thy strength: and will extol thy mercy in the morning. For thou art become my support, and my refuge, in the day of my trouble.


<a id="orgdaba1af"></a>

## Psalms 58:18

Unto thee, O my helper, will I sing, for thou art God my defence: my God my mercy. 


<a id="org18ddaff"></a>

# Psalms 59


<a id="org9cf3d15"></a>

## Psalms 59:1

Unto the end, for them that shall be changed, for the inscription of a title, to David himself, for doctrine,


<a id="orgf9c9edc"></a>

## Psalms 59:2

When he set fire to Mesopotamia of Syria and Sobal: and Joab returned and slew of Edom, in the vale of the saltpits, twelve thousand men.


<a id="org1c2d9c2"></a>

## Psalms 59:3

O God, thou hast cast us off, and hast destroyed us; thou hast been angry, and hast had mercy on us.


<a id="orgfed2909"></a>

## Psalms 59:4

Thou hast moved the earth, and hast troubled it: heal thou the breaches thereof, for it has been moved.


<a id="org1eb9e20"></a>

## Psalms 59:5

Thou hast shewn thy people hard things; thou hast made us drink the wine of sorrow.


<a id="org7bd2e77"></a>

## Psalms 59:6

Thou hast given a warning to them that fear thee: that they may flee from before the bow: That thy beloved may be delivered.


<a id="org9860020"></a>

## Psalms 59:7

Save me with thy right hand, and hear me.


<a id="org9d8eb5c"></a>

## Psalms 59:8

God hath spoken in his holy place: I will rejoice, and I will divide Sichem; and will mete out the vale of tabernacles.


<a id="org0cffe81"></a>

## Psalms 59:9

Galaad is mine, and Manasses is mine: and Ephraim is the strength of my head. Juda is my king:


<a id="orgb368501"></a>

## Psalms 59:10

Moab is the pot of my hope. Into Edom will I stretch out my shoe: to me the foreigners are made subject.


<a id="orgcd6ead2"></a>

## Psalms 59:11

Who will bring me into the strong city? who will lead me into Edom?


<a id="orgcb2eec5"></a>

## Psalms 59:12

Wilt not thou, O God, who hast cast us off? and wilt not thou, O God, go out with our armies?


<a id="orge403182"></a>

## Psalms 59:13

Give us help from trouble: for vain is the salvation of man.


<a id="org1bbdbcf"></a>

## Psalms 59:14

Through God we shall do mightily: and he shall bring to nothing them that afflict us. 


<a id="org587be5b"></a>

# Psalms 60


<a id="org2b3ae26"></a>

## Psalms 60:1

Unto the end, in hymns, for David.


<a id="org93c336e"></a>

## Psalms 60:2

Hear, O God, my supplication: be attentive to my prayer.


<a id="orgbee065a"></a>

## Psalms 60:3

To thee have I cried from the ends of the earth: when my heart was in anguish, thou hast exalted me on a rock. Thou hast conducted me;


<a id="org17fa8b5"></a>

## Psalms 60:4

For thou hast been my hope; a tower of strength against the face of the enemy.


<a id="orgf72fd4a"></a>

## Psalms 60:5

In thy tabernacle I shall dwell for ever: I shall be protected under the covert of thy wings.


<a id="orgf9af786"></a>

## Psalms 60:6

For thou, my God, hast heard my prayer: thou hast given an inheritance to them that fear thy name.


<a id="orgf97e245"></a>

## Psalms 60:7

Thou wilt add days to the days of the king: his years even to generation and generation.


<a id="orge8107a5"></a>

## Psalms 60:8

He abideth for ever in the sight of God: his mercy and truth who shall search?


<a id="orgb5a8412"></a>

## Psalms 60:9

So will I sing a psalm to thy name for ever and ever: that I may pay my vows from day to day. 


<a id="org0011da6"></a>

# Psalms 61


<a id="orgba24eb5"></a>

## Psalms 61:1

Unto the end, for Idithun, a psalm of David.


<a id="orgb067a14"></a>

## Psalms 61:2

Shall not my soul be subject to God? for from him is my salvation.


<a id="org7463ae7"></a>

## Psalms 61:3

For he is my God and my saviour: he is my protector, I shall be moved no more.


<a id="org5e8d497"></a>

## Psalms 61:4

How long do you rush in upon a man? you all kill, as if you were thrusting down a leaning wall, and a tottering fence.


<a id="orgf79b46a"></a>

## Psalms 61:5

But they have thought to cast away my price; I ran in thirst: they blessed with their mouth, but cursed with their heart.


<a id="orgb643517"></a>

## Psalms 61:6

But be thou, O my soul, subject to God: for from him is my patience.


<a id="orgad14451"></a>

## Psalms 61:7

For he is my God and my saviour: he is my helper, I shall not be moved.


<a id="orgad5f6f0"></a>

## Psalms 61:8

In God is my salvation and my glory: he is the God of my help, and my hope is in God.


<a id="org7231126"></a>

## Psalms 61:9

Trust in him, all ye congregation of people: pour out your hearts before him. God is our helper for ever.


<a id="org207d2bb"></a>

## Psalms 61:10

But vain are the sons of men, the sons of men are liars in the balances: that by vanity they may together deceive.


<a id="orgdc07c69"></a>

## Psalms 61:11

Trust not in iniquity, and covet not robberies: if riches abound, set not your heart upon them.


<a id="orgcfc4563"></a>

## Psalms 61:12

God hath spoken once, these two things have I heard, that power belongeth to God,


<a id="org697e9a1"></a>

## Psalms 61:13

And mercy to thee, O Lord; for thou wilt render to every man according to his works. 


<a id="org6a1dd6d"></a>

# Psalms 62


<a id="org11fa625"></a>

## Psalms 62:1

A psalm of David while he was in the desert of Edom.


<a id="org17ba3cb"></a>

## Psalms 62:2

O God, my God, to thee do I watch at break of day. For thee my soul hath thirsted; for thee my flesh, O how many ways!


<a id="org1b3080e"></a>

## Psalms 62:3

In a desert land, and where there is no way, and no water: so in the sanctuary have I come before thee, to see thy power and thy glory.


<a id="orgbd59412"></a>

## Psalms 62:4

For thy mercy is better than lives: thee my lips will praise.


<a id="orgc978e27"></a>

## Psalms 62:5

Thus will I bless thee all my life long: and in thy name I will lift up my hands.


<a id="orge90060e"></a>

## Psalms 62:6

Let my soul be filled as with marrow and fatness: and my mouth shall praise thee with joyful lips.


<a id="org571ea5d"></a>

## Psalms 62:7

If I have remembered thee upon my bed, I will meditate on thee in the morning:


<a id="org85608d6"></a>

## Psalms 62:8

Because thou hast been my helper. And I will rejoice under the cover of thy wings:


<a id="org8f41dcc"></a>

## Psalms 62:9

My soul hath stuck close to thee: thy right hand hath received me.


<a id="orgfeaa55e"></a>

## Psalms 62:10

But they have sought my soul in vain, they shall go into the lower parts of the earth:


<a id="orgd737566"></a>

## Psalms 62:11

They shall be delivered into the hands of the sword, they shall be the portions of foxes.


<a id="org4e02dd7"></a>

## Psalms 62:12

But the king shall rejoice in God, all they shall be praised that swear by him: because the mouth is stopped of them that speak wicked things. 


<a id="orgbf7325d"></a>

# Psalms 63


<a id="org94c9f2f"></a>

## Psalms 63:1

Unto the end, a psalm for David.


<a id="org33a90b5"></a>

## Psalms 63:2

Hear O God, my prayer, when I make supplication to thee: deliver my soul from the fear of the enemy.


<a id="org27c8ba0"></a>

## Psalms 63:3

Thou hast protected me from the assembly of the malignant; from the multitude of the workers of iniquity.


<a id="org7c32253"></a>

## Psalms 63:4

For they have whetted their tongues like a sword; they have bent their bow a bitter thing,


<a id="orga61924a"></a>

## Psalms 63:5

To shoot in secret the undefiled.


<a id="org62ca204"></a>

## Psalms 63:6

They will shoot at him on a sudden, and will not fear: they are resolute in wickedness. They have talked of hiding snares; they have said: Who shall see them?


<a id="org523f94f"></a>

## Psalms 63:7

They have searched after iniquities: they have failed in their search. Man shall come to a deep heart:


<a id="org6215217"></a>

## Psalms 63:8

And God shall be exalted. The arrows of children are their wounds:


<a id="org07832e3"></a>

## Psalms 63:9

And their tongues against them are made weak. All that saw them were troubled;


<a id="org3657249"></a>

## Psalms 63:10

And every man was afraid. And they declared the works of God, and understood his doings.


<a id="org293dacc"></a>

## Psalms 63:11

The just shall rejoice in the Lord, and shall hope in him: and all the upright in heart shall be praised. 


<a id="org3eff127"></a>

# Psalms 64


<a id="org129df11"></a>

## Psalms 64:1

To the end, a psalm of David. The canticle of Jeremias and Ezechiel to the people of the captivity, when they began to go out.


<a id="orgf4e425a"></a>

## Psalms 64:2

A hymn, O God, becometh thee in Sion: and a vow shall be paid to thee in Jerusalem.


<a id="orgef71dba"></a>

## Psalms 64:3

O hear my prayer: all flesh shall come to thee.


<a id="orge94271c"></a>

## Psalms 64:4

The words of the wicked have prevailed over us: and thou wilt pardon our transgressions.


<a id="org8954712"></a>

## Psalms 64:5

Blessed is he whom thou hast chosen and taken to thee: he shall dwell in thy courts. We shall be filled with the good things of thy house; holy is thy temple,


<a id="orgbdb3cdd"></a>

## Psalms 64:6

Wonderful in justice. Hear us, O God our saviour, who art the hope of all the ends of the earth, and in the sea afar off.


<a id="org7a8e8a9"></a>

## Psalms 64:7

Thou who preparest the mountains by thy strength, being girded with power:


<a id="org491d039"></a>

## Psalms 64:8

Who troublest the depth of the sea, the noise of its waves. The Gentiles shall be troubled,


<a id="org17eeba7"></a>

## Psalms 64:9

And they that dwell in the uttermost borders shall be afraid at thy signs: thou shalt make the outgoings of the morning and of the evening to be joyful.


<a id="org8ee4704"></a>

## Psalms 64:10

Thou hast visited the earth, and hast plentifully watered it; thou hast many ways enriched it. The river of God is filled with water, thou hast prepared their food: for so is its preparation.


<a id="org45e12ff"></a>

## Psalms 64:11

Fill up plentifully the streams thereof, multiply its fruits; it shall spring up and rejoice in its showers.


<a id="org049a851"></a>

## Psalms 64:12

Thou shalt bless the crown of the year of thy goodness: and thy fields shall be filled with plenty.


<a id="org0324775"></a>

## Psalms 64:13

The beautiful places of the wilderness shall grow fat: and the hills shall be girded about with joy,


<a id="orgcfc3c3e"></a>

## Psalms 64:14

The rams of the flock are clothed, and the vales shall abound with corn: they shall shout, yea they shall sing a hymn. 


<a id="org380922c"></a>

# Psalms 65


<a id="org0755480"></a>

## Psalms 65:1

Unto the end, a canticle of a psalm of the resurrection. Shout with joy to God, all the earth,


<a id="org86d9c8c"></a>

## Psalms 65:2

Sing ye a psalm to his name; give glory to his praise.


<a id="org97449b3"></a>

## Psalms 65:3

Say unto God, How terrible are thy works, O Lord! in the multitude of thy strength thy enemies shall lie to thee.


<a id="orgd311e98"></a>

## Psalms 65:4

Let all the earth adore thee, and sing to thee: let it sing a psalm to thy name.


<a id="org40f3ab8"></a>

## Psalms 65:5

Come and see the works of God; who is terrible in his counsels over the sons of men.


<a id="orgf567f38"></a>

## Psalms 65:6

Who turneth the sea into dry land, in the river they shall pass on foot: there shall we rejoice in him.


<a id="org4f93b37"></a>

## Psalms 65:7

Who by his power ruleth for ever: his eyes behold the nations; let not them that provoke him be exalted in themselves.


<a id="orga6a5351"></a>

## Psalms 65:8

O bless our God, ye Gentiles: and make the voice of his praise to be heard.


<a id="org6a60a10"></a>

## Psalms 65:9

Who hath set my soul to live: and hath not suffered my feet to be moved:


<a id="orgf1d54c2"></a>

## Psalms 65:10

For thou, O God, hast proved us: thou hast tried us by fire, as silver is tried.


<a id="org95e7d5c"></a>

## Psalms 65:11

Thou hast brought us into a net, thou hast laid afflictions on our back:


<a id="orga42be76"></a>

## Psalms 65:12

Thou hast set men over our heads. We have passed through fire and water, and thou hast brought us out into a refreshment.


<a id="orge93a7c8"></a>

## Psalms 65:13

I will go into thy house with burnt offerings: I will pay thee my vows,


<a id="orgfa255b6"></a>

## Psalms 65:14

Which my lips have uttered, And my mouth hath spoken, when I was in trouble.


<a id="org95621b1"></a>

## Psalms 65:15

I will offer up to thee holocausts full of marrow, with burnt offerings of rams: I will offer to thee bullocks with goats.


<a id="orga1beca8"></a>

## Psalms 65:16

Come and hear, all ye that fear God, and I will tell you what great things he hath done for my soul.


<a id="org5f16427"></a>

## Psalms 65:17

I cried to him with my mouth: and I extolled him with my tongue.


<a id="org1d2485e"></a>

## Psalms 65:18

If I have looked at iniquity in my heart, the Lord will not hear me.


<a id="orgd65a94b"></a>

## Psalms 65:19

Therefore hath God heard me, and hath attended to the voice of my supplication.


<a id="org5745690"></a>

## Psalms 65:20

Blessed be God, who hath not turned away my prayer, nor his mercy from me. 


<a id="org9a60e2a"></a>

# Psalms 66


<a id="org688d206"></a>

## Psalms 66:1

Unto the end, in hymns, a psalm of a canticle for David.


<a id="org39bbcb9"></a>

## Psalms 66:2

May God have mercy on us, and bless us: may he cause the light of his countenance to shine upon us, and may he have mercy on us.


<a id="org161b884"></a>

## Psalms 66:3

That we may know thy way upon earth: thy salvation in all nations.


<a id="orgdd95505"></a>

## Psalms 66:4

Let people confess to thee, O God: let all people give praise to thee.


<a id="org77f389e"></a>

## Psalms 66:5

Let the nations be glad and rejoice: for thou judgest the people with justice, and directest the nations upon earth.


<a id="orgb7d65f2"></a>

## Psalms 66:6

Let the people, O God, confess to thee: let all the people give praise to thee:


<a id="org5ad4c67"></a>

## Psalms 66:7

The earth hath yielded her fruit. May God, our God bless us,


<a id="orgabc2b10"></a>

## Psalms 66:8

May God bless us: and all the ends of the earth fear him. 


<a id="org12e9c9e"></a>

# Psalms 67


<a id="orgcf5f952"></a>

## Psalms 67:1

Unto the end, a psalm of a canticle for David himself.


<a id="orgd7df0f0"></a>

## Psalms 67:2

Let God arise, and let his enemies be scattered: and let them that hate him flee from before his face.


<a id="org65d355b"></a>

## Psalms 67:3

As smoke vanisheth, so let them vanish away: as wax melteth before the fire, so let the wicked perish at the presence of God.


<a id="orge787a23"></a>

## Psalms 67:4

And let the just feast, and rejoice before God: and be delighted with gladness.


<a id="orgee93ed7"></a>

## Psalms 67:5

Sing ye to God, sing a psalm to his name, make a way for him who ascendeth upon the west: the Lord is his name. Rejoice ye before him: but the wicked shall be troubled at his presence,


<a id="orgc8127f1"></a>

## Psalms 67:6

Who is the father of orphans, and the judge of widows. God in his holy place:


<a id="orgbf5adfd"></a>

## Psalms 67:7

God who maketh men of one manner to dwell in a house: Who bringeth out them that were bound in strength; in like manner them that provoke, that dwell in sepulchres.


<a id="orgfa3b4b1"></a>

## Psalms 67:8

O God, when thou didst go forth in the sight of thy people, when thou didst pass through the desert:


<a id="org97bf06c"></a>

## Psalms 67:9

The earth was moved, and the heavens dropped at the presence of the God of Sina, at the presence of the God of Israel.


<a id="orgce4e8e6"></a>

## Psalms 67:10

Thou shalt set aside for thy inheritance a free rain, O God: and it was weakened, but thou hast made it perfect.


<a id="orgb29f079"></a>

## Psalms 67:11

In it shall thy animals dwell; in thy sweetness, O God, thou hast provided for the poor.


<a id="orgb1fbb9a"></a>

## Psalms 67:12

The Lord shall give the word to them that preach good tidings with great power.


<a id="org0340fac"></a>

## Psalms 67:13

The king of powers is of the beloved, of the beloved; and the beauty of the house shall divide spoils.


<a id="org24349b7"></a>

## Psalms 67:14

If you sleep among the midst of lots, you shall be as the wings of a dove covered with silver, and the hinder parts of her back with the paleness of gold.


<a id="orgf413ee8"></a>

## Psalms 67:15

When he that is in heaven appointeth kings over her, they shall be whited with snow in Selmon.


<a id="orgc2abe5d"></a>

## Psalms 67:16

The mountain of God is a fat mountain. A curdled mountain, a fat mountain.


<a id="org185f95d"></a>

## Psalms 67:17

Why suspect, ye curdled mountains? A mountain in which God is well pleased to dwell: for there the Lord shall dwell unto the end.


<a id="org48ead67"></a>

## Psalms 67:18

The chariot of God is attended by ten thousands; thousands of them that rejoice: the Lord is among them in Sina, in the holy place.


<a id="org6ec45c4"></a>

## Psalms 67:19

Thou hast ascended on high, thou hast led captivity captive; thou hast received gifts in men. Yea for those also that do not believe, the dwelling of the Lord God.


<a id="org130b820"></a>

## Psalms 67:20

Blessed be the Lord day by day: the God of our salvation will make our journey prosperous to us.


<a id="orged3fcf0"></a>

## Psalms 67:21

Our God is the God of salvation: and of the Lord, of the Lord are the issues from death.


<a id="orgceaa01a"></a>

## Psalms 67:22

But God shall break the heads of his enemies: the hairy crown of them that walk on in their sins.


<a id="org78a20c9"></a>

## Psalms 67:23

The Lord said: I will turn them from Basan, I will turn them into the depth of the sea:


<a id="orgaf31bb0"></a>

## Psalms 67:24

That thy foot may be dipped in the blood of thy enemies; the tongue of thy dogs be red with the same.


<a id="org74a6051"></a>

## Psalms 67:25

They have seen thy goings, O God, the goings of my God: of my king who is in his sanctuary.


<a id="org8a256e2"></a>

## Psalms 67:26

Princes went before joined with singers, in the midst of young damsels playing on timbrels.


<a id="org677311e"></a>

## Psalms 67:27

In the churches bless ye God the Lord, from the fountains of Israel.


<a id="org21ce552"></a>

## Psalms 67:28

There is Benjamin a youth, in ecstasy of mind. The princes of Juda are their leaders: the princes of Zabulon, the princes of Nephthali.


<a id="org6e68dad"></a>

## Psalms 67:29

Command thy strength, O God confirm, O God, what thou hast wrought in us.


<a id="org31d3ed6"></a>

## Psalms 67:30

From thy temple in Jerusalem, kings shall offer presents to thee.


<a id="org770f4ee"></a>

## Psalms 67:31

Rebuke the wild beasts of the reeds, the congregation of bulls with the kine of the people; who seek to exclude them who are tried with silver. Scatter thou the nations that delight in wars:


<a id="org4ecb035"></a>

## Psalms 67:32

Ambassadors shall come out of Egypt: Ethiopia shall soon stretch out her hands to God.


<a id="org6354f1c"></a>

## Psalms 67:33

Sing to God, ye kingdoms of the earth: sing ye to the Lord: Sing ye to God,


<a id="org3c4d096"></a>

## Psalms 67:34

Who mounteth above the heaven of heavens, to the east. Behold he will give to his voice the voice of power:


<a id="org3a11386"></a>

## Psalms 67:35

Give ye glory to God for Israel, his magnificence, and his power is in the clouds.


<a id="org5c2227e"></a>

## Psalms 67:36

God is wonderful in his saints: the God of Israel is he who will give power and strength to his people. Blessed be God. 


<a id="org3eee097"></a>

# Psalms 68


<a id="org5fabb4e"></a>

## Psalms 68:1

Unto the end, for them that shall be changed; for David.


<a id="org0acba80"></a>

## Psalms 68:2

Save me, O God: for the waters are come in even unto my soul.


<a id="org75f55c0"></a>

## Psalms 68:3

I stick fast in the mire of the deep and there is no sure standing. I am come into the depth of the sea, and a tempest hath overwhelmed me.


<a id="orgef8c487"></a>

## Psalms 68:4

I have laboured with crying; my jaws are become hoarse, my eyes have failed, whilst I hope in my God.


<a id="orgd718b1c"></a>

## Psalms 68:5

They are multiplied above the hairs of my head, who hate me without cause. My enemies are grown strong who have wrongfully persecuted me: then did I pay that which I took not away.


<a id="orgd04e39e"></a>

## Psalms 68:6

O God, thou knowest my foolishness; and my offences are not hidden from thee:


<a id="orge5ae66a"></a>

## Psalms 68:7

Let not them be ashamed for me, who look for thee, O Lord, the Lord of hosts. Let them not be confounded on my account, who seek thee, O God of Israel.


<a id="orgb3807f3"></a>

## Psalms 68:8

Because for thy sake I have borne reproach; shame hath covered my face.


<a id="org0184158"></a>

## Psalms 68:9

I am become a stranger to my brethren, and an alien to the sons of my mother.


<a id="org8bea71f"></a>

## Psalms 68:10

For the zeal of thy house hath eaten me up: and the reproaches of them that reproached thee are fallen upon me.


<a id="orgeebf4a6"></a>

## Psalms 68:11

And I covered my soul in fasting: and it was made a reproach to me.


<a id="orgfcd0663"></a>

## Psalms 68:12

And I made haircloth my garment: and I became a byword to them.


<a id="org63832bb"></a>

## Psalms 68:13

They that sat in the gate spoke against me: and they that drank wine made me their song.


<a id="org846e799"></a>

## Psalms 68:14

But as for me, my prayer is to thee, O Lord; for the time of thy good pleasure, O God. In the multitude of thy mercy hear me, in the truth of thy salvation.


<a id="org756801e"></a>

## Psalms 68:15

Draw me out of the mire, that I may not stick fast: deliver me from them that hate me, and out of the deep waters.


<a id="org2374e2b"></a>

## Psalms 68:16

Let not the tempest of water drown me, nor the deep water swallow me up: and let not the pit shut her mouth upon me.


<a id="org18f04cc"></a>

## Psalms 68:17

Hear me, O Lord, for thy mercy is kind; look upon me according to the multitude of thy tender mercies.


<a id="orge51a230"></a>

## Psalms 68:18

And turn not away thy face from thy servant: for I am in trouble, hear me speedily.


<a id="orgaf84578"></a>

## Psalms 68:19

Attend to my soul, and deliver it: save me because of my enemies.


<a id="orgaeea26e"></a>

## Psalms 68:20

Thou knowest my reproach, and my confusion, and my shame.


<a id="org530b4ff"></a>

## Psalms 68:21

In thy sight are all they that afflict me; my heart hath expected reproach and misery. And I looked for one that would grieve together with me, but there was none: and for one that would comfort me, and I found none.


<a id="orge0114c7"></a>

## Psalms 68:22

And they gave me gall for my food, and in my thirst they gave me vinegar to drink.


<a id="org5c1e246"></a>

## Psalms 68:23

Let their table become as a snare before them, and a recompense, and a stumblingblock.


<a id="org8aee6ff"></a>

## Psalms 68:24

Let their eyes be darkened that they see not; and their back bend thou down always.


<a id="orgde29e0f"></a>

## Psalms 68:25

Pour out thy indignation upon them: and let thy wrathful anger take hold of them.


<a id="org1a4b48d"></a>

## Psalms 68:26

Let their habitation be made desolate: and let there be none to dwell in their tabernacles.


<a id="org904e7df"></a>

## Psalms 68:27

Because they have persecuted him whom thou hast smitten; and they have added to the grief of my wounds.


<a id="orgfd13a44"></a>

## Psalms 68:28

Add thou iniquity upon their iniquity: and let them not come into thy justice.


<a id="org64bb24f"></a>

## Psalms 68:29

Let them be blotted out of the book of the living; and with the just let them not be written.


<a id="org733a0d5"></a>

## Psalms 68:30

But I am poor and sorrowful: thy salvation, O God, hath set me up.


<a id="org610c6b4"></a>

## Psalms 68:31

I will praise the name of God with a canticle: and I will magnify him with praise.


<a id="org0df293d"></a>

## Psalms 68:32

And it shall please God better than a young calf, that bringeth forth horns and hoofs.


<a id="orgdf5c500"></a>

## Psalms 68:33

Let the poor see and rejoice: seek ye God, and your soul shall live.


<a id="org5eb8254"></a>

## Psalms 68:34

For the Lord hath heard the poor: and hath not despised his prisoners.


<a id="org8c1a97b"></a>

## Psalms 68:35

Let the heavens and the earth praise him; the sea, and every thing that creepeth therein.


<a id="org656705c"></a>

## Psalms 68:36

For God will save Sion, and the cities of Juda shall be built up. And they shall dwell there, and acquire it by inheritance.


<a id="orge2a200e"></a>

## Psalms 68:37

And the seed of his servants shall possess it; and they that love his name shall dwell therein. 


<a id="org3a57ef1"></a>

# Psalms 69


<a id="org15c438e"></a>

## Psalms 69:1

Unto the end, a psalm for David, to bring to remembrance that the Lord saved him.


<a id="org79f6de9"></a>

## Psalms 69:2

O God, come to my assistance; O Lord, make haste to help me.


<a id="orga0d8a06"></a>

## Psalms 69:3

Let them be confounded and ashamed that seek my soul:


<a id="org3c50e31"></a>

## Psalms 69:4

Let them be turned backward, and blush for shame that desire evils to me: Let them be presently turned away blushing for shame that say to me: &rsquo;Tis well, &rsquo;tis well.


<a id="orgc13b10c"></a>

## Psalms 69:5

Let all that seek thee rejoice and be glad in thee; and let such as love thy salvation say always: The Lord be magnified.


<a id="orge0a12cf"></a>

## Psalms 69:6

But I am needy and poor; O God, help me. Thou art my helper and my deliverer: O Lord, make no delay. 


<a id="org04a04f1"></a>

# Psalms 70


<a id="orge537391"></a>

## Psalms 70:1

A psalm for David. Of the sons of Jonadab, and the former captives. In thee, O Lord, I have hoped, let me never be put to confusion:


<a id="orga5a1e8f"></a>

## Psalms 70:2

Deliver me in thy justice, and rescue me. Incline thy ear unto me, and save me.


<a id="orge0d974c"></a>

## Psalms 70:3

Be thou unto me a God, a protector, and a place of strength: that thou mayst make me safe. For thou art my firmament and my refuge.


<a id="org4f04e37"></a>

## Psalms 70:4
