Deliver me, O my God, out of the hand of the sinner, and out of the hand of the transgressor of the law and of the unjust.


<a id="orgb4672ef"></a>

## Psalms 70:5

For thou art my patience, O Lord: my hope, O Lord, from my youth.


<a id="org47b2f6d"></a>

## Psalms 70:6

By thee have I been confirmed from the womb: from my mother&rsquo;s womb thou art my protector. Of thee I shall continually sing:


<a id="org825c43f"></a>

## Psalms 70:7

I am become unto many as a wonder, but thou art a strong helper.


<a id="org9f02544"></a>

## Psalms 70:8

Let my mouth be filled with praise, that I may sing thy glory; thy greatness all the day long.


<a id="orgebd5737"></a>

## Psalms 70:9

Cast me not off in the time of old age: when my strength shall fail, do not thou forsake me.


<a id="org22c6091"></a>

## Psalms 70:10

For my enemies have spoken against me; and they that watched my soul have consulted together,


<a id="org6aa30c6"></a>

## Psalms 70:11

Saying: God hath forsaken him: pursue and take him, for there is none to deliver him.


<a id="org83ee8c8"></a>

## Psalms 70:12

O God, be not thou far from me: O my God, make haste to my help.


<a id="orgfe6cb44"></a>

## Psalms 70:13

Let them be confounded and come to nothing that detract my soul; let them be covered with confusion and blame that seek my hurt.


<a id="orgecd2aa6"></a>

## Psalms 70:14

But I will always hope; and will add to all thy praise.


<a id="orge8c389e"></a>

## Psalms 70:15

My mouth shall shew forth thy justice; thy salvation all the day long. Because I have not known learning,


<a id="org1cb4411"></a>

## Psalms 70:16

I will enter into the powers of the Lord: O Lord, I will be mindful of thy justice alone.


<a id="orge92189f"></a>

## Psalms 70:17

Thou hast taught me, O God, from my youth: and till now I will declare thy wonderful works.


<a id="org2a5fdc7"></a>

## Psalms 70:18

And unto old age and grey hairs: O God, forsake me not, Until I shew forth thy arm to all the generation that is to come: Thy power,


<a id="orgf0b360b"></a>

## Psalms 70:19

And thy justice, O God, even to the highest great things thou hast done: O God, who is like to thee?


<a id="org532e45b"></a>

## Psalms 70:20

How great troubles hast thou shewn me, many and grievous: and turning thou hast brought me to life, and hast brought me back again from the depths of the earth:


<a id="org1c120d3"></a>

## Psalms 70:21

Thou hast multiplied thy magnificence; and turning to me thou hast comforted me.


<a id="org1de0389"></a>

## Psalms 70:22

For I will also confess to thee thy truth with the instruments of psaltery: O God, I will sing to thee with the harp, thou holy one of Israel.


<a id="orgdc99726"></a>

## Psalms 70:23

My lips shall greatly rejoice, when I shall sing to thee; and my soul which thou hast redeemed.


<a id="org231d9bc"></a>

## Psalms 70:24

Yea and my tongue shall meditate on thy justice all the day; when they shall be confounded and put to shame that seek evils to me. 


<a id="orgd150f5e"></a>

# Psalms 71


<a id="org72379be"></a>

## Psalms 71:1

A psalm on Solomon.


<a id="org1e6058d"></a>

## Psalms 71:2

Give to the king thy judgment, O God, and to the king&rsquo;s son thy justice: To judge thy people with justice, and thy poor with judgment.


<a id="org8db3e64"></a>

## Psalms 71:3

Let the mountains receive peace for the people: and the hills justice.


<a id="org9321973"></a>

## Psalms 71:4

He shall judge the poor of the people, and he shall save the children of the poor: and he shall humble the oppressor.


<a id="org4e9a9cd"></a>

## Psalms 71:5

And he shall continue with the sun and before the moon, throughout all generations.


<a id="org4b79590"></a>

## Psalms 71:6

He shall come down like rain upon the fleece; and as showers falling gently upon the earth.


<a id="org8c89ea7"></a>

## Psalms 71:7

In his days shall justice spring up, and abundance of peace, till the moon be taken away.


<a id="orgba669b9"></a>

## Psalms 71:8

And he shall rule from sea to sea, and from the river unto the ends of the earth.


<a id="org5d233fd"></a>

## Psalms 71:9

Before him the Ethiopians shall fall down: and his enemies shall lick the ground.


<a id="org3726b1c"></a>

## Psalms 71:10

The kings of Tharsis and the islands shall offer presents: the kings of the Arabians and of Saba shall bring gifts:


<a id="orgee9a9b7"></a>

## Psalms 71:11

And all kings of the earth shall adore him: all nations shall serve him.


<a id="org7b4f338"></a>

## Psalms 71:12

For he shall deliver the poor from the mighty: and the needy that had no helper.


<a id="orgf7fe0e3"></a>

## Psalms 71:13

He shall spare the poor and needy: and he shall save the souls of the poor.


<a id="org4068481"></a>

## Psalms 71:14

He shall redeem their souls from usuries and iniquity: and their names shall be honourable in his sight.


<a id="org4da2a5d"></a>

## Psalms 71:15

And he shall live, and to him shall be given of the gold of Arabia, for him they shall always adore: they shall bless him all the day.


<a id="org1e7335d"></a>

## Psalms 71:16

And there shall be a firmament on the earth on the tops of mountains, above Libanus shall the fruit thereof be exalted: and they of the city shall flourish like the grass of the earth.


<a id="orgf1095a6"></a>

## Psalms 71:17

Let his name be blessed for evermore: his name continueth before the sun. And in him shall all the tribes of the earth be blessed: all nations shall magnify him.


<a id="org784dcc0"></a>

## Psalms 71:18

Blessed be the Lord, the God of Israel, who alone doth wonderful things.


<a id="orgd32533d"></a>

## Psalms 71:19

And blessed be the name of his majesty for ever: and the whole earth shall be filled with his majesty. So be it. So be it.


<a id="org0373ff8"></a>

## Psalms 71:20

The praises of David, the son of Jesse, are ended. 


<a id="org2645729"></a>

# Psalms 72


<a id="org1a6ef4f"></a>

## Psalms 72:1

A psalm for Asaph. How good is God to Israel, to them that are of a right heart!


<a id="orga242f44"></a>

## Psalms 72:2

But my feet were almost moved; my steps had well nigh slipped.


<a id="orgb09ec36"></a>

## Psalms 72:3

Because I had a zeal on occasion of the wicked, seeing the prosperity of sinners.


<a id="orgaab9b99"></a>

## Psalms 72:4

For there is no regard to their death, nor is there strength in their stripes.


<a id="org257a3a4"></a>

## Psalms 72:5

They are not in the labour of men: neither shall they be scourged like other men.


<a id="orgae5aed1"></a>

## Psalms 72:6

Therefore pride hath held them fast: they are covered with their iniquity and their wickedness.


<a id="org5194b49"></a>

## Psalms 72:7

Their iniquity hath come forth, as it were from fatness: they have passed into the affection of the heart.


<a id="org14392f2"></a>

## Psalms 72:8

They have thought and spoken wickedness: they have spoken iniquity on high.


<a id="orgd979080"></a>

## Psalms 72:9

They have set their mouth against heaven: and their tongue hath passed through the earth.


<a id="org7d8d75d"></a>

## Psalms 72:10

Therefore will my people return here and full days shall be found in them.


<a id="org3190d77"></a>

## Psalms 72:11

And they said: How doth God know? and is there knowledge in the most High?


<a id="org82ef0d5"></a>

## Psalms 72:12

Behold these are sinners; and yet, abounding in the world they have obtained riches.


<a id="org08f8c6c"></a>

## Psalms 72:13

And I said: Then have I in vain justified my heart, and washed my hands among the innocent.


<a id="orgd00ad86"></a>

## Psalms 72:14

And I have been scourged all the day; and my chastisement hath been in the mornings.


<a id="org7209247"></a>

## Psalms 72:15

If I said: I will speak thus; behold I should condemn the generation of thy children.


<a id="org4f7266e"></a>

## Psalms 72:16

I studied that I might know this thing, it is a labour in my sight:


<a id="org3222d8e"></a>

## Psalms 72:17

Until I go into the sanctuary of God, and understand concerning their last ends.


<a id="orgc8328f5"></a>

## Psalms 72:18

But indeed for deceits thou hast put it to them: when they were lifted up thou hast cast them down.


<a id="orge5b4bff"></a>

## Psalms 72:19

How are they brought to desolation? they have suddenly ceased to be: they have perished by reason of their iniquity.


<a id="org62aa2c2"></a>

## Psalms 72:20

As the dream of them that awake, O Lord; so in thy city thou shalt bring their image to nothing.


<a id="org53db610"></a>

## Psalms 72:21

For my heart hath been inflamed, and my reins have been changed:


<a id="orgf643e6a"></a>

## Psalms 72:22

And I am brought to nothing, and I knew not.


<a id="org075b34b"></a>

## Psalms 72:23

I am become as a beast before thee: and I am always with thee.


<a id="org9188527"></a>

## Psalms 72:24

Thou hast held me by my right hand; and by thy will thou hast conducted me, and with thy glory thou hast received me.


<a id="org71eecd3"></a>

## Psalms 72:25

For what have I in heaven? and besides thee what do I desire upon earth?


<a id="orgcbdc597"></a>

## Psalms 72:26

For thee my flesh and my heart hath fainted away: thou art the God of my heart, and the God that is my portion for ever.


<a id="orgda9e0e1"></a>

## Psalms 72:27

For behold they that go far from thee shall perish: thou hast destroyed all them that are disloyal to thee.


<a id="org681caf9"></a>

## Psalms 72:28

But it is good for me to adhere to my God, to put my hope in the Lord God: That I may declare all thy praises, in the gates of the daughter of Sion. 


<a id="org98c6f6b"></a>

# Psalms 73


<a id="orgba66db0"></a>

## Psalms 73:1

Understanding for Asaph. O God, why hast thou cast us off unto the end: why is thy wrath enkindled against the sheep of thy pasture?


<a id="orge911e98"></a>

## Psalms 73:2

Remember thy congregation, which thou hast possessed from the beginning. The sceptre of thy inheritance which thou hast redeemed: mount Sion in which thou hast dwelt.


<a id="org209ece8"></a>

## Psalms 73:3

Lift up thy hands against their pride unto the end; see what things the enemy hath done wickedly in the sanctuary.


<a id="org7d56bc8"></a>

## Psalms 73:4

And they that hate thee have made their boasts, in the midst of thy solemnity. They have set up their ensigns for signs,


<a id="org2cc06be"></a>

## Psalms 73:5

And they knew not both in the going out and on the highest top. As with axes in a wood of trees,


<a id="orgc925c28"></a>

## Psalms 73:6

They have cut down at once the gates thereof, with axe and hatchet they have brought it down.


<a id="org358f718"></a>

## Psalms 73:7

They have set fire to thy sanctuary: they have defiled the dwelling place of thy name on the earth.


<a id="orgb16dee9"></a>

## Psalms 73:8

They said in their heart, the whole kindred of them together: Let us abolish all the festival days of God from the land.


<a id="org2b43b7e"></a>

## Psalms 73:9

Our signs we have not seen, there is now no prophet: and he will know us no more.


<a id="org8d34bbb"></a>

## Psalms 73:10

How long, O God, shall the enemy reproach: is the adversary to provoke thy name for ever?


<a id="org31444d6"></a>

## Psalms 73:11

Why dost thou turn away thy hand: and thy right hand out of the midst of thy bosom for ever?


<a id="orgd254668"></a>

## Psalms 73:12

But God is our king before ages: he hath wrought salvation in the midst of the earth.


<a id="org9311b6d"></a>

## Psalms 73:13

Thou by thy strength didst make the sea firm: thou didst crush the heads of the dragons in the waters.


<a id="orge213f22"></a>

## Psalms 73:14

Thou hast broken the heads of the dragon: thou hast given him to be meat for the people of the Ethiopians.


<a id="orgd511fc6"></a>

## Psalms 73:15

Thou hast broken up the fountains and the torrents: thou hast dried up the Ethan rivers.


<a id="org95cf374"></a>

## Psalms 73:16

Thine is the day, and thine is the night: thou hast made the morning light and the sun.


<a id="org0195312"></a>

## Psalms 73:17

Thou hast made all the borders of the earth: the summer and the spring were formed by thee.


<a id="orgcf142d6"></a>

## Psalms 73:18

Remember this, the enemy hath reproached the Lord: and a foolish people hath provoked thy name.


<a id="org3f442e7"></a>

## Psalms 73:19

Deliver not up to beasts the souls that confess to thee: and forget not to the end the souls of thy poor.


<a id="org0a845dd"></a>

## Psalms 73:20

Have regard to thy covenant: for they that are the obscure of the earth have been filled with dwellings of iniquity.


<a id="orgc40dec3"></a>

## Psalms 73:21

Let not the humble be turned away with confusion: the poor and needy shall praise thy name.


<a id="orgf762d47"></a>

## Psalms 73:22

Arise, O God, judge thy own cause: remember thy reproaches with which the foolish man hath reproached thee all the day.


<a id="orgfb3b254"></a>

## Psalms 73:23

Forget not the voices of thy enemies: the pride of them that hate thee ascendeth continually. 


<a id="org04a7e11"></a>

# Psalms 74


<a id="org8b3a8e9"></a>

## Psalms 74:1

Unto the end, corrupt not, a psalm of a canticle for Asaph.


<a id="org101de7b"></a>

## Psalms 74:2

We will praise thee, O God: we will praise, and we will call upon thy name. We will relate thy wondrous works:


<a id="orga34b1b1"></a>

## Psalms 74:3

When I shall take a time, I will judge justices.


<a id="org20ee652"></a>

## Psalms 74:4

The earth is melted, and all that dwell therein: I have established the pillars thereof.


<a id="orgc25574a"></a>

## Psalms 74:5

I said to the wicked: Do not act wickedly: and to the sinners: Lift not up the horn.


<a id="orgf11fb70"></a>

## Psalms 74:6

Lift not up your horn on high: speak not iniquity against God.


<a id="orgda7ddea"></a>

## Psalms 74:7

For neither from the east, nor from the west, nor from the desert hills:


<a id="orgb238614"></a>

## Psalms 74:8

For God is the judge. One he putteth down, and another he lifteth up:


<a id="orgeca5ea0"></a>

## Psalms 74:9

For in the hand of the Lord there is a cup of strong wine full of mixture. And he hath poured it out from this to that: but the dregs thereof are not emptied: all the sinners of the earth shall drink.


<a id="orga9e16e3"></a>

## Psalms 74:10

But I will declare for ever: I will sing to the God of Jacob.


<a id="org813e76f"></a>

## Psalms 74:11

And I will break all the horns of sinners: but the horns of the just shall be exalted. 


<a id="org17ecb76"></a>

# Psalms 75


<a id="org424bbf2"></a>

## Psalms 75:1

Unto the end, in praises, a psalm for Asaph: a canticle to the Assyrians.


<a id="org27d3f35"></a>

## Psalms 75:2

In Judea God is known: his name is great in Israel.


<a id="orge5ff7c1"></a>

## Psalms 75:3

And his place is in peace: and his abode in Sion:


<a id="orgb77112b"></a>

## Psalms 75:4

There hath he broken the powers of bows, the shield, the sword, and the battle.


<a id="orgcb0431e"></a>

## Psalms 75:5

Thou enlightenest wonderfully from the everlasting hills.


<a id="org602cabe"></a>

## Psalms 75:6

All the foolish of heart were troubled. They have slept their sleep; and all the men of riches have found nothing in their hands.


<a id="org850a111"></a>

## Psalms 75:7

At thy rebuke, O God of Jacob, they have all slumbered that mounted on horseback.


<a id="orgb0a7b40"></a>

## Psalms 75:8

Thou art terrible, and who shall resist thee? from that time thy wrath.


<a id="org023a52b"></a>

## Psalms 75:9

Thou hast caused judgment to be heard from heaven: the earth trembled and was still,


<a id="orgde84f4b"></a>

## Psalms 75:10

When God arose in judgment, to save all the meek of the earth.


<a id="org41f7594"></a>

## Psalms 75:11

For the thought of man shall give praise to thee: and the remainders of the thought shall keep holiday to thee.


<a id="org9d54b99"></a>

## Psalms 75:12

Vow ye, and pay to the Lord your God: all you that are round about him bring presents. To him that is terrible,


<a id="orga789004"></a>

## Psalms 75:13

Even to him who taketh away the spirit of princes: to the terrible with the kings of the earth. 


<a id="org10f7696"></a>

# Psalms 76


<a id="orgf471411"></a>

## Psalms 76:1

Unto the end, for Idithun, a psalm of Asaph.


<a id="org21e001b"></a>

## Psalms 76:2

I cried to the Lord with my voice; to God with my voice, and he gave ear to me.


<a id="orgb7340f3"></a>

## Psalms 76:3

In the days of my trouble I sought God, with my hands lifted up to him in the night, and I was not deceived. My soul refused to be comforted:


<a id="orgb293fbe"></a>

## Psalms 76:4

I remembered God, and was delighted, and was exercised, and my spirit swooned away.


<a id="org7100f1a"></a>

## Psalms 76:5

My eyes prevented the watches: I was troubled, and I spoke not.


<a id="orgc78846c"></a>

## Psalms 76:6

I thought upon the days of old: and I had in my mind the eternal years.


<a id="orgc9669e9"></a>

## Psalms 76:7

And I meditated in the night with my own heart: and I was exercised and I swept my spirit.


<a id="orge851d92"></a>

## Psalms 76:8

Will God then cast off for ever? or will he never be more favourable again?


<a id="org2d9f76a"></a>

## Psalms 76:9

Or will he cut off his mercy for ever, from generation to generation?


<a id="org9327b50"></a>

## Psalms 76:10

Or will God forget to shew mercy? or will he in his anger shut up his mercies?


<a id="org881430e"></a>

## Psalms 76:11

And I said, Now have I begun: this is the change of the right hand of the most High.


<a id="orga928e4e"></a>

## Psalms 76:12

I remembered the works of the Lord: for I will be mindful of thy wonders from the beginning.


<a id="org685c3d2"></a>

## Psalms 76:13

And I will meditate on all thy works: and will be employed in thy inventions.


<a id="orge61e08a"></a>

## Psalms 76:14

Thy way, O God, is in the holy place: who is the great God like our God?


<a id="org1de0ec8"></a>

## Psalms 76:15

Thou art the God that dost wonders. Thou hast made thy power known among the nations:


<a id="org11fc203"></a>

## Psalms 76:16

With thy arm thou hast redeemed thy people the children of Jacob and of Joseph.


<a id="org596e1e3"></a>

## Psalms 76:17

The waters saw thee, O God, the waters saw thee: and they were afraid, and the depths were troubled.


<a id="orgb74ab18"></a>

## Psalms 76:18

Great was the noise of the waters: the clouds sent out a sound. For thy arrows pass:


<a id="org35efbb8"></a>

## Psalms 76:19

The voice of thy thunder in a wheel. Thy lightnings enlightened the world: the earth shook and trembled.


<a id="org8921640"></a>

## Psalms 76:20

Thy way is in the sea, and thy paths in many waters: and thy footsteps shall not be known.


<a id="org63bb148"></a>

## Psalms 76:21

Thou hast conducted thy people like sheep, by the hand of Moses and Aaron. 


<a id="orgef7c75f"></a>

# Psalms 77


<a id="org90ed145"></a>

## Psalms 77:1

Understanding for Asaph. Attend, O my people, to my law: incline your ears to the words of my mouth.


<a id="org4d1e339"></a>

## Psalms 77:2

I will open my mouth in parables: I will utter propositions from the beginning.


<a id="org7393a93"></a>

## Psalms 77:3

How great things have we heard and known, and our fathers have told us.


<a id="org5b11a92"></a>

## Psalms 77:4

They have not been hidden from their children, in another generation. Declaring the praises of the Lord, and his powers, and his wonders which he hath done.


<a id="org3741451"></a>

## Psalms 77:5

And he set up a testimony in Jacob: and made a law in Israel. How great things he commanded our fathers, that they should make the same known to their children:


<a id="orga2b9801"></a>

## Psalms 77:6

That another generation might know them. The children that should be born and should rise up, and declare them to their children.


<a id="org50bb197"></a>

## Psalms 77:7

That they may put their hope in God and may not forget the works of God: and may seek his commandments.


<a id="orga462eb0"></a>

## Psalms 77:8

That they may not become like their fathers, a perverse and exasperating generation. A generation that set not their heart aright: and whose spirit was not faithful to God.


<a id="orgd971027"></a>

## Psalms 77:9

The sons of Ephraim who bend and shoot with the bow: they have turned back in the day of battle.


<a id="orgf18b81f"></a>

## Psalms 77:10

They kept not the covenant of God: and in his law they would not walk.


<a id="org657a789"></a>

## Psalms 77:11

And they forgot his benefits, and his wonders that he had shewn them.


<a id="orgabef0b5"></a>

## Psalms 77:12

Wonderful things did he do in the sight of their fathers, in the land of Egypt, in the field of Tanis.


<a id="org0bf612b"></a>

## Psalms 77:13

He divided the sea and brought them through: and he made the waters to stand as in a vessel.


<a id="org7e1afd6"></a>

## Psalms 77:14

And he conducted them with a cloud by day: and all the night with a light of fire.


<a id="orgdfbf3a9"></a>

## Psalms 77:15

He struck the rock in the wilderness: and gave them to drink, as out of the great deep.


<a id="org8de7ef0"></a>

## Psalms 77:16

He brought forth water out of the rock: and made streams run down as rivers.


<a id="org264fe3b"></a>

## Psalms 77:17

And they added yet more sin against him: they provoked the most High to wrath in the place without water.


<a id="org83fa4c9"></a>

## Psalms 77:18

And they tempted God in their hearts, by asking meat for their desires.


<a id="org815e937"></a>

## Psalms 77:19

And they spoke ill of God: they said: Can God furnish a table in the wilderness?


<a id="org1de1236"></a>

## Psalms 77:20

Because he struck the rock, and the waters gushed out, and the streams overflowed. Can he also give bread, or provide a table for his people?


<a id="org83b7d21"></a>

## Psalms 77:21

Therefore the Lord heard, and was angry: and a fire was kindled against Jacob, and wrath came up against Israel.


<a id="org0a956e7"></a>

## Psalms 77:22

Because they believed not in God: and trusted not in his salvation.


<a id="org2c7c3d1"></a>

## Psalms 77:23

And he had commanded the clouds from above, and had opened the doors of heaven.


<a id="org58a04f0"></a>

## Psalms 77:24

And had rained down manna upon them to eat, and had given them the bread of heaven.


<a id="orgc22b0c5"></a>

## Psalms 77:25

Man ate the bread of angels: he sent them provisions in abundance.


<a id="org92e469f"></a>

## Psalms 77:26

He removed the south wind from heaven: and by his power brought in the southwest wind.


<a id="org8c3b313"></a>

## Psalms 77:27

And he rained upon them flesh as dust: and feathered fowls like as the sand of the sea.


<a id="org988bde5"></a>

## Psalms 77:28

And they fell in the midst of their camp, round about their pavilions.


<a id="org5911288"></a>

## Psalms 77:29

So they did eat, and were filled exceedingly, and he gave them their desire:


<a id="org8fea224"></a>

## Psalms 77:30

they were not defrauded of that which they craved. As yet their meat was in their mouth:


<a id="org4d4c47a"></a>

## Psalms 77:31

And the wrath of God came upon them. And he slew the fat ones amongst them, and brought down the chosen men of Israel.


<a id="orgba56238"></a>

## Psalms 77:32

In all these things they sinned still: and they behaved not for his wondrous works.


<a id="org59a5bfd"></a>

## Psalms 77:33

And their days were consumed in vanity, and their years in haste.


<a id="org71a8765"></a>

## Psalms 77:34

When he slew them, then they sought him: and they returned, and came to him early in the morning.


<a id="orge42813f"></a>

## Psalms 77:35

And they remembered that God was their helper: and the most high God their redeemer.


<a id="org3b29922"></a>

## Psalms 77:36

And they loved him with their mouth: and with their tongue they lied unto him:


<a id="org1f53673"></a>

## Psalms 77:37

But their heart was not right with him: nor were they counted faithful in his covenant.


<a id="org72e6aeb"></a>

## Psalms 77:38

But he is merciful, and will forgive their sins: and will not destroy them. And many a time did he turn away his anger: and did not kindle all his wrath.


<a id="org6991b38"></a>

## Psalms 77:39

And he remembered that they are flesh: a wind that goeth and returneth not.


<a id="org99cc1fe"></a>

## Psalms 77:40

How often did they provoke him in the desert: and move him to wrath in the place without water?


<a id="orgb3b6abd"></a>

## Psalms 77:41

And they turned back and tempted God: and grieved the holy one of Israel.


<a id="org0b3391b"></a>

## Psalms 77:42

They remembered not his hand, in the day that he redeemed them from the hand of him that afflicted them:


<a id="orgcff5c76"></a>

## Psalms 77:43

How he wrought his signs in Egypt, and his wonders in the field of Tanis.


<a id="orgdfaabbe"></a>

## Psalms 77:44

And he turned their rivers into blood, and their showers that they might not drink.


<a id="orgc23e9e6"></a>

## Psalms 77:45

He sent amongst them divers sorts of flies, which devoured them: and frogs which destroyed them.


<a id="org0dc79c0"></a>

## Psalms 77:46

And he gave up their fruits to the blast, and their labours to the locust.


<a id="org2d74fa4"></a>

## Psalms 77:47

And he destroyed their vineyards with hail, and their mulberry trees with hoarfrost.


<a id="orge64da3f"></a>

## Psalms 77:48

And he gave up their cattle to the hail, and their stock to the fire.


<a id="orge429018"></a>

## Psalms 77:49

And he sent upon them the wrath of his indignation: indignation and wrath and trouble, which he sent by evil angels.


<a id="org1f1b97b"></a>

## Psalms 77:50

He made a way for a path to his anger: he spared not their souls from death, and their cattle he shut up in death.


<a id="org54146c4"></a>

## Psalms 77:51

And he killed all the firstborn in the land of Egypt: the firstfruits of all their labour in the tabernacles of Cham.


<a id="org2fcdc85"></a>

## Psalms 77:52

And he took away his own people as sheep: and guided them in the wilderness like a flock.


<a id="org61528b4"></a>

## Psalms 77:53

And he brought them out in hope and they feared not: and the sea overwhelmed their enemies.


<a id="org3eb6455"></a>

## Psalms 77:54

And he brought them into the mountain of his sanctuary: the mountain which his right hand had purchased. And he cast out the Gentiles before them: and by lot divided to them their land by a line of distribution.


<a id="org6190f0d"></a>

## Psalms 77:55

And he made the tribes of Israel to dwell in their tabernacles.


<a id="org705bbe2"></a>

## Psalms 77:56

Yet they tempted, and provoked the most high God: and they kept not his testimonies.


<a id="orgcffaccc"></a>

## Psalms 77:57

And they turned away, and kept not the covenant: even like their fathers they were turned aside as a crooked bow.


<a id="org3936958"></a>

## Psalms 77:58

They provoked him to anger on their hills: and moved him to jealousy with their graven things.


<a id="orgeab7668"></a>

## Psalms 77:59

God heard, and despised them, and he reduced Israel exceedingly as it were to nothing.


<a id="org8effa10"></a>

## Psalms 77:60

And he put away the tabernacle of Silo, his tabernacle where he dwelt among men.


<a id="org68e1eaa"></a>

## Psalms 77:61

And he delivered their strength into captivity: and their beauty into the hands of the enemy.


<a id="org28c6ee3"></a>

## Psalms 77:62

And he shut up his people under the sword: and he despised his inheritance.


<a id="org7986ba8"></a>

## Psalms 77:63

Fire consumed their young men: and their maidens were not lamented.


<a id="org5d744b8"></a>

## Psalms 77:64

Their priests fell by the sword: and their widows did not mourn.


<a id="org8fb43f3"></a>

## Psalms 77:65

And the Lord was awaked as one out of sleep, and like a mighty man that hath been surfeited with wine.


<a id="org25fd837"></a>

## Psalms 77:66

And he smote his enemies on the hinder parts: he put them to an everlasting reproach.


<a id="org96536ec"></a>

## Psalms 77:67

And he rejected the tabernacle of Joseph: and chose not the tribe of Ephraim:


<a id="org77a3be8"></a>

## Psalms 77:68

But he chose the tribe of Juda, mount Sion which he loved.


<a id="orgdd5c956"></a>

## Psalms 77:69

And he built his sanctuary as of unicorns, in the land which he founded for ever.


<a id="org0fe768b"></a>

## Psalms 77:70

And he chose his servant David, and took him from the flocks of sheep: he brought him from following the ewes great with young,


<a id="orgc7fb56c"></a>

## Psalms 77:71

To feed Jacob his servant and Israel his inheritance.


<a id="org92cf9e7"></a>

## Psalms 77:72

And he fed them in the innocence of his heart: and conducted them by the skilfulness of his hands. 


<a id="orgc9824c3"></a>

# Psalms 78


<a id="org87d8af7"></a>

## Psalms 78:1

A psalm for Asaph. O God, the heathens are come into thy inheritance, they have defiled thy holy temple: they have made Jerusalem as a place to keep fruit.


<a id="orgb008741"></a>

## Psalms 78:2

They have given the dead bodies of thy servants to be meat for the fowls of the air: the flesh of thy saints for the beasts of the earth.


<a id="orgf80a962"></a>

## Psalms 78:3

They have poured out their blood as water, round about Jerusalem and there was none to bury them.


<a id="orga38ff15"></a>

## Psalms 78:4

We are become a reproach to our neighbours: a scorn and derision to them that are round about us.


<a id="org2e555b1"></a>

## Psalms 78:5

How long, O Lord, wilt thou be angry for ever: shall thy zeal be kindled like a fire?


<a id="org65d4f04"></a>

## Psalms 78:6

Pour out thy wrath upon the nations that have not known thee: and upon the kingdoms that have not called upon thy name.


<a id="org15eb4cc"></a>

## Psalms 78:7

Because they have devoured Jacob; and have laid waste his place.


<a id="orgf54b319"></a>

## Psalms 78:8

Remember not our former iniquities: let thy mercies speedily prevent us, for we are become exceeding poor.


<a id="org3101028"></a>

## Psalms 78:9

Help us, O God, our saviour: and for the glory of thy name, O Lord, deliver us: and forgive us our sins for thy name&rsquo;s sake:


<a id="org25329fc"></a>

## Psalms 78:10

Lest they should say among the Gentiles: Where is their God? And let him be made known among the nations before our eyes, By the revenging the blood of thy servants, which hath been shed:


<a id="org5a2e377"></a>

## Psalms 78:11

Let the sighing of the prisoners come in before thee. According to the greatness of thy arm, take possession of the children of them that have been put to death.


<a id="orgfef69ad"></a>

## Psalms 78:12

And render to our neighbours sevenfold in their bosom: the reproach wherewith they have reproached thee, O Lord.


<a id="org0d5945d"></a>

## Psalms 78:13

But we thy people, and the sheep of thy pasture, will give thanks to thee for ever. We will shew forth thy praise, unto generation and generation. 


<a id="org6898b35"></a>

# Psalms 79


<a id="org3e953a0"></a>

## Psalms 79:1

Unto the end, for them that shall be changed, a testimony for Asaph, a psalm.


<a id="orgf9f24ea"></a>

## Psalms 79:2

Give ear, O thou that rulest Israel: thou that leadest Joseph like a sheep. Thou that sittest upon the cherubims, shine forth


<a id="orgb938fc7"></a>

## Psalms 79:3

Before Ephraim, Benjamin, and Manasses. Stir up thy might, and come to save us.


<a id="org9fb1a38"></a>

## Psalms 79:4

Convert us, O God: and shew us thy face, and we shall be saved.


<a id="orgb08670d"></a>

## Psalms 79:5

O Lord God of hosts, how long wilt thou be angry against the prayer of thy servant?


<a id="org6286bae"></a>

## Psalms 79:6

How long wilt thou feed us with the bread of tears: and give us for our drink tears in measure?


<a id="org0e2f869"></a>

## Psalms 79:7

Thou hast made us to be a contradiction to our neighbours: and our enemies have scoffed at us.


<a id="org2f08f61"></a>

## Psalms 79:8

O God of hosts, convert us: and shew thy face, and we shall be saved.


<a id="orgfea865e"></a>

## Psalms 79:9

Thou hast brought a vineyard out of Egypt: thou hast cast out the Gentiles and planted it.


<a id="org1453bc5"></a>

## Psalms 79:10

Thou wast the guide of its journey in its sight: thou plantedst the roots thereof, and it filled the land.


<a id="orgd3b5de3"></a>

## Psalms 79:11

The shadow of it covered the hills: and the branches thereof the cedars of God.


<a id="org15391d7"></a>

## Psalms 79:12

It stretched forth its branches unto the sea, and its boughs unto the river.


<a id="org992f142"></a>

## Psalms 79:13

Why hast thou broken down the hedge thereof, so that all they who pass by the way do pluck it?


<a id="orgfd22ff6"></a>

## Psalms 79:14

The boar out of the wood hath laid it waste: and a singular wild beast hath devoured it.


<a id="orgd456ce4"></a>

## Psalms 79:15

Turn again, O God of hosts, look down from heaven, and see, and visit this vineyard:


<a id="org478c7f9"></a>

## Psalms 79:16

And perfect the same which thy right hand hath planted: and upon the son of man whom thou hast confirmed for thyself.


<a id="org9d022ed"></a>

## Psalms 79:17

Things set on fire and dug down shall perish at the rebuke of thy countenance.


<a id="org295c0b0"></a>

## Psalms 79:18

Let thy hand be upon the man of thy right hand: and upon the son of man whom thou hast confirmed for thyself.


<a id="org043bd3c"></a>

## Psalms 79:19

And we depart not from thee, thou shalt quicken us: and we will call upon thy name.


<a id="org5ce8c30"></a>

## Psalms 79:20

O Lord God of hosts, convert us and shew thy face, and we shall be saved. 


<a id="org2a2a4ec"></a>

# Psalms 80


<a id="org91b8029"></a>

## Psalms 80:1

Unto the end, for the winepresses, a psalm for Asaph himself.


<a id="orgb7aa4aa"></a>

## Psalms 80:2

Rejoice to God our helper: sing aloud to the God of Jacob.


<a id="org71cac05"></a>

## Psalms 80:3

Take a psalm, and bring hither the timbrel: the pleasant psaltery with the harp.


<a id="org55968f2"></a>

## Psalms 80:4

Blow up the trumpet on the new moon, on the noted day of your solemnity.


<a id="org48ae80f"></a>

## Psalms 80:5

For it is a commandment in Israel, and a judgment to the God of Jacob.


<a id="org94aed36"></a>

## Psalms 80:6

He ordained it for a testimony in Joseph, when he came out of the land of Egypt: he heard a tongue which he knew not.


<a id="orga8cdf49"></a>

## Psalms 80:7

He removed his back from the burdens: his hands had served in baskets.


<a id="org0b121cd"></a>

## Psalms 80:8

Thou calledst upon me in affliction, and I delivered thee: I heard thee in the secret place of tempest: I proved thee at the waters of contradiction.


<a id="org47a8350"></a>

## Psalms 80:9

Hear, O my people, and I will testify to thee: O Israel, if thou wilt hearken to me,


<a id="org9d071d1"></a>

## Psalms 80:10

there shall be no new god in thee: neither shalt thou adore a strange god.


<a id="orga154f73"></a>

## Psalms 80:11

For I am the Lord thy God, who brought thee out of the land of Egypt: open thy mouth wide, and I will fill it.


<a id="org99f1a69"></a>

## Psalms 80:12

But my people heard not my voice: and Israel hearkened not to me.


<a id="orgde693db"></a>

## Psalms 80:13

So I let them go according to the desires of their heart: they shall walk in their own inventions.


<a id="org0b24856"></a>

## Psalms 80:14

If my people had heard me: if Israel had walked in my ways:


<a id="org204229e"></a>

## Psalms 80:15

I should soon have humbled their enemies, and laid my hand on them that troubled them.


<a id="org7cdf7d4"></a>

## Psalms 80:16

The enemies of the Lord have lied to him: and their time shall be for ever.


<a id="orgb4f67cb"></a>

## Psalms 80:17

And he fed them with the fat of wheat, and filled them with honey out of the rock. 


<a id="orgd5710cd"></a>

# Psalms 81


<a id="orge3710dd"></a>

## Psalms 81:1

A psalm for Asaph. God hath stood in the congregation of gods: and being in the midst of them he judgeth gods.


<a id="orge8f2305"></a>

## Psalms 81:2

How long will you judge unjustly: and accept the persons of the wicked?


<a id="org526d0f4"></a>

## Psalms 81:3

Judge for the needy and fatherless: do justice to the humble and the poor.


<a id="orge5550ea"></a>

## Psalms 81:4

Rescue the poor; and deliver the needy out of the hand of the sinner.


<a id="org1f7be66"></a>

## Psalms 81:5

They have not known nor understood: they walk on in darkness: all the foundations of the earth shall be moved.


<a id="orgae09248"></a>

## Psalms 81:6

I have said: You are gods and all of you the sons of the most High.


<a id="orgab4d9c8"></a>

## Psalms 81:7

But you like men shall die: and shall fall like one of the princes.


<a id="org57f612a"></a>

## Psalms 81:8

Arise, O God, judge thou the earth: for thou shalt inherit among all the nations. 


<a id="orgee3f5d0"></a>

# Psalms 82


<a id="org90603d5"></a>

## Psalms 82:1

A canticle of a psalm for Asaph.


<a id="orgc7901bd"></a>

## Psalms 82:2

O God, who shall be like to thee? hold not thy peace, neither be thou still, O God.


<a id="org779beeb"></a>

## Psalms 82:3

For lo, thy enemies have made a noise: and they that hate thee have lifted up the head.


<a id="org6af790c"></a>

## Psalms 82:4

They have taken a malicious counsel against thy people, and have consulted against thy saints.


<a id="orgb5dc5a8"></a>

## Psalms 82:5

They have said: Come and let us destroy them, so that they be not a nation: and let the name of Israel be remembered no more.


<a id="orga0eebea"></a>

## Psalms 82:6

For they have contrived with one consent: they have made a covenant together against thee,


<a id="org82c4182"></a>

## Psalms 82:7

The tabernacle of the Edomites, and the Ishmahelites: Moab, and the Agarens,


<a id="org35e7c70"></a>

## Psalms 82:8

Gebal, and Ammon and Amalec: the Philistines, with the inhabitants of Tyre.


<a id="org1a2225e"></a>

## Psalms 82:9

Yea, and the Assyrian also is joined with them: they are come to the aid of the sons of Lot.


<a id="orgc28378f"></a>

## Psalms 82:10

Do to them as thou didst to Madian and to Sisara: as to Jabin at the brook of Cisson.


<a id="orga9f52e1"></a>

## Psalms 82:11

Who perished at Endor: and became as dung for the earth.


<a id="orged4e147"></a>

## Psalms 82:12

Make their princes like Oreb, and Zeb, and Zebee, and Salmana. All their princes,


<a id="orgb183d2f"></a>

## Psalms 82:13

Who have said: Let us possess the sanctuary of God for an inheritance.


<a id="org4adae4e"></a>

## Psalms 82:14

O my God, make them like a wheel; and as stubble before the wind.


<a id="orgafbb34c"></a>

## Psalms 82:15

As fire which burneth the wood: and as a flame burning mountains:


<a id="orgea45b8f"></a>

## Psalms 82:16

So shalt thou pursue them with thy tempest: and shalt trouble them in thy wrath.


<a id="org7f67376"></a>

## Psalms 82:17

Fill their faces with shame; and they shall seek thy name, O Lord.


<a id="orgd2d0ab8"></a>

## Psalms 82:18

Let them be ashamed and troubled for ever and ever: and let them be confounded and perish.


<a id="org452260b"></a>

## Psalms 82:19

And let them know that the Lord is thy name: thou alone art the most High over all the earth. 


<a id="org935a2ce"></a>

# Psalms 83


<a id="org323ce59"></a>

## Psalms 83:1

Unto the end, for the winepresses, a psalm for the sons of Core.


<a id="org51b0707"></a>

## Psalms 83:2

How lovely are thy tabernacles, O Lord of hosts!


<a id="org0c94821"></a>

## Psalms 83:3

my soul longeth and fainteth for the courts of the Lord. My heart and my flesh have rejoiced in the living God.


<a id="orgaef74f0"></a>

## Psalms 83:4

For the sparrow hath found herself a house, and the turtle a nest for herself where she may lay her young ones: Thy altars, O Lord of hosts, my king and my God.


<a id="org1f22255"></a>

## Psalms 83:5

Blessed are they that dwell in thy house, O Lord: they shall praise thee for ever and ever.


<a id="org0b8fd07"></a>

## Psalms 83:6

Blessed is the man whose help is from thee: in his heart he hath disposed to ascend by steps,


<a id="org726375c"></a>

## Psalms 83:7

In the vale of tears, in the place which he hath set.


<a id="orga8310de"></a>

## Psalms 83:8

For the lawgiver shall give a blessing, they shall go from virtue to virtue: the God of gods shall be seen in Sion.


<a id="org7afc257"></a>

## Psalms 83:9

O Lord God of hosts, hear my prayer: give ear, O God of Jacob.


<a id="org6ecea29"></a>

## Psalms 83:10

Behold, O God our protector: and look on the face of thy Christ.


<a id="orge88ed08"></a>

## Psalms 83:11

For better is one day in thy courts above thousands. I have chosen to be an abject in the house of my God, rather than to dwell in the tabernacles of sinners.


<a id="org931ad0e"></a>

## Psalms 83:12

For God loveth mercy and truth: the Lord will give grace and glory.


<a id="org2dc1b90"></a>

## Psalms 83:13

He will not deprive of good things them that walk in innocence: O Lord of hosts, blessed is the man that trusteth in thee. 


<a id="org6273119"></a>

# Psalms 84


<a id="orgb62b972"></a>

## Psalms 84:1

Unto the end, for the sons of Core, a psalm.


<a id="orgfd7950b"></a>

## Psalms 84:2

Lord, thou hast blessed thy land: thou hast turned away the captivity of Jacob.


<a id="orgfbe2507"></a>

## Psalms 84:3

Thou hast forgiven the iniquity of thy people: thou hast covered all their sins.


<a id="orgc86048a"></a>

## Psalms 84:4

Thou hast mitigated all thy anger: thou hast turned away from the wrath of thy indignation.


<a id="org0799ce8"></a>

## Psalms 84:5

Convert us, O God our saviour: and turn off thy anger from us.


<a id="org3fa571b"></a>

## Psalms 84:6

Wilt thou be angry with us for ever: or wilt thou extend thy wrath from generation to generation?


<a id="org6b06965"></a>

## Psalms 84:7

Thou wilt turn, O God, and bring us to life: and thy people shall rejoice in thee.


<a id="org6b62931"></a>

## Psalms 84:8

Shew us, O Lord, thy mercy; and grant us thy salvation.


<a id="orgcb69bde"></a>

## Psalms 84:9

I will hear what the Lord God will speak in me: for he will speak peace unto his people: And unto his saints: and unto them that are converted to the heart.


<a id="orgcbc92c9"></a>

## Psalms 84:10

Surely his salvation is near to them that fear him : that glory may dwell in our land.


<a id="orga3dbdff"></a>

## Psalms 84:11

Mercy and truth have met each other: justice and peace have kissed.


<a id="orgda543bc"></a>

## Psalms 84:12

Truth is sprung out of the earth: and justice hath looked down from heaven.


<a id="orgb9f1d1f"></a>

## Psalms 84:13

For the Lord will give goodness: and our earth shall yield her fruit.


<a id="orgfb5da5e"></a>

## Psalms 84:14

Justice shall walk before him: and he shall set his steps in the way. 


<a id="orgefc3bf7"></a>

# Psalms 85


<a id="orgdf3be34"></a>

## Psalms 85:1

A prayer for David himself. Incline thy ear, O Lord, and hear me: for I am needy and poor.


<a id="org0ad7418"></a>

## Psalms 85:2

Preserve my soul, for I am holy: save thy servant, O my God, that trusteth in thee.


<a id="orgc0d888e"></a>

## Psalms 85:3

Have mercy on me, O Lord, for I have cried to thee all the day.


<a id="org8d58b61"></a>

## Psalms 85:4

Give joy to the soul of thy servant, for to thee, O Lord, I have lifted up my soul.


<a id="orgfb86ec1"></a>

## Psalms 85:5

For thou, O Lord, art sweet and mild: and plenteous in mercy to all that call upon thee.


<a id="orgcd19cd3"></a>

## Psalms 85:6

Give ear, O Lord, to my prayer: and attend to the voice of my petition.


<a id="org81f96af"></a>

## Psalms 85:7

I have called upon thee in the day of my trouble: because thou hast heard me.


<a id="orgd04e0d8"></a>

## Psalms 85:8

There is none among the gods like unto thee, O Lord: and there is none according to thy works.


<a id="org6377468"></a>

## Psalms 85:9

All the nations thou hast made shall come and adore before thee, O Lord: and they shall glorify thy name.


<a id="orga7992f1"></a>

## Psalms 85:10

For thou art great and dost wonderful things: thou art God alone.


<a id="org0c3ba4b"></a>

## Psalms 85:11

Conduct me, O Lord, in thy way, and I will walk in thy truth: let my heart rejoice that it may fear thy name.


<a id="org7b6bd00"></a>

## Psalms 85:12

I will praise thee, O Lord my God, with my whole heart, and I will glorify thy name for ever:


<a id="org88a3400"></a>

## Psalms 85:13

For thy mercy is great towards me: and thou hast delivered my soul out of the lower hell.


<a id="org0b6ec09"></a>

## Psalms 85:14

O God, the wicked are risen up against me, and the assembly of the mighty have sought my soul: and they have not set thee before their eyes.


<a id="org820cca9"></a>

## Psalms 85:15

And thou, O Lord, art a God of compassion, and merciful, patient, and of much mercy, and true.


<a id="org9400910"></a>

## Psalms 85:16

O look upon me, and have mercy on me: give thy command to thy servant, and save the son of thy handmaid.


<a id="orge7a3a97"></a>

## Psalms 85:17

Shew me a token for good: that they who hate me may see, and be confounded, because thou, O Lord, hast helped me and hast comforted me. 


<a id="org813a049"></a>

# Psalms 86


<a id="orgaf154e6"></a>

## Psalms 86:1

For the sons of Core, a psalm of a canticle. The foundations thereof are the holy mountains:


<a id="org375fb02"></a>

## Psalms 86:2

The Lord loveth the gates of Sion above all the tabernacles of Jacob.


<a id="orgb2bafec"></a>

## Psalms 86:3

Glorious things are said of thee, O city of God.


<a id="orgf7d4e71"></a>

## Psalms 86:4

I will be mindful of Rahab and of Babylon knowing me. Behold the foreigners, and Tyre, and the people of the Ethiopians, these were there.


<a id="org8c1ce40"></a>

## Psalms 86:5

Shall not Sion say: This man and that man is born in her? and the Highest himself hath founded her.


<a id="org552abfb"></a>

## Psalms 86:6

The Lord shall tell in his writings of peoples and of princes, of them that have been in her.


<a id="org4412ad7"></a>

## Psalms 86:7

The dwelling in thee is as it were of all rejoicing. 


<a id="org1589a6b"></a>

# Psalms 87


<a id="orgaa42f97"></a>

## Psalms 87:1

A canticle of a psalm for the sons of Core: unto the end, for Maheleth, to answer understanding of Eman the Ezrahite.


<a id="org9231f7d"></a>

## Psalms 87:2

O Lord, the God of my salvation: I have cried in the day, and in the night before thee.


<a id="orgc27a16f"></a>

## Psalms 87:3

Let my prayer come in before thee: incline thy ear to my petition.


<a id="orgc04dc79"></a>

## Psalms 87:4

For my soul is filled with evils: and my life hath drawn nigh to hell.


<a id="org4233c24"></a>

## Psalms 87:5

I am counted among them that go down to the pit: I am become as a man without help,


<a id="orgff0e608"></a>

## Psalms 87:6

Free among the dead. Like the slain sleeping in the sepulchres, whom thou rememberest no more: and they are cut off from thy hand.


<a id="orga7b23c3"></a>

## Psalms 87:7

They have laid me in the lower pit: in the dark places, and in the shadow of death.


<a id="orgddc02fa"></a>

## Psalms 87:8

Thy wrath is strong over me: and all thy waves thou hast brought in upon me.


<a id="org6e7cad0"></a>

## Psalms 87:9

Thou hast put away my acquaintance far from me: they have set me an abomination to themselves. I was delivered up, and came not forth:


<a id="orgdc13d51"></a>

## Psalms 87:10

My eyes languished through poverty. All the day I cried to thee, O Lord: I stretched out my hands to thee.


<a id="org360372b"></a>

## Psalms 87:11

Wilt thou shew wonders to the dead? or shall physicians raise to life, and give praise to thee?


<a id="org4202bc3"></a>

## Psalms 87:12

Shall any one in the sepulchre declare thy mercy: and thy truth in destruction?


<a id="org23c7086"></a>

## Psalms 87:13

Shall thy wonders be known in the dark; and thy justice in the land of forgetfulness?


<a id="orgb5273c2"></a>

## Psalms 87:14

But I, O Lord, have cried to thee: and in the morning my prayer shall prevent thee.


<a id="org89fd941"></a>

## Psalms 87:15

Lord, why castest thou off my prayer: why turnest thou away thy face from me?


<a id="org8e09ed0"></a>

## Psalms 87:16

I am poor, and in labours from my youth: and being exalted have been humbled and troubled.


<a id="org0aaa55c"></a>

## Psalms 87:17

Thy wrath hath come upon me: and thy terrors have troubled me.


<a id="org4c4c274"></a>

## Psalms 87:18

They have come round about me like water all the day: they have compassed me about together.


<a id="orga132c87"></a>

## Psalms 87:19

Friend and neighbour thou hast put far from me: and my acquaintance, because of misery. 


<a id="orgd78a90c"></a>

# Psalms 88


<a id="org39c4ff0"></a>

## Psalms 88:1

Of understanding, for Ethan the Ezrahite.


<a id="org4a2ef4a"></a>

## Psalms 88:2

The mercies of the Lord I will sing for ever. I will shew forth thy truth with my mouth to generation and generation.


<a id="orga7bd18e"></a>

## Psalms 88:3

For thou hast said: Mercy shall be built up for ever in the heavens: thy truth shall be prepared in them.


<a id="org19dcc6c"></a>

## Psalms 88:4

I have made a covenant with my elect: I have sworn to David my servant:


<a id="org07991ab"></a>

## Psalms 88:5

Thy seed will I settle for ever. And I will build up thy throne unto generation and generation.


<a id="orgf87c3d8"></a>

## Psalms 88:6

The heavens shall confess thy wonders, O Lord: and thy truth in the church of the saints.


<a id="org6d8253a"></a>

## Psalms 88:7

For who in the clouds can be compared to the Lord: or who among the sons of God shall be like to God?


<a id="org24e31bb"></a>

## Psalms 88:8

God, who is glorified in the assembly of the saints: great and terrible above all them that are about him.


<a id="org29ae70e"></a>

## Psalms 88:9

O Lord God of hosts, who is like to thee? thou art mighty, O Lord, and thy truth is round about thee.


<a id="orgac3997f"></a>

## Psalms 88:10

Thou rulest the power of the sea: and appeasest the motion of the waves thereof.


<a id="org023f7e9"></a>

## Psalms 88:11

Thou hast humbled the proud one, as one that is slain: with the arm of thy strength thou hast scattered thy enemies.


<a id="orgb73950e"></a>

## Psalms 88:12

Thine are the heavens, and thine is the earth: the world and the fulness thereof thou hast founded:


<a id="org224a735"></a>

## Psalms 88:13

The north and the sea thou hast created. Thabor and Hermon shall rejoice in thy name:


<a id="orgd3dd3a4"></a>

## Psalms 88:14

Thy arm is with might. Let thy hand be strengthened, and thy right hand exalted:


<a id="orgdfaddab"></a>

## Psalms 88:15

Justice and judgment are the preparation of thy throne. Mercy and truth shall go before thy face:


<a id="orge24ea3f"></a>

## Psalms 88:16

Blessed is the people that knoweth jubilation. They shall walk, O Lord, in the light of thy countenance:


<a id="org0f5e2a1"></a>

## Psalms 88:17

And in thy name they shall rejoice all the day, and in thy justice they shall be exalted.


<a id="orgdbdc5cf"></a>

## Psalms 88:18

For thou art the glory of their strength: and in thy good pleasure shall our horn be exalted.


<a id="org1461f1c"></a>

## Psalms 88:19

For our protection is of the Lord, and of our king the holy one of Israel.


<a id="org295c5da"></a>

## Psalms 88:20

Then thou spokest in a vision to thy saints, and saidst: I have laid help upon one that is mighty, and have exalted one chosen out of my people.


<a id="org03c3a44"></a>

## Psalms 88:21

I have found David my servant: with my holy oil I have anointed him.


<a id="org4190ad7"></a>

## Psalms 88:22

For my hand shall help him: and my arm shall strengthen him.


<a id="org2e5e59c"></a>

## Psalms 88:23

The enemy shall have no advantage over him: nor the son of iniquity have power to hurt him.


<a id="orgfc8c0af"></a>

## Psalms 88:24

And I will cut down his enemies before his face; and them that hate him I will put to flight.


<a id="orgd43f4e9"></a>

## Psalms 88:25

And my truth and my mercy shall be with him: and in my name shall his horn be exalted.


<a id="orgf4f2fc1"></a>

## Psalms 88:26

And I will set his hand in the sea; and his right hand in the rivers.


<a id="orgeaf6427"></a>

## Psalms 88:27

He shall cry out to me: Thou art my father: my God, and the support of my salvation.


<a id="orgba0d559"></a>

## Psalms 88:28

And I will make him my firstborn, high above the kings of the earth.


<a id="org43e12ea"></a>

## Psalms 88:29

I will keep my mercy for him for ever: and my covenant faithful to him.


<a id="orgcc51d3a"></a>

## Psalms 88:30

And I will make his seed to endure for evermore: and his throne as the days of heaven.


<a id="org1c08c08"></a>

## Psalms 88:31

And if his children forsake my law, and walk not in my judgments:


<a id="orga512644"></a>

## Psalms 88:32

If they profane my justices: and keep not my commandments:


<a id="orgd1d1aef"></a>

## Psalms 88:33

I will visit their iniquities with a rod and their sins with stripes.


<a id="orgeb0b04c"></a>

## Psalms 88:34

But my mercy I will not take away from him: nor will I suffer my truth to fail.


<a id="orgdf49db7"></a>

## Psalms 88:35

Neither will I profane my covenant: and the words that proceed from my mouth I will not make void.


<a id="orgf2efd99"></a>

## Psalms 88:36

Once have I sworn by my holiness: I will not lie unto David:


<a id="orgac4d9f3"></a>

## Psalms 88:37

His seed shall endure for ever.


<a id="org69c4cc5"></a>

## Psalms 88:38

And his throne as the sun before me: and as the moon perfect for ever, and a faithful witness in heaven.


<a id="org5be49e2"></a>

## Psalms 88:39

But thou hast rejected and despised: thou hast been angry with my anointed.


<a id="orgb952df8"></a>

## Psalms 88:40

Thou hast overthrown the covenant of thy servant: thou hast profaned his sanctuary on the earth.


<a id="orgc24d5a7"></a>

## Psalms 88:41

Thou hast broken down all his hedges: thou hast made his strength fear.


<a id="org5c26a4a"></a>

## Psalms 88:42

All that pass by the way have robbed him: he is become a reproach to his neighbours.


<a id="orge015771"></a>

## Psalms 88:43

Thou hast set up the right hand of them that oppress him: thou hast made all his enemies to rejoice.


<a id="orgdada558"></a>

## Psalms 88:44

Thou hast turned away the help of his sword; and hast not assisted him in battle.


<a id="orgc33cdba"></a>

## Psalms 88:45

Thou hast made his purification to cease: and thou hast cast his throne down to the ground.


<a id="org6661f04"></a>

## Psalms 88:46

Thou hast shortened the days of his time: thou hast covered him with confusion.


<a id="orgddd4bce"></a>

## Psalms 88:47

How long, O Lord, turnest thou away unto the end? shall thy anger burn like fire?


<a id="org4c36dea"></a>

## Psalms 88:48

Remember what my substance is: for hast thou made all the children of men in vain?


<a id="org8e68170"></a>

## Psalms 88:49

Who is the man that shall live, and not see death: that shall deliver his soul from the hand of hell?


<a id="org26d098c"></a>

## Psalms 88:50

Lord, where are thy ancient mercies, according to what thou didst swear to David in thy truth?


<a id="org3323377"></a>

## Psalms 88:51

Be mindful, O Lord, of the reproach of thy servants (which I have held in my bosom) of many nations:


<a id="org15a5c98"></a>

## Psalms 88:52

Wherewith thy enemies have reproached, O Lord; wherewith they have reproached the change of thy anointed.


<a id="org388bc7d"></a>

## Psalms 88:53

Blessed be the Lord for evermore. So be it. So be it. 


<a id="org175fe64"></a>

# Psalms 89


<a id="org3abdadc"></a>

## Psalms 89:1

A prayer of Moses the man of God. Lord, thou hast been our refuge from generation to generation.


<a id="orga8418a3"></a>

## Psalms 89:2

Before the mountains were made, or the earth and the world was formed; from eternity and to eternity thou art God.


<a id="org3deb9dc"></a>

## Psalms 89:3

Turn not man away to be brought low: and thou hast said: Be converted, O ye sons of men.


<a id="orgb55cce3"></a>

## Psalms 89:4

For a thousand years in thy sight are as yesterday, which is past. And as a watch in the night,


<a id="org9a90fda"></a>

## Psalms 89:5

Things that are counted nothing, shall their years be.


<a id="orgbe1f926"></a>

## Psalms 89:6

In the morning man shall grow up like grass; in the morning he shall flourish and pass away: in the evening he shall fall, grow dry, and wither.


<a id="orgcde7b58"></a>

## Psalms 89:7

For in thy wrath we have fainted away: and are troubled in thy indignation.


<a id="org0c819d6"></a>

## Psalms 89:8

Thou hast set our iniquities before thy eyes: our life in the light of thy countenance.


<a id="org6966f2b"></a>

## Psalms 89:9

For all our days are spent; and in thy wrath we have fainted away. Our years shall be considered as a spider:


<a id="orgdc6c784"></a>

## Psalms 89:10

The days of our years in them are threescore and ten years. But if in the strong they be fourscore years: and what is more of them is labour and sorrow. For mildness is come upon us: and we shall be corrected.


<a id="orgc9f0fac"></a>

## Psalms 89:11

Who knoweth the power of thy anger, and for thy fear


<a id="org2b1df0c"></a>

## Psalms 89:12

Can number thy wrath? So make thy right hand known: and men learned in heart, in wisdom.


<a id="orgc9d9c7f"></a>

## Psalms 89:13

Return, O Lord, how long? and be entreated in favour of thy servants.


<a id="org314b2c0"></a>

## Psalms 89:14

We are filled in the morning with thy mercy: and we have rejoiced, and are delighted all our days.


<a id="orgecaec81"></a>

## Psalms 89:15

We have rejoiced for the days in which thou hast humbled us: for the years in which we have seen evils.


<a id="orge646712"></a>

## Psalms 89:16

Look upon thy servants and upon their works: and direct their children.


<a id="orgb77b213"></a>

## Psalms 89:17

And let the brightness of the Lord our God be upon us: and direct thou the works of our hands over us; yea, the work of our hands do thou direct. 


<a id="orgb1837a9"></a>

# Psalms 90


<a id="orgdaa9039"></a>

## Psalms 90:1

The praise of a canticle for David. He that dwelleth in the aid of the most High, shall abide under the protection of the God of Jacob.


<a id="org6269018"></a>

## Psalms 90:2

He shall say to the Lord: Thou art my protector, and my refuge: my God, in him will I trust.


<a id="org08b48a9"></a>

## Psalms 90:3

For he hath delivered me from the snare of the hunters: and from the sharp word.


<a id="org048a82a"></a>

## Psalms 90:4

He will overshadow thee with his shoulders: and under his wings thou shalt trust.


<a id="org6c207c1"></a>

## Psalms 90:5

His truth shall compass thee with a shield: thou shalt not be afraid of the terror of the night.


<a id="orged84f87"></a>

## Psalms 90:6

Of the arrow that flieth in the day, of the business that walketh about in the dark: of invasion, or of the noonday devil.


<a id="orgf9d40ed"></a>

## Psalms 90:7

A thousand shall fall at thy side, and ten thousand at thy right hand: but it shall not come nigh thee.


<a id="orgb57fdee"></a>

## Psalms 90:8

But thou shalt consider with thy eyes: and shalt see the reward of the wicked.


<a id="orgfe2460b"></a>

## Psalms 90:9

Because thou, O Lord, art my hope: thou hast made the most High thy refuge.


<a id="org994c9d6"></a>

## Psalms 90:10

There shall no evil come to thee: nor shall the scourge come near thy dwelling.


<a id="org99812de"></a>

## Psalms 90:11

For he hath given his angels charge over thee; to keep thee in all thy ways.


<a id="orgda30987"></a>

## Psalms 90:12

In their hands they shall bear thee up: lest thou dash thy foot against a stone.


<a id="org2ecccf5"></a>

## Psalms 90:13

Thou shalt walk upon the asp and the basilisk: and thou shalt trample under foot the lion and the dragon.


<a id="orgc661e15"></a>

## Psalms 90:14

Because he hoped in me I will deliver him: I will protect him because he hath known my name.


<a id="org723e902"></a>

## Psalms 90:15

He shall cry to me, and I will hear him: I am with him in tribulation, I will deliver him, and I will glorify him.


<a id="org7dd48d9"></a>

## Psalms 90:16

I will fill him with length of days; and I will shew him my salvation. 


<a id="orgd8d50cb"></a>

# Psalms 91


<a id="org5b58ec5"></a>

## Psalms 91:1

A psalm of a canticle on the sabbath day.


<a id="org66367b3"></a>

## Psalms 91:2

It is good to give praise to the Lord: and to sing to thy name, O most High.


<a id="org09d8b62"></a>

## Psalms 91:3

To shew forth thy mercy in the morning, and thy truth in the night:


<a id="org3dbaf41"></a>

## Psalms 91:4

Upon an instrument of ten strings, upon the psaltery: with a canticle upon the harp.


<a id="org037d7eb"></a>

## Psalms 91:5

For thou hast given me, O Lord, a delight in thy doings: and in the works of thy hands I shall rejoice.


<a id="orgb5bd3eb"></a>

## Psalms 91:6

O Lord, how great are thy works! thy thoughts are exceeding deep.


<a id="orgbf92af3"></a>

## Psalms 91:7

The senseless man shall not know: nor will the fool understand these things.


<a id="org5c5fc98"></a>

## Psalms 91:8

When the wicked shall spring up as grass: and all the workers of iniquity shall appear: That they may perish for ever and ever:


<a id="org9acc973"></a>

## Psalms 91:9

But thou, O Lord, art most high for evermore.


<a id="orgb942813"></a>

## Psalms 91:10

For behold thy enemies, O Lord, for behold thy enemies shall perish: and all the workers of iniquity shall be scattered.


<a id="orgd6a2ffc"></a>

## Psalms 91:11

But my horn shall be exalted like that of the unicorn: and my old age in plentiful mercy.


<a id="org9cffaff"></a>

## Psalms 91:12

My eye also hath looked down upon my enemies: and my ear shall hear of the downfall of the malignant that rise up against me.


<a id="org6820e45"></a>

## Psalms 91:13

The just shall flourish like the palm tree: he shall grow up like the cedar of Libanus.


<a id="org2cd4036"></a>

## Psalms 91:14

They that are planted in the house of the Lord shall flourish in the courts of the house of our God.


<a id="org41d6c92"></a>

## Psalms 91:15

They shall still increase in a fruitful old age: and shall be well treated,


<a id="org37de2b9"></a>

## Psalms 91:16

That they may shew, That the Lord our God is righteous, and there is no iniquity in him. 


<a id="orgb9b8759"></a>

# Psalms 92


<a id="org73e7931"></a>

## Psalms 92:1

The Lord hath reigned, he is clothed with beauty: the Lord is clothed with strength, and hath girded himself. For he hath established the world which shall not be moved.


<a id="org3a6e48b"></a>

## Psalms 92:2

My throne is prepared from of old: thou art from everlasting.


<a id="orga6e6581"></a>

## Psalms 92:3

The floods have lifted up, O Lord: the floods have lifted up their voice. The floods have lifted up their waves,


<a id="orgf443786"></a>

## Psalms 92:4

With the noise of many waters. Wonderful are the surges of the sea: wonderful is the Lord on high.


<a id="orgf114696"></a>

## Psalms 92:5

Thy testimonies are become exceedingly credible: holiness becometh thy house, O Lord, unto length of days. 


<a id="org03d5a38"></a>

# Psalms 93


<a id="orge22c03a"></a>

## Psalms 93:1

The Lord is the God to whom revenge belongeth: the God of revenge hath acted freely.


<a id="orgd6013c8"></a>

## Psalms 93:2

Lift up thyself, thou that judgest the earth: render a reward to the proud.


<a id="orga40700b"></a>

## Psalms 93:3

How long shall sinners, O Lord: how long shall sinners glory?


<a id="org8afec1a"></a>

## Psalms 93:4

Shall they utter, and speak iniquity: shall all speak who work injustice?


<a id="org31e150f"></a>

## Psalms 93:5

Thy people, O Lord, they have brought low: and they have afflicted thy inheritance.


<a id="org6917c5f"></a>

## Psalms 93:6

They have slain the widow and the stranger: and they have murdered the fatherless.


<a id="org9641866"></a>

## Psalms 93:7

And they have said: The Lord shall not see: neither shall the God of Jacob understand.


<a id="orgbd4e7b9"></a>

## Psalms 93:8

Understand, ye senseless among the people: and, you fools, be wise at last.


<a id="org6fd16ff"></a>

## Psalms 93:9

He that planted the ear, shall he not hear? or he that formed the eye, doth he not consider?


<a id="orgc90ea0c"></a>

## Psalms 93:10

He that chastiseth nations, shall he not rebuke: he that teacheth man knowledge?


<a id="org31b468e"></a>

## Psalms 93:11

The Lord knoweth the thoughts of men, that they are vain.


<a id="orga1fb1c8"></a>

## Psalms 93:12

Blessed is the man whom thou shalt instruct, O Lord: and shalt teach him out of thy law.


<a id="org086f452"></a>

## Psalms 93:13

That thou mayst give him rest from the evil days: till a pit be dug for the wicked.


<a id="org947727f"></a>

## Psalms 93:14

For the Lord will not cast off his people: neither will he forsake his own inheritance.


<a id="orge1853b4"></a>

## Psalms 93:15

Until justice be turned into judgment: and they that are near it are all the upright in heart.


<a id="org26d9ef2"></a>

## Psalms 93:16

Who shall rise up for me against the evildoers? or who shall stand with me against the workers of iniquity?


<a id="org7ce61b1"></a>

## Psalms 93:17

Unless the Lord had been my helper, my soul had almost dwelt in hell.


<a id="org5aa5655"></a>

## Psalms 93:18

If I said: My foot is moved: thy mercy, O Lord, assisted me.


<a id="org1c798a2"></a>

## Psalms 93:19

According to the multitude of my sorrows in my heart, thy comforts have given joy to my soul.


<a id="org90bb809"></a>

## Psalms 93:20

Doth the seat of iniquity stick to thee, who framest labour in commandment?


<a id="org0623c4d"></a>

## Psalms 93:21

They will hunt after the soul of the just, and will condemn innocent blood.


<a id="orgc64c6b7"></a>

## Psalms 93:22

But the Lord is my refuge: and my God the help of my hope.


<a id="orgeecbd06"></a>

## Psalms 93:23

And he will render them their iniquity : and in their malice he will destroy them: the Lord our God will destroy them. 


<a id="orgc494390"></a>

# Psalms 94


<a id="org58a5607"></a>

## Psalms 94:1

Come let us praise the Lord with joy: let us joyfully sing to God our saviour.


<a id="orga2d91a4"></a>

## Psalms 94:2

Let us come before his presence with thanksgiving; and make a joyful noise to him with psalms.


<a id="orgfb3d3ea"></a>

## Psalms 94:3

For the Lord is a great God, and a great King above all gods.


<a id="orgabd9c91"></a>

## Psalms 94:4

For in his hand are all the ends of the earth: and the heights of the mountains are his.


<a id="orgfad3db5"></a>

## Psalms 94:5

For the sea is his, and he made it: and his hands formed the dry land.


<a id="org897778b"></a>

## Psalms 94:6

Come let us adore and fall down: and weep before the Lord that made us.


<a id="org3d092fc"></a>

## Psalms 94:7

For he is the Lord our God: and we are the people of his pasture and the sheep of his hand.


<a id="orgd8ed677"></a>

## Psalms 94:8

To day if you shall hear his voice, harden not your hearts:


<a id="org140226e"></a>

## Psalms 94:9

As in the provocation, according to the day of temptation in the wilderness: where your fathers tempted me, they proved me, and saw my works.


<a id="org174216f"></a>

## Psalms 94:10

Forty years long was I offended with that generation, and I said: These always err in heart.


<a id="org46316e2"></a>

## Psalms 94:11

And these men have not known my ways: so I swore in my wrath that they shall not enter into my rest. 


<a id="orgbd0bb60"></a>

# Psalms 95


<a id="orgcac971b"></a>

## Psalms 95:1

A canticle for David himself, when the house was built after the captivity. Sing ye to the Lord a new canticle: sing to the Lord, all the earth.


<a id="orgc877d79"></a>

## Psalms 95:2

Sing ye to the Lord and bless his name: shew forth his salvation from day to day.


<a id="org947be90"></a>

## Psalms 95:3

Declare his glory among the Gentiles: his wonders among all people.


<a id="orgdb0faa9"></a>

## Psalms 95:4

For the Lord is great, and exceedingly to be praised: he is to be feared above all gods.


<a id="orgf3912ae"></a>

## Psalms 95:5

For all the gods of the Gentiles are devils: but the Lord made the heavens.


<a id="org77fd111"></a>

## Psalms 95:6

Praise and beauty are before him: holiness and majesty in his sanctuary.


<a id="orgd92c40f"></a>

## Psalms 95:7

Bring ye to the Lord, O ye kindreds of the Gentiles, bring ye to the Lord glory and honour:


<a id="orga4d7f13"></a>

## Psalms 95:8

Bring to the Lord glory unto his name. Bring up sacrifices, and come into his courts:


<a id="org36a6823"></a>

## Psalms 95:9

Adore ye the Lord in his holy court. Let all the earth be moved at his presence.


<a id="orgcb04ac4"></a>

## Psalms 95:10

Say ye among the Gentiles, the Lord hath reigned. For he hath corrected the world, which shall not be moved: he will judge the people with justice.


<a id="orgb8c8ef6"></a>

## Psalms 95:11

Let the heavens rejoice, and let the earth be glad, let the sea be moved, and the fulness thereof:


<a id="org2479a58"></a>

## Psalms 95:12

The fields and all things that are in them shall be joyful. Then shall all the trees of the woods rejoice


<a id="orgf41a82b"></a>

## Psalms 95:13

before the face of the Lord, because he cometh: because he cometh to judge the earth. He shall judge the world with justice, and the people with his truth. 


<a id="orgdc4b3a4"></a>

# Psalms 96


<a id="orgf65d08c"></a>

## Psalms 96:1

For the same David, when his land was restored again to him. The Lord hath reigned, let the earth rejoice: let many islands be glad.


<a id="orgda732a5"></a>

## Psalms 96:2

Clouds and darkness are round about him: justice and judgment are the establishment of his throne.


<a id="orgb26f66c"></a>

## Psalms 96:3

A fire shall go before him, and shall burn his enemies round about.


<a id="org6d117a9"></a>

## Psalms 96:4

His lightnings have shone forth to the world: the earth saw and trembled.


<a id="org2b4e7ee"></a>

## Psalms 96:5

The mountains melted like wax, at the presence of the Lord: at the presence of the Lord of all the earth.


<a id="orgf3d1db7"></a>

## Psalms 96:6

The heavens declared his justice: and all people saw his glory.


<a id="orgdb6b525"></a>

## Psalms 96:7

Let them be all confounded that adore graven things, and that glory in their idols. Adore him, all you his angels:


<a id="org97a1150"></a>

## Psalms 96:8

Sion heard, and was glad. And the daughters of Juda rejoiced, because of thy judgments, O Lord.


<a id="orgb642f7c"></a>

## Psalms 96:9

For thou art the most high Lord over all the earth: thou art exalted exceedingly above all gods.


<a id="org613338f"></a>

## Psalms 96:10

You that love the Lord, hate evil: the Lord preserveth the souls of his saints, he will deliver them out of the hand of the sinner.


<a id="orgcf7f54c"></a>

## Psalms 96:11

Light is risen to the just, and joy to the right of heart.


<a id="orge6062da"></a>

## Psalms 96:12

Rejoice, ye just, in the Lord: and give praise to the remembrance of his holiness. 


<a id="orgac6e79d"></a>

# Psalms 97


<a id="org34e71d5"></a>

## Psalms 97:1

A psalm for David himself. Sing ye to the Lord a new canticle: because he hath done wonderful things. His right hand hath wrought for him salvation, and his arm is holy.


<a id="orga6df625"></a>

## Psalms 97:2

The Lord hath made known his salvation: he hath revealed his justice in the sight of the Gentiles.


<a id="org6be78cd"></a>

## Psalms 97:3

He hath remembered his mercy and his truth toward the house of Israel. All the ends of the earth have seen the salvation of our God.


<a id="orga2647a2"></a>

## Psalms 97:4

Sing joyfully to God, all the earth; make melody, rejoice and sing.


<a id="org808060c"></a>

## Psalms 97:5

Sing praise to the Lord on the harp, on the harp, and with the voice of a psalm:


<a id="org2a959fb"></a>

## Psalms 97:6

With long trumpets, and sound of cornet. Make a joyful noise before the Lord our king:


<a id="orgcbb5caa"></a>

## Psalms 97:7

Let the sea be moved and the fullness thereof: the world and they that dwell therein.


<a id="org36e8956"></a>

## Psalms 97:8

The rivers shall clap their hands, the mountains shall rejoice together


<a id="org8ab6b2c"></a>

## Psalms 97:9

At the presence of the Lord: because he cometh to judge the earth. He shall judge the world with justice, and the people with equity. 


<a id="orgfaafe93"></a>

# Psalms 98


<a id="orgd2c1d2b"></a>

## Psalms 98:1

A psalm for David himself. The Lord hath reigned, let the people be angry: he that sitteth on the cherubims: let the earth be moved.


<a id="orgc19ef95"></a>

## Psalms 98:2

The Lord is great in Sion, and high above all people.


<a id="orgeb8ccae"></a>

## Psalms 98:3

Let them give praise to thy great name: for it is terrible and holy:


<a id="orgda20693"></a>

## Psalms 98:4

And the king&rsquo;s honour loveth judgment. Thou hast prepared directions: thou hast done judgment and justice in Jacob.


<a id="org7bec8c6"></a>

## Psalms 98:5

Exalt ye the Lord our God, and adore his footstool, for it is holy.


<a id="orgbf52d79"></a>

## Psalms 98:6

Moses and Aaron among his priests: and Samuel among them that call upon his name. They called upon the Lord, and he heard them:


<a id="org0dc086d"></a>

## Psalms 98:7

He spoke to them in the pillar of the cloud. They kept his testimonies, and the commandment which he gave them.


<a id="org0f15056"></a>

## Psalms 98:8

Thou didst hear them, O Lord our God: thou wast a merciful God to them, and taking vengeance on all their inventions.


<a id="orge87e05d"></a>

## Psalms 98:9

Exalt ye the Lord our God, and adore at his holy mountain: for the Lord our God is holy. 


<a id="org787404d"></a>

# Psalms 99


<a id="orgf82c566"></a>

## Psalms 99:1

A psalm of praise.


<a id="org06a55e6"></a>

## Psalms 99:2

Sing joyfully to God, all the earth: serve ye the Lord with gladness. Come in before his presence with exceeding great joy.


<a id="org70d2aaf"></a>

## Psalms 99:3

Know ye that the Lord he is God: he made us, and not we ourselves. We are his people and the sheep of his pasture.


<a id="org6a36184"></a>

## Psalms 99:4

Go ye into his gates with praise, into his courts with hymns: and give glory to him. Praise ye his name:


<a id="org329f89f"></a>

## Psalms 99:5

For the Lord is sweet, his mercy endureth for ever, and his truth to generation and generation. 


<a id="org0d49f84"></a>

# Psalms 100


<a id="org61801da"></a>

## Psalms 100:1

A psalm for David himself. Mercy and judgment I will sing to thee, O Lord: I will sing,


<a id="org101e276"></a>

## Psalms 100:2

And I will understand in the unspotted way, when thou shalt come to me. I walked in the innocence of my heart, in the midst of my house.


<a id="org7e33ed1"></a>

## Psalms 100:3

I will not set before my eyes any unjust thing: I hated the workers of iniquities.


<a id="org958fe96"></a>

## Psalms 100:4

The perverse heart did not cleave to me: and the malignant, that turned aside from me, I would not know.


<a id="org0082fa7"></a>

## Psalms 100:5

The man that in private detracted his neighbour, him did I persecute. With him that had a proud eye, and an unsatiable heart, I would not eat.


<a id="orgbf42895"></a>

## Psalms 100:6

My eyes were upon the faithful of the earth, to sit with me: the man that walked in the perfect way, he served me.


<a id="org4e8126b"></a>

## Psalms 100:7

He that worketh pride shall not dwell in the midst of my house: he that speaketh unjust things did not prosper before my eyes.


<a id="org10a1082"></a>

## Psalms 100:8

In the morning I put to death all the wicked of the land: that I might cut off all the workers of iniquity from the city of the Lord. 


<a id="org5c6e202"></a>

# Psalms 101


<a id="orgbee4ce1"></a>

## Psalms 101:1

The prayer of the poor man, when he was anxious, and poured out his supplication before the Lord.


<a id="org6e00d34"></a>

## Psalms 101:2

Hear, O Lord, my prayer: and let my cry come to thee.


<a id="org2f43121"></a>

## Psalms 101:3

Turn not away thy face from me: in the day when I am in trouble, incline thy ear to me. In what day soever I shall call upon thee, hear me speedily.


<a id="orga606f21"></a>

## Psalms 101:4

For my days are vanished like smoke, and my bones are grown dry like fuel for the fire.


<a id="orgf0f7316"></a>

## Psalms 101:5

I am smitten as grass, and my heart is withered: because I forgot to eat my bread.


<a id="org45451b6"></a>

## Psalms 101:6

Through the voice of my groaning, my bone hath cleaved to my flesh.


<a id="org10d45a1"></a>

## Psalms 101:7

I am become like to a pelican of the wilderness: I am like a night raven in the house.


<a id="org2024f52"></a>

## Psalms 101:8

I have watched, and am become as a sparrow all alone on the housetop.


<a id="org3a49e62"></a>

## Psalms 101:9

All the day long my enemies reproached me: and they that praised me did swear against me.


<a id="org8aa038f"></a>

## Psalms 101:10

For I did eat ashes like bread, and mingled my drink with weeping.


<a id="org973d5d2"></a>

## Psalms 101:11

Because of thy anger and indignation: for having lifted me up thou hast thrown me down.


<a id="org32ec9b7"></a>

## Psalms 101:12

My days have declined like a shadow, and I am withered like grass.


<a id="orgb623d0f"></a>

## Psalms 101:13

But thou, O Lord, endurest for ever: and thy memorial to all generations.


<a id="org97ad4ad"></a>

## Psalms 101:14

Thou shalt arise and have mercy on Sion: for it is time to have mercy on it, for the time is come.


<a id="org713c43b"></a>

## Psalms 101:15

For the stones thereof have pleased thy servants: and they shall have pity on the earth thereof.


<a id="org6c8e79a"></a>

## Psalms 101:16

All the Gentiles shall fear thy name, O Lord, and all the kings of the earth thy glory.


<a id="org703af82"></a>

## Psalms 101:17

For the Lord hath built up Sion: and he shall be seen in his glory.


<a id="orgaf4b812"></a>

## Psalms 101:18

He hath had regard to the prayer of the humble: and he hath not despised their petition.


<a id="org80587f3"></a>

## Psalms 101:19

Let these things be written unto another generation: and the people that shall be created shall praise the Lord:


<a id="org4496144"></a>

## Psalms 101:20

Because he hath looked forth from his high sanctuary: from heaven the Lord hath looked upon the earth.


<a id="org7b45621"></a>

## Psalms 101:21

That he might hear the groans of them that are in fetters: that he might release the children of the slain:


<a id="org19cf779"></a>

## Psalms 101:22

That they may declare the name of the Lord in Sion: and his praise in Jerusalem;


<a id="orga5883d8"></a>

## Psalms 101:23

When the people assemble together, and kings, to serve the Lord.


<a id="org2a51711"></a>

## Psalms 101:24

He answered him in the way of his strength: Declare unto me the fewness of my days.


<a id="org9eed5f6"></a>

## Psalms 101:25

Call me not away in the midst of my days: thy years are unto generation and generation.


<a id="org8490ff1"></a>

## Psalms 101:26

In the beginning, O Lord, thou foundedst the earth: and the heavens are the works of thy hands.


<a id="org3916d9f"></a>

## Psalms 101:27

They shall perish but thou remainest: and all of them shall grow old like a garment: And as a vesture thou shalt change them, and they shall be changed.


<a id="org0da5146"></a>

## Psalms 101:28

But thou art always the selfsame, and thy years shall not fail.


<a id="orgaffd893"></a>

## Psalms 101:29
