The children of thy servants shall continue and their seed shall be directed for ever. 


<a id="org85f9bce"></a>

# Psalms 102


<a id="org0bd12f0"></a>

## Psalms 102:1

For David himself. Bless the Lord, O my soul: and let all that is within me bless his holy name.


<a id="org5e80404"></a>

## Psalms 102:2

Bless the Lord, O my soul, and never forget all he hath done for thee.


<a id="orga2fae7e"></a>

## Psalms 102:3

Who forgiveth all thy iniquities: who healeth all thy diseases.


<a id="org8da0bd4"></a>

## Psalms 102:4

Who redeemeth thy life from destruction: who crowneth thee with mercy and compassion.


<a id="org3a3e959"></a>

## Psalms 102:5

Who satisfieth thy desire with good things: thy youth shall be renewed like the eagle&rsquo;s.


<a id="org92c8a8d"></a>

## Psalms 102:6

The Lord doth mercies, and judgment for all that suffer wrong.


<a id="org7bca8c1"></a>

## Psalms 102:7

He hath made his ways known to Moses: his wills to the children of Israel.


<a id="org1fd80bb"></a>

## Psalms 102:8

The Lord is compassionate and merciful: longsuffering and plenteous in mercy.


<a id="orga7cf513"></a>

## Psalms 102:9

He will not always be angry: nor will he threaten for ever.


<a id="org3c859f7"></a>

## Psalms 102:10

He hath not dealt with us according to our sins: nor rewarded us according to our iniquities.


<a id="orgbf7ae71"></a>

## Psalms 102:11

For according to the height of the heaven above the earth: he hath strengthened his mercy towards them that fear him.


<a id="org2186cff"></a>

## Psalms 102:12

As far as the east is from the west, so far hath he removed our iniquities from us.


<a id="org05c8722"></a>

## Psalms 102:13

As a father hath compassion on his children, so hath the Lord compassion on them that fear him:


<a id="org8b70c6a"></a>

## Psalms 102:14

For he knoweth our frame. He remembereth that we are dust:


<a id="orga85c080"></a>

## Psalms 102:15

Man&rsquo;s days are as grass, as the flower of the field so shall he flourish.


<a id="org80b7e08"></a>

## Psalms 102:16

For the spirit shall pass in him, and he shall not be: and he shall know his place no more.


<a id="org3ddfe60"></a>

## Psalms 102:17

But the mercy of the Lord is from eternity and unto eternity upon them that fear him: And his justice unto children&rsquo;s children,


<a id="orgda849e4"></a>

## Psalms 102:18

To such as keep his covenant, And are mindful of his commandments to do them.


<a id="org8ccca00"></a>

## Psalms 102:19

The Lord hath prepared his throne in heaven: and his kingdom shall rule over all.


<a id="orgf81168a"></a>

## Psalms 102:20

Bless the Lord, all ye his angels: you that are mighty in strength, and execute his word, hearkening to the voice of his orders.


<a id="org6c5faf9"></a>

## Psalms 102:21

Bless the Lord, all ye his hosts: you ministers of his that do his will.


<a id="org89f3677"></a>

## Psalms 102:22

Bless the Lord, all his works: in every place of his dominion, O my soul, bless thou the Lord. 


<a id="orgd750c9e"></a>

# Psalms 103


<a id="org2e57e01"></a>

## Psalms 103:1

For David himself. Bless the Lord, O my soul: O Lord my God, thou art exceedingly great. Thou hast put on praise and beauty:


<a id="org9c74a11"></a>

## Psalms 103:2

And art clothed with light as with a garment. Who stretchest out the heaven like a pavilion:


<a id="orgd414fce"></a>

## Psalms 103:3

Who coverest the higher rooms thereof with water. Who makest the clouds thy chariot: who walkest upon the wings of the winds.


<a id="org7adc237"></a>

## Psalms 103:4

Who makest thy angels spirits: and thy ministers a burning fire.


<a id="org106aafa"></a>

## Psalms 103:5

Who hast founded the earth upon its own bases: it shall not be moved for ever and ever.


<a id="org82bfb55"></a>

## Psalms 103:6

The deep like a garment is its clothing: above the mountains shall the waters stand.


<a id="org7ed0c40"></a>

## Psalms 103:7

At thy rebuke they shall flee: at the voice of thy thunder they shall fear.


<a id="org5fd3328"></a>

## Psalms 103:8

The mountains ascend, and the plains descend into the place which thou hast founded for them.


<a id="org7baef46"></a>

## Psalms 103:9

Thou hast set a bound which they shall not pass over; neither shall they return to cover the earth.


<a id="orgdc3e4b2"></a>

## Psalms 103:10

Thou sendest forth springs in the vales: between the midst of the hills the waters shall pass.


<a id="org96d9194"></a>

## Psalms 103:11

All the beasts of the field shall drink: the wild asses shall expect in their thirst.


<a id="org79016ce"></a>

## Psalms 103:12

Over them the birds of the air shall dwell: from the midst of the rocks they shall give forth their voices.


<a id="orgbd84129"></a>

## Psalms 103:13

Thou waterest the hills from thy upper rooms: the earth shall be filled with the fruit of thy works:


<a id="orgf490a14"></a>

## Psalms 103:14

Bringing forth grass for cattle, and herb for the service of men. That thou mayst bring bread out of the earth:


<a id="org9fe392c"></a>

## Psalms 103:15

And that wine may cheer the heart of man. That he may make the face cheerful with oil: and that bread may strengthen man&rsquo;s heart.


<a id="orgbe17466"></a>

## Psalms 103:16

The trees of the field shall be filled, and the cedars of Libanus which he hath planted:


<a id="org86ca298"></a>

## Psalms 103:17

There the sparrows shall make their nests. The highest of them is the house of the heron.


<a id="org8281c27"></a>

## Psalms 103:18

The high hills are a refuge for the harts, the rock for the irchins.


<a id="org3066bbf"></a>

## Psalms 103:19

He hath made the moon for seasons: the sun knoweth his going down.


<a id="org576f58a"></a>

## Psalms 103:20

Thou hast appointed darkness, and it is night: in it shall all the beasts of the woods go about:


<a id="org2840d6a"></a>

## Psalms 103:21

The young lions roaring after their prey, and seeking their meat from God.


<a id="org9bbfcde"></a>

## Psalms 103:22

The sun ariseth, and they are gathered together: and they shall lie down in their dens.


<a id="org5e71a9e"></a>

## Psalms 103:23

Man shall go forth to his work, and to his labour until the evening.


<a id="orgac938e1"></a>

## Psalms 103:24

How great are thy works, O Lord ? thou hast made all things in wisdom: the earth is filled with thy riches.


<a id="org5d97b03"></a>

## Psalms 103:25

So is this great sea, which stretcheth wide its arms: there are creeping things without number: Creatures little and great.


<a id="org8ba2d23"></a>

## Psalms 103:26

There the ships shall go. This sea dragon which thou hast formed to play therein.


<a id="orgf0a0a05"></a>

## Psalms 103:27

All expect of thee that thou give them food in season.


<a id="org8913fb6"></a>

## Psalms 103:28

What thou givest to them they shall gather up: when thou openest thy hand, they shall all be filled with good.


<a id="org9f906b4"></a>

## Psalms 103:29

But if thou turnest away thy face, they shall be troubled: thou shalt take away their breath, and they shall fail, and shall return to their dust.


<a id="orgc707661"></a>

## Psalms 103:30

Thou shalt send forth thy spirit, and they shall be created: and thou shalt renew the face of the earth.


<a id="orgd1787ce"></a>

## Psalms 103:31

May the glory of the Lord endure for ever: the Lord shall rejoice in his works.


<a id="org8f0eaf7"></a>

## Psalms 103:32

He looketh upon the earth, and maketh it tremble: he troubleth the mountains, and they smoke.


<a id="orga15105b"></a>

## Psalms 103:33

I will sing to the Lord as long as I live: I will sing praise to my God while I have my being.


<a id="org3e5bd30"></a>

## Psalms 103:34

Let my speech be acceptable to him: but I will take delight in the Lord.


<a id="org5041590"></a>

## Psalms 103:35

Let sinners be consumed out of the earth, and the unjust, so that they be no more: O my soul, bless thou the Lord. 


<a id="org14d9973"></a>

# Psalms 104


<a id="org5fb8571"></a>

## Psalms 104:1

Give glory to the Lord, and call upon his name: declare his deeds among the Gentiles.


<a id="org2d1528f"></a>

## Psalms 104:2

Sing to him, yea sing praises to him: relate all his wondrous works.


<a id="org3ff550a"></a>

## Psalms 104:3

Glory ye in his holy name: let the heart of them rejoice that seek the Lord.


<a id="org1d2b37e"></a>

## Psalms 104:4

Seek ye the Lord, and be strengthened: seek his face evermore.


<a id="org68e2dae"></a>

## Psalms 104:5

Remember his marvellous works which he hath done; his wonders, and the judgments of his mouth.


<a id="org12531f4"></a>

## Psalms 104:6

O ye seed of Abraham his servant; ye sons of Jacob his chosen.


<a id="org3b696d1"></a>

## Psalms 104:7

He is the Lord our God: his judgments are in all the earth.


<a id="orgc4aaad3"></a>

## Psalms 104:8

He hath remembered his covenant for ever: the word which he commanded to a thousand generations.


<a id="org13a4f6c"></a>

## Psalms 104:9

Which he made to Abraham; and his oath to Isaac:


<a id="org9b989a2"></a>

## Psalms 104:10

And he appointed the same to Jacob for a law, and to Israel for an everlasting testament:


<a id="orgd0d3ab1"></a>

## Psalms 104:11

Saying: To thee will I give the land of Chanaan, the lot of your inheritance.


<a id="org54862c8"></a>

## Psalms 104:12

When they were but a small number: yea very few, and sojourners therein:


<a id="org0137a75"></a>

## Psalms 104:13

And they passed from nation to nation, and from one kingdom to another people.


<a id="org07b7cbe"></a>

## Psalms 104:14

He suffered no man to hurt them: and he reproved kings for their sakes.


<a id="org22ccca0"></a>

## Psalms 104:15

Touch ye not my anointed: and do no evil to my prophets.


<a id="orgce513cc"></a>

## Psalms 104:16

And he called a famine upon the land: and he broke in pieces all the support of bread.


<a id="org3d599d9"></a>

## Psalms 104:17

He sent a man before them: Joseph, who was sold for a slave.


<a id="orgd23f111"></a>

## Psalms 104:18

They humbled his feet in fetters: the iron pierced his soul,


<a id="org25e94d7"></a>

## Psalms 104:19

Until his word came. The word of the Lord inflamed him.


<a id="orgdcc345d"></a>

## Psalms 104:20

The king sent, and he released him: the ruler of the people, and he set him at liberty.


<a id="org014bdbc"></a>

## Psalms 104:21

He made him master of his house, and ruler of all his possession.


<a id="org44d70e0"></a>

## Psalms 104:22

That he might instruct his princes as himself, and teach his ancients wisdom.


<a id="orgd137f83"></a>

## Psalms 104:23

And Israel went into Egypt: and Jacob was a sojourner in the land of Cham.


<a id="org967fcc2"></a>

## Psalms 104:24

And he increased his people exceedingly: and strengthened them over their enemies.


<a id="org3c35b3d"></a>

## Psalms 104:25

He turned their heart to hate his people: and to deal deceitfully with his servants.


<a id="orge2a1498"></a>

## Psalms 104:26

He sent Moses his servant: Aaron the man whom he had chosen.


<a id="org001f575"></a>

## Psalms 104:27

He gave them power to shew them signs, and his wonders in the land of Cham.


<a id="org3c62891"></a>

## Psalms 104:28

He sent darkness, and made it obscure: and grieved not his words.


<a id="orga8a6bda"></a>

## Psalms 104:29

He turned their waters into blood, and destroyed their fish.


<a id="org5397f62"></a>

## Psalms 104:30

Their land brought forth frogs, in the inner chambers of their kings.


<a id="orgd831ff3"></a>

## Psalms 104:31

He spoke, and there came divers sorts of flies and sciniphs in all their coasts.


<a id="org069378d"></a>

## Psalms 104:32

He gave them hail for rain, a burning fire in the land.


<a id="org21e055d"></a>

## Psalms 104:33

And he destroyed their vineyards and their fig trees: and he broke in pieces the trees of their coasts.


<a id="org5877ec6"></a>

## Psalms 104:34

He spoke, and the locust came, and the bruchus, of which there was no number.


<a id="orgd2f0a11"></a>

## Psalms 104:35

And they devoured all the grass in their land, and consumed all the fruit of their ground.


<a id="org42d01ff"></a>

## Psalms 104:36

And he slew all the firstborn in their land: the firstfruits of all their labour.


<a id="org32cade4"></a>

## Psalms 104:37

And he brought them out with silver and gold: and there was not among their tribes one that was feeble.


<a id="orgd8b68b8"></a>

## Psalms 104:38

Egypt was glad when they departed: for the fear of them lay upon them.


<a id="org0cd46ed"></a>

## Psalms 104:39

He spread a cloud for their protection, and fire to give them light in the night.


<a id="org4dbf214"></a>

## Psalms 104:40

They asked, and the quail came: and he filled them with the bread of heaven.


<a id="orgd7dff57"></a>

## Psalms 104:41

He opened the rock, and waters flowed: rivers ran down in the dry land.


<a id="org9443282"></a>

## Psalms 104:42

Because he remembered his holy word, which he had spoken to his servant Abraham.


<a id="org4cd8904"></a>

## Psalms 104:43

And he brought forth his people with joy, and his chosen with gladness.


<a id="orgd611ae7"></a>

## Psalms 104:44

And he gave them the lands of the Gentiles: and they possessed the labours of the people:


<a id="org8e3e45e"></a>

## Psalms 104:45

That they might observe his justifications, and seek after his law. 


<a id="orga9ffd27"></a>

# Psalms 105


<a id="orgad6f610"></a>

## Psalms 105:1

Give glory to the Lord, for he is good: for his mercy endureth for ever.


<a id="org618ac3b"></a>

## Psalms 105:2

Who shall declare the powers of the Lord? who shall set forth all his praises?


<a id="orgce9b4f9"></a>

## Psalms 105:3

Blessed are they that keep judgment, and do justice at all times.


<a id="org4fc592f"></a>

## Psalms 105:4

Remember us, O Lord, in the favour of thy people: visit us with thy salvation.


<a id="orgfdac68b"></a>

## Psalms 105:5

That we may see the good of thy chosen, that we may rejoice in the joy of thy nation: that thou mayst be praised with thy inheritance.


<a id="orgaa304f4"></a>

## Psalms 105:6

We have sinned with our fathers: we have acted unjustly, we have wrought iniquity.


<a id="org0e69cec"></a>

## Psalms 105:7

Our fathers understood not thy wonders in Egypt: they remembered not the multitude of thy mercies: And they provoked to wrath going up to the sea, even the Red Sea.


<a id="orgc603cc1"></a>

## Psalms 105:8

And he saved them for his own name&rsquo;s sake: that he might make his power known.


<a id="org99412c0"></a>

## Psalms 105:9

And he rebuked the Red Sea and it was dried up: and he led them through the depths, as in a wilderness.


<a id="org21dca4f"></a>

## Psalms 105:10

And he saved them from the hand of them that hated them: and he redeemed them from the hand of the enemy.


<a id="orgfcc55f0"></a>

## Psalms 105:11

And the water covered them that afflicted them: there was not one of them left.


<a id="orgf6d90fb"></a>

## Psalms 105:12

And they believed his words: and they sang his praises.


<a id="org3470d5b"></a>

## Psalms 105:13

They had quickly done, they forgot his works: and they waited not for his counsel.


<a id="org8eb7d54"></a>

## Psalms 105:14

And they coveted their desire in the desert: and they tempted God in the place without water.


<a id="org90e5086"></a>

## Psalms 105:15

And he gave them their request: and sent fulness into their souls.


<a id="org80af1da"></a>

## Psalms 105:16

And they provoked Moses in the camp, Aaron the holy one of the Lord.


<a id="org9197212"></a>

## Psalms 105:17

The earth opened and swallowed up Dathan: and covered the congregation of Abiron.


<a id="org273009d"></a>

## Psalms 105:18

And a fire was kindled in their congregation: the flame burned the wicked.


<a id="org0daeb43"></a>

## Psalms 105:19

They made also a calf in Horeb: and they adored the graven thing.


<a id="orgaa3f5b5"></a>

## Psalms 105:20

And they changed their glory into the likeness of a calf that eateth grass.


<a id="orge4c753d"></a>

## Psalms 105:21

They forgot God, who saved them, who had done great things in Egypt,


<a id="orgf8097ae"></a>

## Psalms 105:22

Wondrous works in the land of Cham: terrible things in the Red Sea.


<a id="org8b46edd"></a>

## Psalms 105:23

And he said that he would destroy them: had not Moses his chosen stood before him in the breach: To turn away his wrath, lest he should destroy them.


<a id="orga4d84b1"></a>

## Psalms 105:24

And they set at nought the desirable land. They believed not his word,


<a id="orgd38eae0"></a>

## Psalms 105:25

And they murmured in their tents: they hearkened not to the voice of the Lord.


<a id="org01027e7"></a>

## Psalms 105:26

And he lifted up his hand over them: to overthrow them in the desert;


<a id="org69c22a3"></a>

## Psalms 105:27

And to cast down their seed among the nations, and to scatter them in the countries.


<a id="org5ad5e06"></a>

## Psalms 105:28

They also were initiated to Beelphegor: and ate the sacrifices of the dead.


<a id="orgbc84910"></a>

## Psalms 105:29

And they provoked him with their inventions: and destruction was multiplied among them.


<a id="org39f4ba6"></a>

## Psalms 105:30

Then Phinees stood up, and pacified him: and the slaughter ceased.


<a id="org5367929"></a>

## Psalms 105:31

And it was reputed to him unto justice, to generation and generation for evermore.


<a id="orga760034"></a>

## Psalms 105:32

They provoked him also at the waters of contradiction: and Moses was afflicted for their sakes:


<a id="orgff1f422"></a>

## Psalms 105:33

Because they exasperated his spirit. And he distinguished with his lips.


<a id="orgb10b2f4"></a>

## Psalms 105:34

They did not destroy the nations of which the Lord spoke unto them.


<a id="org2743835"></a>

## Psalms 105:35

And they were mingled among the heathens, and learned their works:


<a id="org16ccb78"></a>

## Psalms 105:36

And served their idols, and it became a stumblingblock to them.


<a id="org21dd16a"></a>

## Psalms 105:37

And they sacrificed their sons, and their daughters to devils.


<a id="org64679b9"></a>

## Psalms 105:38

And they shed innocent blood: the blood of their sons and of their daughters which they sacrificed to the idols of Chanaan. And the land was polluted with blood,


<a id="org2141d05"></a>

## Psalms 105:39

And was defiled with their works: and they went aside after their own inventions.


<a id="orgc08ea10"></a>

## Psalms 105:40

And the Lord was exceedingly angry with his people: and he abhorred his inheritance.


<a id="org8fa78cc"></a>

## Psalms 105:41

And he delivered them into the hands of the nations: and they that hated them had dominion over them.


<a id="org7d375d6"></a>

## Psalms 105:42

And their enemies afflicted them: and they were humbled under their hands:


<a id="org3453579"></a>

## Psalms 105:43

Many times did he deliver them. But they provoked him with their counsel: and they were brought low by their iniquities.


<a id="orgdfbd043"></a>

## Psalms 105:44

And he saw when they were in tribulation: and he heard their prayer.


<a id="org08db781"></a>

## Psalms 105:45

And he was mindful of his covenant: and repented according to the multitude of his mercies.


<a id="org5ce4ea5"></a>

## Psalms 105:46

And he gave them unto mercies, in the sight of all those that had made them captives.


<a id="org68810df"></a>

## Psalms 105:47

Save us, O Lord, our God: and gather us from among the nations: That we may give thanks to thy holy name, and may glory in thy praise.


<a id="org57fbdc1"></a>

## Psalms 105:48

Blessed be the Lord the God of Israel, from everlasting to everlasting: and let all the people say: So be it, so be it. 


<a id="org42df542"></a>

# Psalms 106


<a id="orgdb172ef"></a>

## Psalms 106:1

Give glory to the Lord, for he is good: for his mercy endureth for ever.


<a id="org16a654a"></a>

## Psalms 106:2

Let them say so that have been redeemed by the Lord, whom he hath redeemed from the hand of the enemy: and gathered out of the countries.


<a id="org520e819"></a>

## Psalms 106:3

From the rising and from the setting of the sun, from the north and from the sea.


<a id="orge9e7137"></a>

## Psalms 106:4

They wandered in a wilderness, in a place without water: they found not the way of a city for their habitation.


<a id="org552a7bc"></a>

## Psalms 106:5

They were hungry and thirsty: their soul fainted in them.


<a id="org6e3710b"></a>

## Psalms 106:6

And they cried to the Lord in their tribulation: and he delivered them out of their distresses.


<a id="org7f69734"></a>

## Psalms 106:7

And he led them into the right way, that they might go to a city of habitation.


<a id="orgd50972a"></a>

## Psalms 106:8

Let the mercies of the Lord give glory to him: and his wonderful works to the children of men.


<a id="org1b9452d"></a>

## Psalms 106:9

For he hath satisfied the empty soul, and hath filled the hungry soul with good things.


<a id="org991888b"></a>

## Psalms 106:10

Such as sat in darkness and in the shadow of death: bound in want and in iron.


<a id="orgfa302a8"></a>

## Psalms 106:11

Because they had exasperated the words of God: and provoked the counsel of the most High:


<a id="orga1f2d0d"></a>

## Psalms 106:12

And their heart was humbled with labours: they were weakened, and there was none to help them.


<a id="orge5668a4"></a>

## Psalms 106:13

Then they cried to the Lord in their affliction: and he delivered them out of their distresses.


<a id="org725af81"></a>

## Psalms 106:14

And he brought them out of darkness, and the shadow of death; and broke their bonds in sunder.


<a id="orgcf4e39c"></a>

## Psalms 106:15

Let the mercies of the Lord give glory to him, and his wonderful works to the children of men.


<a id="org96cb112"></a>

## Psalms 106:16

Because he hath broken gates of brass, and burst iron bars.


<a id="orgad607d0"></a>

## Psalms 106:17

He took them out of the way of their iniquity: for they were brought low for their injustices.


<a id="org296c87d"></a>

## Psalms 106:18

Their soul abhorred all manner of meat: and they drew nigh even to the gates of death.


<a id="org4241d1b"></a>

## Psalms 106:19

And they cried to the Lord in their affliction: and he delivered them out of their distresses.


<a id="org2f017a9"></a>

## Psalms 106:20

He sent his word, and healed them: and delivered them from their destructions.


<a id="org9bef147"></a>

## Psalms 106:21

Let the mercies of the Lord give glory to him: and his wonderful works to the children of men.


<a id="org297bc50"></a>

## Psalms 106:22

And let them sacrifice the sacrifice of praise: and declare his works with joy.


<a id="org3d82eb2"></a>

## Psalms 106:23

They that go down to the sea in ships, doing business in the great waters:


<a id="org5a8c6e6"></a>

## Psalms 106:24

These have seen the works of the Lord, and his wonders in the deep.


<a id="orge13a6c4"></a>

## Psalms 106:25

He said the word, and there arose a storm of wind: and the waves thereof were lifted up.


<a id="orgd46d469"></a>

## Psalms 106:26

They mount up to the heavens, and they go down to the depths: their soul pined away with evils.


<a id="orgc330071"></a>

## Psalms 106:27

They were troubled, and reeled like a drunken man; and all their wisdom was swallowed up.


<a id="org18bf8d6"></a>

## Psalms 106:28

And they cried to the Lord in their affliction: and he brought them out of their distresses.


<a id="orgae4f292"></a>

## Psalms 106:29

And he turned the storm into a breeze: and its waves were still.


<a id="org4f2e77f"></a>

## Psalms 106:30

And they rejoiced because they were still: and he brought them to the haven which they wished for.


<a id="orgce0a0ac"></a>

## Psalms 106:31

Let the mercies of the Lord give glory to him, and his wonderful works to the children of men.


<a id="org8b707de"></a>

## Psalms 106:32

And let them exalt him in the church of the people: and praise him in the chair of the ancients.


<a id="org7b3bf8e"></a>

## Psalms 106:33

He hath turned rivers into a wilderness: and the sources of waters into dry ground:


<a id="orgbf79235"></a>

## Psalms 106:34

A fruitful land into barrenness, for the wickedness of them that dwell therein.


<a id="org524a0a9"></a>

## Psalms 106:35

He hath turned a wilderness into pools of waters, and a dry land into water springs.


<a id="orgfe91b1d"></a>

## Psalms 106:36

And hath placed there the hungry; and they made a city for their habitation.


<a id="orgceedfe9"></a>

## Psalms 106:37

And they sowed fields, and planted vineyards: and they yielded fruit of birth.


<a id="org04c150c"></a>

## Psalms 106:38

And he blessed them, and they were multiplied exceedingly: and their cattle he suffered not to decrease.


<a id="orgd7abcbf"></a>

## Psalms 106:39

Then they were brought to be few: and they were afflicted through the trouble of evils and sorrow.


<a id="orgf71b820"></a>

## Psalms 106:40

Contempt was poured forth upon their princes: and he caused them to wander where there was no passing, and out of the way.


<a id="org6ef06cb"></a>

## Psalms 106:41

And he helped the poor out of poverty: and made him families like a flock of sheep.


<a id="orgca6db79"></a>

## Psalms 106:42

The just shall see, and shall rejoice, and all iniquity shall stop her mouth.


<a id="orgaa03799"></a>

## Psalms 106:43

Who is wise, and will keep these things; and will understand the mercies of the Lord? 


<a id="orgeaf452d"></a>

# Psalms 107


<a id="orgeb472fd"></a>

## Psalms 107:1

A canticle of a psalm for David himself.


<a id="org6749c52"></a>

## Psalms 107:2

My heart is ready, O God, my heart is ready: I will sing, and will give praise, with my glory.


<a id="orge249487"></a>

## Psalms 107:3

Arise, my glory; arise, psaltery and harp: I will arise in the morning early.


<a id="orgc4f3bb3"></a>

## Psalms 107:4

I will praise thee, O Lord, among the people: and I will sing unto thee among the nations.


<a id="org1e07392"></a>

## Psalms 107:5

For thy mercy is great above the heavens: and thy truth even unto the clouds.


<a id="org729628e"></a>

## Psalms 107:6

Be thou exalted, O God, above the heavens, and thy glory over all the earth:


<a id="org3501fe7"></a>

## Psalms 107:7

That thy beloved may be delivered. Save with thy right hand and hear me.


<a id="org7ede301"></a>

## Psalms 107:8

God hath spoken in his holiness. I will rejoice, and I will divide Sichem and I will mete out the vale of tabernacles.


<a id="orgb48853a"></a>

## Psalms 107:9

Galaad is mine: and Manasses is mine and Ephraim the protection of my head. Juda is my king:


<a id="org8e590e2"></a>

## Psalms 107:10

Moab the pot of my hope. Over Edom I will stretch out my shoe: the aliens are become my friends.


<a id="org2ec8ebe"></a>

## Psalms 107:11

Who will bring me into the strong city? who will lead me into Edom?


<a id="orgf291dff"></a>

## Psalms 107:12

Wilt not thou, O God, who hast cast us off ? and wilt not thou, O God, go forth with our armies?


<a id="org3455c47"></a>

## Psalms 107:13

O grant us help from trouble: for vain is the help of man.


<a id="org30dad68"></a>

## Psalms 107:14

Through God we shall do mightily: and he will bring our enemies to nothing. 


<a id="orgd872459"></a>

# Psalms 108


<a id="orgeb9cc0e"></a>

## Psalms 108:1

Unto the end, a psalm for David.


<a id="org4414f4c"></a>

## Psalms 108:2

O God, be not thou silent in my praise: for the mouth of the wicked and the mouth of the deceitful man is opened against me.


<a id="orgd33df1e"></a>

## Psalms 108:3

They have spoken against me with deceitful tongues; and they have compassed me about with words of hatred; and have fought against me without cause.


<a id="org9848e00"></a>

## Psalms 108:4

Instead of making me a return of love, they detracted me: but I gave myself to prayer.


<a id="org22b1a42"></a>

## Psalms 108:5

And they repaid me evil for good: and hatred for my love.


<a id="org51288f9"></a>

## Psalms 108:6

Set thou the sinner over him: and may the devil stand at his right hand.


<a id="orgc6fbb4f"></a>

## Psalms 108:7

When he is judged, may he go out condemned; and may his prayer be turned to sin.


<a id="org17058b0"></a>

## Psalms 108:8

May his days be few: and his bishopric let another take.


<a id="orgf48d6f7"></a>

## Psalms 108:9

May his children be fatherless, and his wife a widow.


<a id="org8f7cdcb"></a>

## Psalms 108:10

Let his children be carried about vagabonds, and beg; and let them be cast out of their dwellings.


<a id="org87bd7da"></a>

## Psalms 108:11

May the usurer search all his substance: and let strangers plunder his labours.


<a id="org48f77b2"></a>

## Psalms 108:12

May there be none to help him: nor none to pity his fatherless offspring.


<a id="org9e7b67d"></a>

## Psalms 108:13

May his posterity be cut off; in one generation may his name be blotted out.


<a id="org367ff59"></a>

## Psalms 108:14

May the iniquity of his fathers be remembered in the sight of the Lord: and let not the sin of his mother be blotted out.


<a id="org8a5f8a6"></a>

## Psalms 108:15

May they be before the Lord continually, and let the memory of them perish from the earth:


<a id="orgb0ab468"></a>

## Psalms 108:16

because he remembered not to shew mercy,


<a id="org20807fb"></a>

## Psalms 108:17

But persecuted the poor man and the beggar; and the broken in heart, to put him to death.


<a id="org259acb8"></a>

## Psalms 108:18

And he loved cursing, and it shall come unto him: and he would not have blessing, and it shall be far from him. And he put on cursing, like a garment: and it went in like water into his entrails, and like oil in his bones.


<a id="orgfe0d25e"></a>

## Psalms 108:19

May it be unto him like a garment which covereth him; and like a girdle with which he is girded continually.


<a id="org0d3a5fb"></a>

## Psalms 108:20

This is the work of them who detract me before the Lord; and who speak evils against my soul.


<a id="orgca2502b"></a>

## Psalms 108:21

But thou, O Lord, do with me for thy name&rsquo;s sake: because thy mercy is sweet. Do thou deliver me,


<a id="org18b2bf6"></a>

## Psalms 108:22

For I am poor and needy, and my heart is troubled within me.


<a id="org9e08bc8"></a>

## Psalms 108:23

I am taken away like the shadow when it declineth: and I am shaken off as locusts.


<a id="orge10bcf7"></a>

## Psalms 108:24

My knees are weakened through fasting: and my flesh is changed for oil.


<a id="orgaa16adb"></a>

## Psalms 108:25

And I am become a reproach to them: they saw me and they shaked their heads.


<a id="org3deecf8"></a>

## Psalms 108:26

Help me, O Lord my God; save me; according to thy mercy.


<a id="orgcfa6aa1"></a>

## Psalms 108:27

And let them know that this is thy hand: and that thou, O Lord, hast done it.


<a id="org57fc6c3"></a>

## Psalms 108:28

They will curse and thou wilt bless: let them that rise up against me be confounded: but thy servant shall rejoice.


<a id="org210191a"></a>

## Psalms 108:29

Let them that detract me be clothed with shame: and let them be covered with their confusion as with a double cloak.


<a id="org8e72aee"></a>

## Psalms 108:30

I will give great thanks to the Lord with my mouth: and in the midst of many I will praise him.


<a id="org49f3349"></a>

## Psalms 108:31

Because he hath stood at the right hand of the poor, to save my soul from persecutors. 


<a id="org24b6490"></a>

# Psalms 109


<a id="orge3f084e"></a>

## Psalms 109:1

A psalm for David. The Lord said to my Lord: Sit thou at my right hand: Until I make thy enemies thy footstool.


<a id="orge8a1a8b"></a>

## Psalms 109:2

The Lord will send forth the sceptre of thy power out of Sion: rule thou in the midst of thy enemies.


<a id="org79b437a"></a>

## Psalms 109:3

With thee is the principality in the day of thy strength: in the brightness of the saints: from the womb before the day star I begot thee.


<a id="org9729a71"></a>

## Psalms 109:4

The Lord hath sworn, and he will not repent: Thou art a priest for ever according to the order of Melchisedech.


<a id="org9fea710"></a>

## Psalms 109:5

The Lord at thy right hand hath broken kings in the day of his wrath.


<a id="org5245845"></a>

## Psalms 109:6

He shall judge among nations, he shall fill ruins: he shall crush the heads in the land of many.


<a id="orgdd58ca4"></a>

## Psalms 109:7

He shall drink of the torrent in the way: therefore shall he lift up the head. 


<a id="org01101e1"></a>

# Psalms 110


<a id="org0aadf60"></a>

## Psalms 110:1

I will praise thee, O Lord, with my whole heart; in the council of the just, and in the congregation.


<a id="org15b2296"></a>

## Psalms 110:2

Great are the works of the Lord: sought out according to all his wills.


<a id="org5e300d0"></a>

## Psalms 110:3

His work is praise and magnificence: and his justice continueth for ever and ever.


<a id="org22dd0a9"></a>

## Psalms 110:4

He hath made a remembrance of his wonderful works, being a merciful and gracious Lord:


<a id="orgfd0ffdc"></a>

## Psalms 110:5

He hath given food to them that fear him. He will be mindful for ever of his covenant:


<a id="org8e1ba6a"></a>

## Psalms 110:6

He will shew forth to his people the power of his works.


<a id="org8e94f04"></a>

## Psalms 110:7

That he may give them the inheritance of the Gentiles: the works of his hands are truth and judgment.


<a id="org7d690fb"></a>

## Psalms 110:8

All his commandments are faithful: confirmed for ever and ever, made in truth and equity.


<a id="org6e67660"></a>

## Psalms 110:9

He hath sent redemption to his people: he hath commanded his covenant for ever. Holy and terrible is his name:


<a id="org99bbde6"></a>

## Psalms 110:10

The fear of the Lord is the beginning of wisdom. A good understanding to all that do it: his praise continueth for ever and ever. 


<a id="org303efca"></a>

# Psalms 111


<a id="org95ab951"></a>

## Psalms 111:1

Blessed is the man that feareth the Lord: he shall delight exceedingly in his commandments.


<a id="org5ca60f3"></a>

## Psalms 111:2

His seed shall be mighty upon earth: the generation of the righteous shall be blessed.


<a id="org61dc408"></a>

## Psalms 111:3

Glory and wealth shall be in his house: and his justice remaineth for ever and ever.


<a id="org102d262"></a>

## Psalms 111:4

To the righteous a light is risen up in darkness: he is merciful, and compassionate and just.


<a id="org8165662"></a>

## Psalms 111:5

Acceptable is the man that sheweth mercy and lendeth: he shall order his words with judgment:


<a id="org0e45173"></a>

## Psalms 111:6

Because he shall not be moved for ever.


<a id="org356d780"></a>

## Psalms 111:7

The just shall be in everlasting remembrance: he shall not fear the evil hearing. His heart is ready to hope in the Lord:


<a id="orgf295b3a"></a>

## Psalms 111:8

His heart is strengthened, he shall not be moved until he look over his enemies.


<a id="org46a371d"></a>

## Psalms 111:9

He hath distributed, he hath given to the poor: his justice remaineth for ever and ever: his horn shall be exalted in glory.


<a id="org79d5dd2"></a>

## Psalms 111:10

The wicked shall see, and shall be angry, he shall gnash with his teeth and pine away: the desire of the wicked shall perish. 


<a id="org27f38cf"></a>

# Psalms 112


<a id="orgb7e7c83"></a>

## Psalms 112:1

Praise the Lord, ye children: praise ye the name of the Lord.


<a id="org610f193"></a>

## Psalms 112:2

Blessed be the name of the Lord, from henceforth now and for ever.


<a id="org237a767"></a>

## Psalms 112:3

From the rising of the sun unto the going down of the same, the name of the Lord is worthy of praise.


<a id="org4c6cd3b"></a>

## Psalms 112:4

The Lord is high above all nations; and his glory above the heavens.


<a id="orga9a042e"></a>

## Psalms 112:5

Who is as the Lord our God, who dwelleth on high:


<a id="orgd410254"></a>

## Psalms 112:6

and looketh down on the low things in heaven and in earth?


<a id="orgd84b37e"></a>

## Psalms 112:7

Raising up the needy from the earth, and lifting up the poor out of the dunghill:


<a id="orgfee496e"></a>

## Psalms 112:8

That he may place him with princes, with the princes of his people.


<a id="org726f77c"></a>

## Psalms 112:9

Who maketh a barren woman to dwell in a house, the joyful mother of children. 


<a id="org581ae94"></a>

# Psalms 113


<a id="orgc238f8f"></a>

## Psalms 113:1

When Israel went out of Egypt, the house of Jacob from a barbarous people:


<a id="org478b15e"></a>

## Psalms 113:2

Judea was made his sanctuary, Israel his dominion.


<a id="orgfff5c67"></a>

## Psalms 113:3

The sea saw and fled: Jordan was turned back.


<a id="orgc1c78e9"></a>

## Psalms 113:4

The mountains skipped like rams, and the hills like the lambs of the flock.


<a id="org6ad9165"></a>

## Psalms 113:5

What ailed thee, O thou sea, that thou didst flee: and thou, O Jordan, that thou wast turned back?


<a id="org15b4e04"></a>

## Psalms 113:6

Ye mountains, that ye skipped like rams, and ye hills, like lambs of the flock?


<a id="orgf74b7fc"></a>

## Psalms 113:7

At the presence of the Lord the earth was moved, at the presence of the God of Jacob:


<a id="org6ba6e1d"></a>

## Psalms 113:8

Who turned the rock into pools of water, and the stony hill into fountains of waters.


<a id="orgfdee744"></a>

## Psalms 113:9

Not to us, O Lord, not to us; but to thy name give glory.


<a id="org6f966cf"></a>

## Psalms 113:10

For thy mercy, and for thy truth&rsquo;s sake: lest the Gentiles should say: Where is their God?


<a id="orgcee297a"></a>

## Psalms 113:11

But our God is in heaven: he hath done all things whatsoever he would.


<a id="orgecd0ff3"></a>

## Psalms 113:12

The idols of the Gentiles are silver and gold, the works of the hands of men.


<a id="org7ed36d9"></a>

## Psalms 113:13

They have mouths and speak not: they have eyes and see not.


<a id="orgfb99cf4"></a>

## Psalms 113:14

They have ears and hear not: they have noses and smell not.


<a id="org881fb19"></a>

## Psalms 113:15

They have hands and feel not: they have feet and walk not: neither shall they cry out through their throat.


<a id="org37d8c52"></a>

## Psalms 113:16

Let them that make them become like unto them: and all such as trust in them.


<a id="orgbdb8efd"></a>

## Psalms 113:17

The house of Israel hath hoped in the Lord: he is their helper and their protector.


<a id="org332c97a"></a>

## Psalms 113:18

The house of Aaron hath hoped in the Lord: he is their helper and their protector.


<a id="org9e158bf"></a>

## Psalms 113:19

They that fear the Lord have hoped in the Lord: he is their helper and their protector.


<a id="org40521ec"></a>

## Psalms 113:20

The Lord hath been mindful of us, and hath blessed us. He hath blessed the house of Israel: he hath blessed the house of Aaron.


<a id="org6c9eb05"></a>

## Psalms 113:21

He hath blessed all that fear the Lord, both little and great.


<a id="orgc104660"></a>

## Psalms 113:22

May the Lord add blessings upon you: upon you, and upon your children.


<a id="orgca2c644"></a>

## Psalms 113:23

Blessed be you of the Lord, who made heaven and earth.


<a id="org317d3b2"></a>

## Psalms 113:24

The heaven of heaven is the Lord&rsquo;s: but the earth he has given to the children of men.


<a id="orgbb969d6"></a>

## Psalms 113:25

The dead shall not praise thee, O Lord: nor any of them that go down to hell.


<a id="orgaea142e"></a>

## Psalms 113:26

But we that live bless the Lord: from this time now and for ever. 


<a id="orgc159958"></a>

# Psalms 114


<a id="orga412b90"></a>

## Psalms 114:1

I have loved, because the Lord will hear the voice of my prayer.


<a id="org6ca7874"></a>

## Psalms 114:2

Because he hath inclined his ear unto me: and in my days I will call upon him.


<a id="orgd1ae8aa"></a>

## Psalms 114:3

The sorrows of death have compassed me: and the perils of hell have found me. I met with trouble and sorrow:


<a id="org7bd58bd"></a>

## Psalms 114:4

And I called upon the name of the Lord. O Lord, deliver my soul.


<a id="org5bb43b0"></a>

## Psalms 114:5

The Lord is merciful and just, and our God sheweth mercy.


<a id="orgfddf00f"></a>

## Psalms 114:6

The Lord is the keeper of little ones: I was humbled, and he delivered me.


<a id="orgff3921c"></a>

## Psalms 114:7

Turn, O my soul, into thy rest: for the Lord hath been bountiful to thee.


<a id="org13a381a"></a>

## Psalms 114:8

For he hath delivered my soul from death: my eyes from tears, my feet from falling.


<a id="orga9d52a9"></a>

## Psalms 114:9

I will please the Lord in the land of the living. 


<a id="org637600b"></a>

# Psalms 115


<a id="org3505881"></a>

## Psalms 115:1

I have believed, therefore have I spoken; but I have been humbled exceedingly.


<a id="org1237321"></a>

## Psalms 115:2

I said in my excess: Every man is a liar.


<a id="orgf84a6bb"></a>

## Psalms 115:3

What shall I render to the Lord, for all the things that he hath rendered to me?


<a id="org62bb13e"></a>

## Psalms 115:4

I will take the chalice of salvation; and I will call upon the name of the Lord.


<a id="org09789fb"></a>

## Psalms 115:5

<a id="org3059969"></a>

## Psalms 115:6

<a id="orgc3ea848"></a>

<a id="org299ffba"></a>

<a id="org130c0fb"></a>

## Psalms 115:9

<a id="org54aaf54"></a>

<a id="orgc909402"></a>

## Psalms 116:1

O Praise the Lord, all ye nations: praise him, all ye people.


<a id="org25797f4"></a>

## Psalms 116:2

<a id="org344324c"></a>

# Psalms 117


<a id="org8e39751"></a>

## Psalms 117:1

Give praise to the Lord, for he is good: for his mercy endureth for ever.


<a id="org578d401"></a>

## Psalms 117:2

Let Israel now say, that he is good: that his mercy endureth for ever.


<a id="org017743d"></a>

## Psalms 117:3

Let the house of Aaron now say, that his mercy endureth for ever.


<a id="org8b71920"></a>

## Psalms 117:4

Let them that fear the Lord now say, that his mercy endureth for ever.


<a id="orgbd30197"></a>

## Psalms 117:5

In my trouble I called upon the Lord: and the Lord heard me, and enlarged me.


<a id="org510ed15"></a>

## Psalms 117:6

The Lord is my helper: I will not fear what man can do unto me.


<a id="org16bb5a7"></a>

## Psalms 117:7

The Lord is my helper: and I will look over my enemies.


<a id="orgd95e670"></a>

## Psalms 117:8

It is good to confide in the Lord, rather than to have confidence in man.


<a id="orgde327ea"></a>

## Psalms 117:9

It is good to trust in the Lord, rather than to trust in princes.


<a id="org275fa56"></a>

## Psalms 117:10

All nations compassed me about; and, in the name of the Lord I have been revenged on them.


<a id="orga774402"></a>

## Psalms 117:11

Surrounding me they compassed me about: and in the name of the Lord I have been revenged on them.


<a id="org0662180"></a>

## Psalms 117:12

They surrounded me like bees, and they burned like fire among thorns: and in the name of the Lord I was revenged on them.


<a id="org84260f9"></a>

## Psalms 117:13

Being pushed I was overturned that I might fall: but the Lord supported me.


<a id="org7fcbe23"></a>

## Psalms 117:14

The Lord is my strength and my praise: and he is become my salvation.


<a id="org853c1aa"></a>

## Psalms 117:15

The voice of rejoicing and of salvation is in the tabernacles of the just.


<a id="org3bfb96b"></a>

## Psalms 117:16

The right hand of the Lord hath wrought strength: the right hand of the Lord hath exalted me: the right hand of the Lord hath wrought strength.


<a id="orgae3e41b"></a>

## Psalms 117:17

I shall not die, but live: and shall declare the works of the Lord.


<a id="orgfeddf85"></a>

## Psalms 117:18

The Lord chastising hath chastised me: but he hath not delivered me over to death.


<a id="orgfe5e249"></a>

## Psalms 117:19

Open ye to me the gates of justice: I will go in to them, and give praise to the Lord.


<a id="org0c6575b"></a>

## Psalms 117:20

This is the gate of the Lord, the just shall enter into it.


<a id="org76c11e4"></a>

## Psalms 117:21

I will give glory to thee because thou hast heard me: and art become my salvation.


<a id="org2d1a5d9"></a>

## Psalms 117:22

The stone which the builders rejected; the same is become the head of the corner.


<a id="org52211b9"></a>

## Psalms 117:23

This is the Lord&rsquo;s doing, and it is wonderful in our eyes.


<a id="org5f1b3b6"></a>

## Psalms 117:24

This is the day which the Lord hath made: let us be glad and rejoice therein.


<a id="orgd5f66a7"></a>

## Psalms 117:25

O Lord, save me: O Lord, give good success.


<a id="orgfdc36e9"></a>

## Psalms 117:26

Blessed be he that cometh in the name of the Lord. We have blessed you out of the house of the Lord.


<a id="org4962450"></a>

## Psalms 117:27

The Lord is God, and he hath shone upon us. Appoint a solemn day, with shady boughs, even to the horn of the altar.


<a id="orgf868eaa"></a>

## Psalms 117:28

Thou art my God, and I will praise thee: thou art my God, and I will exalt thee. I will praise thee, because thou hast heard me, and art become my salvation.


<a id="orgf89c76a"></a>

## Psalms 117:29

O praise ye the Lord, for he is good: for his mercy endureth for ever. 


<a id="org806969b"></a>

# Psalms 118


<a id="org1c68d5c"></a>

## Psalms 118:1

Blessed are the undefiled in the way, who walk in the law of the Lord.


<a id="orgc197341"></a>

## Psalms 118:2

Blessed are they that search his testimonies: that seek him with their whole heart.


<a id="orgd9f5185"></a>

## Psalms 118:3

For they that work iniquity, have not walked in his ways.


<a id="org7b5eb14"></a>

## Psalms 118:4

Thou hast commanded thy commandments to be kept most diligently.


<a id="org9f69328"></a>

## Psalms 118:5

O! that my ways may be directed to keep thy justifications.


<a id="org508bba2"></a>

## Psalms 118:6

Then shall I not be confounded, when I shall look into all thy commandments.


<a id="org41fccb7"></a>

## Psalms 118:7

I will praise thee with uprightness of heart, when I shall have learned the judgments of thy justice.


<a id="org71d6581"></a>

## Psalms 118:8

I will keep thy justifications: O! do not thou utterly forsake me.


<a id="orgeff89e1"></a>

## Psalms 118:9

By what doth a young man correct his way? by observing thy words.


<a id="orgcfd3fae"></a>

## Psalms 118:10

With my whole heart have I sought after thee: let me not stray from thy commandments.


<a id="org4f2e958"></a>

## Psalms 118:11

Thy words have I hidden in my heart, that I may not sin against thee.


<a id="orge4400a6"></a>

## Psalms 118:12

Blessed art thou, O Lord: teach me thy justifications.


<a id="org8a91bff"></a>

## Psalms 118:13

With my lips I have pronounced all the judgments of thy mouth.


<a id="orgdbbf250"></a>

## Psalms 118:14

I have been delighted in the way of thy testimonies, as in all riches.


<a id="org76c8bdb"></a>

## Psalms 118:15

I will meditate on thy commandments: and I will consider thy ways.


<a id="org99ec12b"></a>

## Psalms 118:16

I will think of thy justifications: I will not forget thy words.


<a id="org8b25363"></a>

## Psalms 118:17

Give bountifully to thy servant, enliven me: and I shall keep thy words.


<a id="org40e47fb"></a>

## Psalms 118:18

Open thou my eyes: and I will consider the wondrous things of thy law.


<a id="orgf2dbb1b"></a>

## Psalms 118:19

I am a sojourner on the earth: hide not thy commandments from me.


<a id="org46b6c74"></a>

## Psalms 118:20

My soul hath coveted to long for thy justifications, at all times.


<a id="org19ac17a"></a>

## Psalms 118:21

Thou hast rebuked the proud: they are cursed who decline from thy commandments.


<a id="orgbb44cba"></a>

## Psalms 118:22

Remove from me reproach and contempt: because I have sought after thy testimonies.


<a id="org14b6db7"></a>

## Psalms 118:23

For princes sat, and spoke against me: but thy servant was employed in thy justifications.


<a id="orgaf4d84a"></a>

## Psalms 118:24

For thy testimonies are my meditation: and thy justifications my counsel.


<a id="orgc7cce7e"></a>

## Psalms 118:25

My soul hath cleaved to the pavement: quicken thou me according to thy word.


<a id="org9930e52"></a>

## Psalms 118:26

I have declared my ways, and thou hast heard me: teach me thy justifications.


<a id="orgcd3d73f"></a>

## Psalms 118:27

Make me to understand the way of thy justifications: and I shall be exercised in thy wondrous works.


<a id="org11078cd"></a>

## Psalms 118:28

My soul hath slumbered through heaviness: strengthen thou me in thy words.


<a id="orge888771"></a>

## Psalms 118:29

Remove from me the way of iniquity: and out of thy law have mercy on me.


<a id="org80827d3"></a>

## Psalms 118:30

I have chosen the way of truth: thy judgments I have not forgotten.


<a id="org7e6d3fb"></a>

## Psalms 118:31

I have stuck to thy testimonies, O Lord: put me not to shame.


<a id="orgd8f7d12"></a>

## Psalms 118:32

I have run the way of thy commandments, when thou didst enlarge my heart.


<a id="org50cd743"></a>

## Psalms 118:33

Set before me for a law the way of thy justifications, O Lord: and I will always seek after it.


<a id="orgfff8b3b"></a>

## Psalms 118:34

Give me understanding, and I will search thy law; and I will keep it with my whole heart.


<a id="org7265df0"></a>

## Psalms 118:35

Lead me into the path of thy commandments; for this same I have desired.


<a id="orgc0bec1e"></a>

## Psalms 118:36

Incline my heart into thy testimonies and not to covetousness.


<a id="org26feffe"></a>

## Psalms 118:37

Turn away my eyes that they may not behold vanity: quicken me in thy way.


<a id="orga0c073b"></a>

## Psalms 118:38

Establish thy word to thy servant, in thy fear.


<a id="orgc65126b"></a>

## Psalms 118:39

Turn away my reproach, which I have apprehended: for thy judgments are delightful.


<a id="orgf046697"></a>

## Psalms 118:40

Behold I have longed after thy precepts: quicken me in thy justice.


<a id="orge87e361"></a>

## Psalms 118:41

Let thy mercy also come upon me, O Lord: thy salvation according to thy word.


<a id="org387e1c8"></a>

## Psalms 118:42

So shall I answer them that reproach me in any thing; that I have trusted in thy words.


<a id="org26a0eda"></a>

## Psalms 118:43

And take not thou the word of truth utterly out of my mouth: for in thy words, I have hoped exceedingly.


<a id="org3d5d9e1"></a>

## Psalms 118:44

So shall I always keep thy law, for ever and ever.


<a id="org84cc061"></a>

## Psalms 118:45

And I walked at large: because I have sought after thy commandments.


<a id="orgc4bac53"></a>

## Psalms 118:46

And I spoke of thy testimonies before kings: and I was not ashamed.


<a id="orga45436e"></a>

## Psalms 118:47

I meditated also on thy commandments, which I loved.


<a id="org5350ef4"></a>

## Psalms 118:48

And I lifted up my hands to thy commandments, which I loved: and I was exercised in thy justifications.


<a id="org77e9426"></a>

## Psalms 118:49

Be thou mindful of thy word to thy servant, in which thou hast given me hope.


<a id="org958c833"></a>

## Psalms 118:50

This hath comforted me in my humiliation: because thy word hath enlivened me.


<a id="orgc20dd9f"></a>

## Psalms 118:51

The proud did iniquitously altogether: but I declined not from thy law.


<a id="org974bb1c"></a>

## Psalms 118:52

I remembered, O Lord, thy judgments of old: and I was comforted.


<a id="orga735cbf"></a>

## Psalms 118:53

A fainting hath taken hold of me, because of the wicked that forsake thy law.


<a id="org0c98fd6"></a>

## Psalms 118:54

Thy justifications were the subject of my song, in the place of my pilgrimage.


<a id="orgfa806cd"></a>

## Psalms 118:55

In the night I have remembered thy name, O Lord: and have kept thy law.


<a id="orga0a669b"></a>

## Psalms 118:56

This happened to me: because I sought after thy justifications.


<a id="orgaf24b02"></a>

## Psalms 118:57

O Lord, my portion, I have said, I would keep thy law.


<a id="orgc2394f2"></a>

## Psalms 118:58

I entreated thy face with all my heart: have mercy on me according to thy word.


<a id="org8003024"></a>

## Psalms 118:59

I have thought on my ways: and turned my feet unto thy testimonies.


<a id="orgc1a7123"></a>

## Psalms 118:60

I am ready, and am not troubled: that I may keep thy commandments.


<a id="org970fabc"></a>

## Psalms 118:61

The cords of the wicked have encompassed me: but I have not forgotten thy law.


<a id="orgee706d3"></a>

## Psalms 118:62

I rose at midnight to give praise to thee; for the judgments of thy justification.


<a id="org37b9ddc"></a>

## Psalms 118:63

I am a partaker with all them that fear thee, and that keep thy commandments.


<a id="org3ff1c56"></a>

## Psalms 118:64

The earth, O Lord, is full of thy mercy: teach me thy justifications.


<a id="orgb7d9566"></a>

## Psalms 118:65

Thou hast done well with thy servant, O Lord, according to thy word.


<a id="org35491d2"></a>

## Psalms 118:66

Teach me goodness and discipline and knowledge; for I have believed thy commandments.


<a id="org579307e"></a>

## Psalms 118:67

Before I was humbled I offended; therefore have I kept thy word.


<a id="org153c0c5"></a>

## Psalms 118:68

Thou art good; and in thy goodness teach me thy justifications.


<a id="orgba87eb0"></a>

## Psalms 118:69

The iniquity of the proud hath been multiplied over me: but I will seek thy commandments with my whole heart.


<a id="org6f87d6b"></a>

## Psalms 118:70

Their heart is curdled like milk: but I have meditated on thy law.


<a id="orgbc797d0"></a>

## Psalms 118:71

It is good for me that thou hast humbled me, that I may learn thy justifications.


<a id="org4198446"></a>

## Psalms 118:72

The law of thy mouth is good to me, above thousands of gold and silver.


<a id="org95ab103"></a>

## Psalms 118:73

Thy hands have made me and formed me: give me understanding, and I will learn thy commandments.


<a id="org45d123d"></a>

## Psalms 118:74

They that fear thee shall see me, and shall be glad : because I have greatly hoped in thy words.


<a id="org2966db9"></a>

## Psalms 118:75

I know, O Lord, that thy judgments are equity: and in thy truth thou hast humbled me.


<a id="org12a7359"></a>

## Psalms 118:76

O! let thy mercy be for my comfort, according to thy word unto thy servant.


<a id="orgb9ce828"></a>

## Psalms 118:77

Let thy tender mercies come unto me, and I shall live: for thy law is my meditation.


<a id="orgff68b9c"></a>

## Psalms 118:78

Let the proud be ashamed, because they have done unjustly towards me: but I will be employed in thy commandments.


<a id="org8f0ddf8"></a>

## Psalms 118:79

Let them that fear thee turn to me: and they that know thy testimonies.


<a id="org410e594"></a>

## Psalms 118:80

Let my heart be undefiled in thy justifications, that I may not be confounded.


<a id="org15f4717"></a>

## Psalms 118:81

My soul hath fainted after thy salvation: and in thy word I have very much hoped.


<a id="orge8b2ad3"></a>

## Psalms 118:82

My eyes have failed for thy word, saying: When wilt thou comfort me?


<a id="org3ad7a14"></a>

## Psalms 118:83

For I am become like a bottle in the frost: I have not forgotten thy justifications.


<a id="org110081a"></a>

## Psalms 118:84

How many are the days of thy servant: when wilt thou execute judgment on them that persecute me?


<a id="org4d03d62"></a>

## Psalms 118:85

The wicked have told me fables: but not as thy law.


<a id="orgd357039"></a>

## Psalms 118:86

All thy statutes are truth: they have persecuted me unjustly, do thou help me.


<a id="orgedfabc5"></a>

## Psalms 118:87

They had almost made an end of me upon earth: but I have not forsaken thy commandments.


<a id="org5b94547"></a>

## Psalms 118:88

Quicken thou me according to thy mercy: and I shall keep the testimonies of thy mouth.


<a id="org32354d3"></a>

## Psalms 118:89

For ever, O Lord, thy word standeth firm in heaven.


<a id="org1a63fa9"></a>

## Psalms 118:90

Thy truth unto all generations: thou hast founded the earth, and it continueth.


<a id="org3eb0804"></a>

## Psalms 118:91

By thy ordinance the day goeth on: for all things serve thee.


<a id="orgcd727fb"></a>

## Psalms 118:92

Unless thy law had been my meditation, I had then perhaps perished in my abjection.


<a id="orgdc2c209"></a>

## Psalms 118:93

Thy justifications I will never forget: for by them thou hast given me life.


<a id="org7aa2439"></a>

## Psalms 118:94

I am thine, save thou me: for I have sought thy justifications.


<a id="org911389d"></a>

## Psalms 118:95

The wicked have waited for me to destroy me: but I have understood thy testimonies.


<a id="org45d3869"></a>

## Psalms 118:96

I have seen an end of all perfection: thy commandment is exceeding broad.


<a id="org8b30a63"></a>

## Psalms 118:97

O how have I loved thy law, O Lord! it is my meditation all the day.


<a id="org6a4224c"></a>

## Psalms 118:98

Through thy commandment, thou hast made me wiser than my enemies: for it is ever with me.


<a id="orgf9b9c4d"></a>

## Psalms 118:99

I have understood more than all my teachers: because thy testimonies are my meditation.


<a id="org81d7fcb"></a>

## Psalms 118:100

I have had understanding above ancients: because I have sought thy commandments.


<a id="orgf25c95c"></a>

## Psalms 118:101

I have restrained my feet from every evil way: that I may keep thy words.


<a id="org5f5395a"></a>

## Psalms 118:102

I have not declined from thy judgments, because thou hast set me a law.


<a id="orge6990b8"></a>

## Psalms 118:103

How sweet are thy words to my palate! more than honey to my mouth.


<a id="org7353b43"></a>

## Psalms 118:104

By thy commandments I have had understanding: therefore have I hated every way of iniquity.


<a id="orge0fe1e0"></a>

## Psalms 118:105

Thy word is a lamp to my feet, and a light to my paths.


<a id="org30cf4a6"></a>

## Psalms 118:106

I have sworn and am determined to keep the judgments of thy justice.


<a id="org37246c2"></a>

## Psalms 118:107

I have been humbled, O Lord, exceedingly: quicken thou me according to thy word.


<a id="orgd6878b3"></a>

## Psalms 118:108

The free offerings of my mouth make acceptable, O Lord: and teach me thy judgments.


<a id="org204acd2"></a>

## Psalms 118:109

My soul is continually in my hands: and I have not forgotten thy law.


<a id="org120e698"></a>

## Psalms 118:110

Sinners have laid a snare for me: but I have not erred from thy precepts.


<a id="orgcd7d5d2"></a>

## Psalms 118:111

I have purchased thy testimonies for an inheritance for ever: because they are the joy of my heart.


<a id="org1757e50"></a>

## Psalms 118:112

I have inclined my heart to do thy justifications for ever, for the reward.


<a id="org7e4bfa4"></a>

## Psalms 118:113

I have hated the unjust: and have loved thy law.


<a id="orgb70b128"></a>

## Psalms 118:114

Thou art my helper and my protector: and in thy word I have greatly hoped.


<a id="org31df1b0"></a>

## Psalms 118:115

Depart from me, ye malignant: and I will search the commandments of my God.


<a id="orge9da511"></a>

## Psalms 118:116

Uphold me according to thy word, and I shall live: and let me not be confounded in my expectation.


<a id="org6deb9aa"></a>

## Psalms 118:117

Help me, and I shall be saved: and I will meditate always on thy justifications.


<a id="org5addcad"></a>

## Psalms 118:118

Thou hast despised all them that fall off from thy judgments; for their thought is unjust.


<a id="org20ad7d6"></a>

## Psalms 118:119

I have accounted all the sinners of the earth prevaricators: therefore have I loved thy testimonies.


<a id="orga120747"></a>

## Psalms 118:120

Pierce thou my flesh with thy fear: for I am afraid of thy judgments.


<a id="org26d4cea"></a>

## Psalms 118:121

I have done judgment and justice: give me not up to them that slander me.


<a id="orgb7e2c0b"></a>

## Psalms 118:122

Uphold thy servant unto good: let not the proud calumniate me.


<a id="org95745f1"></a>

## Psalms 118:123

My eyes have fainted after thy salvation: and for the word of thy justice.


<a id="org4498363"></a>

## Psalms 118:124

Deal with thy servant according to thy mercy: and teach me thy justifications.


<a id="org4f3f942"></a>

## Psalms 118:125

I am thy servant: give me understanding that I may know thy testimonies.


<a id="org431e7a9"></a>

## Psalms 118:126

It is time, O Lord, to do: they have dissipated thy law.


<a id="org6cd7c09"></a>

## Psalms 118:127

Therefore have I loved thy commandments above gold and the topaz.


<a id="org41f5ace"></a>

## Psalms 118:128

Therefore was I directed to all thy commandments: I have hated all wicked ways.


<a id="org7dff7f7"></a>

## Psalms 118:129

Thy testimonies are wonderful: therefore my soul hath sought them.


<a id="org63f9f0b"></a>

## Psalms 118:130

The declaration of thy words giveth light: and giveth understanding to little ones.


<a id="orga210755"></a>

## Psalms 118:131

I opened my mouth, and panted: because I longed for thy commandments.


<a id="orge7500fb"></a>

## Psalms 118:132

Look thou upon me, and have mercy on me according to the judgment of them that love thy name.


<a id="orgc84e67e"></a>

## Psalms 118:133

Direct my steps according to thy word: and let no iniquity have dominion over me.


<a id="org3cce325"></a>

## Psalms 118:134

Redeem me from the calumnies of men: that I may keep thy commandments.


<a id="org56ea1a5"></a>

## Psalms 118:135

Make thy face to shine upon thy servant: and teach me thy justifications.


<a id="org3992fb8"></a>

## Psalms 118:136

My eyes have sent forth springs of water: because they have not kept thy law.


<a id="orgc1deadf"></a>

## Psalms 118:137

Thou art just, O Lord: and thy judgment is right.


<a id="orgbfe5136"></a>

## Psalms 118:138

Thou hast commanded justice thy testimonies: and thy truth exceedingly.


<a id="orgdb4bf58"></a>

## Psalms 118:139

My zeal hath made me pine away: because my enemies forgot thy words.


<a id="org0854fc9"></a>

## Psalms 118:140

Thy word is exceedingly refined: and thy servant hath loved it.


<a id="orgc3db104"></a>

## Psalms 118:141

I am very young and despised; but I forget not thy justifications.


<a id="org0daf6bc"></a>

## Psalms 118:142

Thy justice is justice for ever: and thy law is the truth.


<a id="org80c5d26"></a>

## Psalms 118:143

Trouble and anguish have found me: thy commandments are my meditation.


<a id="org4b083f1"></a>

## Psalms 118:144

Thy testimonies are justice for ever: give me understanding, and I shall live.


<a id="org39479f8"></a>

## Psalms 118:145

I cried with my whole heart, hear me, O Lord: I will seek thy justifications.


<a id="orgc753a58"></a>

## Psalms 118:146

I cried unto thee, save me: that I may keep thy commandments.


<a id="orga5206f4"></a>

## Psalms 118:147

I prevented the dawning of the day, and cried: because in thy words I very much hoped.


<a id="orgb8d64f9"></a>

## Psalms 118:148

My eyes to thee have prevented the morning: that I might meditate on thy words.


<a id="org518723b"></a>

## Psalms 118:149

Hear thou my voice, O Lord, according to thy mercy: and quicken me according to thy judgment.


<a id="org144e42c"></a>

## Psalms 118:150

They that persecute me have drawn nigh to iniquity; but they are gone far off from thy law.


<a id="org52d3135"></a>

## Psalms 118:151

Thou art near, O Lord: and all thy ways are truth.


<a id="orgdb6687b"></a>

## Psalms 118:152

I have known from the beginning concerning thy testimonies: that thou hast founded them for ever.


<a id="org5a72fbd"></a>

## Psalms 118:153

See my humiliation and deliver me for I have not forgotten thy law.


<a id="org3c92115"></a>

## Psalms 118:154

Judge my judgment and redeem me: quicken thou me for thy word&rsquo;s sake.


<a id="orgbf6495d"></a>

## Psalms 118:155

Salvation is far from sinners; because they have not sought thy justifications.


<a id="org0c55588"></a>

## Psalms 118:156

Many, O Lord, are thy mercies: quicken me according to thy judgment.


<a id="org1823906"></a>

## Psalms 118:157

Many are they that persecute me and afflict me; but I have not declined from thy testimonies.


<a id="org04a69ec"></a>

## Psalms 118:158

I beheld the transgressors, and pined away; because they kept not thy word.


<a id="orge0ea702"></a>

## Psalms 118:159

Behold I have loved thy commandments, O Lord; quicken me thou in thy mercy.


<a id="orgc60f262"></a>

## Psalms 118:160

The beginning of thy words is truth: all the judgments of thy justice are for ever.


<a id="org92bc1d9"></a>

## Psalms 118:161

Princes have persecuted me without cause: and my heart hath been in awe of thy words.


<a id="org34a0ba1"></a>

## Psalms 118:162

I will rejoice at thy words, as one that hath found great spoil.


<a id="orgb952e8a"></a>

## Psalms 118:163

I have hated and abhorred iniquity; but I have loved thy law.


<a id="org15e314c"></a>

## Psalms 118:164

Seven times a day I have given praise to thee, for the judgments of thy justice.


<a id="org681a474"></a>

## Psalms 118:165

Much peace have they that love thy law, and to them there is no stumbling block.


<a id="org408e2f0"></a>

## Psalms 118:166

I looked for thy salvation, O Lord: and I loved thy commandments.


<a id="org54a4c6b"></a>

## Psalms 118:167

My soul hath kept thy testimonies and hath loved them exceedingly.


<a id="org1affc03"></a>

## Psalms 118:168

I have kept thy commandments and thy testimonies: because all my ways are in thy sight.


<a id="org09240ad"></a>

## Psalms 118:169

Let my supplication, O Lord, come near in thy sight: give me understanding according to thy word.


<a id="org8e5ec48"></a>

## Psalms 118:170

Let my request come in before thee; deliver thou me according to thy word.


<a id="orgd87b1e0"></a>

## Psalms 118:171

My lips shall utter a hymn, when thou shalt teach me thy justifications.


<a id="org1d2ce42"></a>

## Psalms 118:172

My tongue shall pronounce thy word: because all thy commandments are justice.


<a id="org6491065"></a>

## Psalms 118:173

Let thy hand be with me to save me; for I have chosen thy precepts.


<a id="orgdb129b0"></a>

## Psalms 118:174

I have longed for thy salvation, O Lord; and thy law is my meditation.


<a id="org7ce9e66"></a>

## Psalms 118:175

My soul shall live and shall praise thee: and thy judgments shall help me.


<a id="org67a04b1"></a>

## Psalms 118:176

I have gone astray like a sheep that is lost: seek thy servant, because I have not forgotten thy commandments. 


<a id="orgfc9f91f"></a>

# Psalms 119


<a id="orge711b59"></a>

## Psalms 119:1

In my trouble I cried to the Lord: and he heard me.


<a id="orgbc5a939"></a>

## Psalms 119:2

O Lord, deliver my soul from wicked lips, and a deceitful tongue.


<a id="org000a17f"></a>

## Psalms 119:3

What shall be given to thee, or what shall be added to thee, to a deceitful tongue?


<a id="org798906e"></a>

## Psalms 119:4

The sharp arrows of the mighty, with coals that lay waste.


<a id="org75cb014"></a>

## Psalms 119:5

Woe is me, that my sojourning is prolonged! I have dwelt with the inhabitants of Cedar:


<a id="orgfa756e2"></a>

## Psalms 119:6

My soul hath been long a sojourner.


<a id="org79902a2"></a>

## Psalms 119:7

With them that hated peace I was peaceable: when I spoke to them they fought against me without cause. 


<a id="orgc461bbd"></a>

# Psalms 120


<a id="org2ebf3ae"></a>

## Psalms 120:1

I have lifted up my eyes to the mountains, from whence help shall come to me.


<a id="orgc9f7afa"></a>

## Psalms 120:2

My help is from the Lord, who made heaven and earth.


<a id="org1ccb1e8"></a>

## Psalms 120:3

May he not suffer thy foot to be moved: neither let him slumber that keepeth thee.


<a id="org7987946"></a>

## Psalms 120:4

Behold he shall neither slumber nor sleep, that keepeth Israel.


<a id="orgb193163"></a>

## Psalms 120:5

The Lord is thy keeper, the Lord is thy protection upon thy right hand.


<a id="orgace1f2a"></a>

## Psalms 120:6

The sun shall not burn thee by day: nor the moon by night.


<a id="org7490450"></a>

## Psalms 120:7

The Lord keepeth thee from all evil: may the Lord keep thy soul.


<a id="org1edf72e"></a>

## Psalms 120:8

May the Lord keep thy coming in and thy going out; from henceforth now and for ever. 


<a id="orgecae20c"></a>

# Psalms 121


<a id="orgf1f762b"></a>

## Psalms 121:1

A gradual canticle. I rejoiced at the things that were said to me: We shall go into the house of the Lord.


<a id="orgf6acd21"></a>

## Psalms 121:2

Our feet were standing in thy courts, O Jerusalem.


<a id="org8ff1626"></a>

## Psalms 121:3

Jerusalem, which is built as a city, which is compact together.


<a id="org1639e4a"></a>

## Psalms 121:4

For thither did the tribes go up, the tribes of the Lord: the testimony of Israel, to praise the name of the Lord.


<a id="org5a4010c"></a>

## Psalms 121:5

Because their seats have sat in judgment, seats upon the house of David.


<a id="org0e34c8b"></a>

## Psalms 121:6

Pray ye for the things that are for the peace of Jerusalem: and abundance for them that love thee.


<a id="org1f86347"></a>

## Psalms 121:7

Let peace be in thy strength: and abundance in thy towers.


<a id="org3dd609d"></a>

## Psalms 121:8

For the sake of my brethren, and of my neighbours, I spoke peace of thee.


<a id="org6083292"></a>

## Psalms 121:9

Because of the house of the Lord our God, I have sought good things for thee. 


<a id="orgc37650e"></a>

# Psalms 122


<a id="org9a65a87"></a>

## Psalms 122:1

To thee have I lifted up my eyes, who dwellest in heaven.


<a id="org0dead91"></a>

## Psalms 122:2

Behold as the eyes of servants are on the hands of their masters, As the eyes of the handmaid are on the hands of her mistress: so are our eyes unto the Lord our God, until he have mercy on us.


<a id="orgfe1044a"></a>

## Psalms 122:3

Have mercy on us, O Lord, have mercy on us: for we are greatly filled with contempt.


<a id="org6e9f179"></a>

## Psalms 122:4

For our soul is greatly filled: we are a reproach to the rich, and contempt to the proud. 


<a id="orgb8c7577"></a>

# Psalms 123


<a id="org7bc1d9c"></a>

## Psalms 123:1

A gradual canticle. If it had not been that the Lord was with us, let Israel now say:


<a id="org6e51f73"></a>

## Psalms 123:2

If it had not been that the Lord was with us, When men rose up against us,


<a id="org0c1e2d5"></a>

## Psalms 123:3

Perhaps they had swallowed us up alive. When their fury was enkindled against us,


<a id="orgfac34a7"></a>

## Psalms 123:4

Perhaps the waters had swallowed us up.


<a id="org2a271dc"></a>

## Psalms 123:5

Our soul hath passed through a torrent: perhaps our soul had passed through a water insupportable.


<a id="orgf37dce1"></a>

## Psalms 123:6

Blessed be the Lord, who hath not given us to be a prey to their teeth.


<a id="orgb3445be"></a>

## Psalms 123:7

Our soul hath been delivered as a sparrow out of the snare of the fowlers. The snare is broken, and we are delivered.


<a id="orgc47eacc"></a>

## Psalms 123:8

Our help is in the name of the Lord, who made heaven and earth. 


<a id="orgf7c05bc"></a>

# Psalms 124


<a id="org51f6d68"></a>

## Psalms 124:1

A gradual canticle. They that trust in the Lord shall be as mount Sion: he shall not be moved for ever that dwelleth


<a id="orgb432efe"></a>

## Psalms 124:2

In Jerusalem. Mountains are round about it: so the Lord is round about his people from henceforth now and for ever.


<a id="orgd1bca22"></a>

## Psalms 124:3

For the Lord will not leave the rod of sinners upon the lot of the just: that the just may not stretch forth their hands to iniquity.


<a id="orge3c9d5a"></a>

## Psalms 124:4

Do good, O Lord, to those that are good, and to the upright of heart.


<a id="org3291a74"></a>

## Psalms 124:5

But such as turn aside into bonds, the Lord shall lead out with the workers of iniquity: peace upon Israel. 


<a id="orgcdafeff"></a>

# Psalms 125


<a id="org3a961e5"></a>

## Psalms 125:1

A gradual canticle. When the Lord brought back the captivity of Sion, we became like men comforted.


<a id="org7d7a66a"></a>

## Psalms 125:2

Then was our mouth filled with gladness; and our tongue with joy. Then shall they say among the Gentiles: The Lord hath done great things for them.


<a id="orgf13cfb5"></a>

## Psalms 125:3

The Lord hath done great things for us: we are become joyful.


<a id="org01c48d8"></a>

## Psalms 125:4

Turn again our captivity, O Lord, as a stream in the south.


<a id="org337aff4"></a>

## Psalms 125:5

They that sow in tears shall reap in joy.


<a id="org582e1c5"></a>

## Psalms 125:6

Going they went and wept, casting their seeds.


<a id="orgceabe54"></a>

## Psalms 125:7

But coming they shall come with joyfulness, carrying their sheaves. 


<a id="org0af93de"></a>

# Psalms 126


<a id="orgc0b5e96"></a>

## Psalms 126:1

A gradual canticle of Solomon. Unless the Lord build the house, they labour in vain that build it. Unless the Lord keep the city, he watcheth in vain that keepeth it.


<a id="org2b8b55f"></a>

## Psalms 126:2

It is vain for you to rise before light, rise ye after you have sitten, you that eat the bread of sorrow. When he shall give sleep to his beloved,


<a id="org07e23d3"></a>

## Psalms 126:3

Behold the inheritance of the Lord are children: the reward, the fruit of the womb.


<a id="org8ccabcd"></a>

## Psalms 126:4

As arrows in the hand of the mighty, so the children of them that have been shaken.


<a id="org49708f5"></a>

## Psalms 126:5

Blessed is the man that hath filled the desire with them; he shall not be confounded when he shall speak to his enemies in the gate.

# Psalms 127

<a id="orgfc8c6f1"></a>

For thou shalt eat the labours of thy hands: blessed art thou, and it shall be well with thee.


<a id="org866a602"></a>

## Psalms 127:3

<a id="org341acf8"></a>

## Psalms 127:4

<a id="orga2d28f7"></a>

## Psalms 127:5

<a id="org422b987"></a>

## Psalms 127:6

# Psalms 128


<a id="org4868db8"></a>

## Psalms 128:1

A gradual canticle. Often have they fought against me from my youth, let Israel now say.


<a id="orge30eba2"></a>

## Psalms 128:2

Often have they fought against me from my youth: but they could not prevail over me.


<a id="org745a059"></a>

## Psalms 128:3

The wicked have wrought upon my back: they have lengthened their iniquity.


<a id="org6a11e25"></a>

## Psalms 128:4

The Lord who is just will cut the necks of sinners:


<a id="org96646f3"></a>

## Psalms 128:5

Let them all be confounded and turned back that hate Sion.


<a id="orge57e5d2"></a>

## Psalms 128:6

<a id="orgf54a522"></a>

## Psalms 128:7

Who with the mower filleth not his hand: nor he that gathereth sheaves his bosom.


<a id="orgc6f017d"></a>

## Psalms 128:8

And they that passed by have not said: The blessing of the Lord be upon you: we have blessed you in the name of the Lord.

# Psalms 129


<a id="orgf8c8237"></a>

<a id="org7ea7899"></a>

<a id="org4bf5ae0"></a>

## Psalms 129:3

<a id="org94100e1"></a>

## Psalms 129:4

<a id="org3e15fe0"></a>

## Psalms 129:5

my soul hath hoped in the Lord.


<a id="orgf234efb"></a>

## Psalms 129:6

## Psalms 129:7

<a id="org9628fe6"></a>

# Psalms 130


<a id="orgfeefb2b"></a>

<a id="org3029040"></a>

## Psalms 130:2

<a id="org4599581"></a>

## Psalms 130:3

# Psalms 131


<a id="org4155071"></a>

## Psalms 131:1

A gradual canticle. O Lord, remember David, and all his meekness.


<a id="orgafa20ad"></a>

## Psalms 131:2

How he swore to the Lord, he vowed a vow to the God of Jacob:


<a id="org6c63269"></a>

## Psalms 131:3

<a id="orgfa1e85f"></a>

## Psalms 131:4

<a id="org2ba82d6"></a>

## Psalms 131:5

<a id="org3c6ed21"></a>

## Psalms 131:6

Behold we have heard of it in Ephrata: we have found it in the fields of the wood.


<a id="orgaf0f426"></a>

## Psalms 131:7

We will go into his tabernacle: we will adore in the place where his feet stood.


<a id="org42f36bb"></a>

## Psalms 131:8

Arise, O Lord, into thy resting place: thou and the ark, which thou hast sanctified.


<a id="org068f446"></a>

## Psalms 131:9

<a id="org45caa9f"></a>

<a id="org1473061"></a>

## Psalms 131:11

<a id="org5a6f5d5"></a>

## Psalms 131:12

<a id="orgdbc8b94"></a>

## Psalms 131:13

For the Lord hath chosen Sion: he hath chosen it for his dwelling.


<a id="org00960c5"></a>

## Psalms 131:14

<a id="orge91908b"></a>

## Psalms 131:15

Blessing I will bless her widow: I will satisfy her poor with bread.


<a id="org7003992"></a>

## Psalms 131:16

<a id="org09edfc1"></a>

## Psalms 131:17

There will I bring forth a horn to David: I have prepared a lamp for my anointed.


<a id="org4b87d00"></a>

## Psalms 131:18

His enemies I will clothe with confusion: but upon him shall my sanctification flourish.
