# Psalms 134


<a id="org543a460"></a>

## Psalms 134:1

Alleluia. Praise ye the name of the Lord: O you his servants, praise the Lord:


<a id="org94e396b"></a>

## Psalms 134:2

You that stand in the house of the Lord, in the courts of the house of our God.


<a id="orgb3aff8e"></a>

## Psalms 134:3

Praise ye the Lord, for the Lord is good: sing ye to his name, for it is sweet.


<a id="org152daa9"></a>

## Psalms 134:4

For the Lord hath chosen Jacob unto himself: Israel for his own possession.


<a id="org850e804"></a>

## Psalms 134:5

For I have known that the Lord is great, and our God is above all gods.


<a id="org9154c12"></a>

## Psalms 134:6

Whatsoever the Lord pleased he hath done, in heaven, in earth, in the sea, and in all the deeps.


<a id="org74a9745"></a>

## Psalms 134:7

He bringeth up clouds from the end of the earth: he hath made lightnings for the rain. He bringeth forth winds out of his stores:


<a id="orgbc1fae8"></a>

## Psalms 134:8

He slew the firstborn of Egypt from man even unto beast.


<a id="orgea83d38"></a>

## Psalms 134:9

He sent forth signs and wonders in the midst of thee, O Egypt: upon Pharao, and upon all his servants.


<a id="org17c37e7"></a>

## Psalms 134:10

He smote many nations, and slew mighty kings:


<a id="orga210cd5"></a>

## Psalms 134:11

Sehon king of the Amorrhites, and Og king of Basan, and all the kingdoms of Chanaan.


<a id="org54afded"></a>

## Psalms 134:12

And gave their land for an inheritance, for an inheritance to his people Israel.


<a id="org638f0ec"></a>

## Psalms 134:13

Thy name, O Lord, is for ever: thy memorial, O Lord, unto all generations.


<a id="orgfd48470"></a>

## Psalms 134:14

For the Lord will judge his people, and will be entreated in favour of his servants.


<a id="org6d99983"></a>

## Psalms 134:15

The idols of the Gentiles are silver and gold, the works of men&rsquo;s hands.


<a id="org9cf5898"></a>

## Psalms 134:16

They have a mouth, but they speak not: they have eyes, but they see not.


<a id="org19740ca"></a>

## Psalms 134:17

They have ears, but they hear not: neither is there any breath in their mouths.


<a id="org37cb183"></a>

## Psalms 134:18

Let them that make them be like to them: and every one that trusteth in them.


<a id="org1c9faef"></a>

## Psalms 134:19

Bless the Lord, O house of Israel: bless the Lord, O house of Aaron.


<a id="org72684b1"></a>

## Psalms 134:20

Bless the Lord, O house of Levi: you that fear the Lord, bless the Lord.


<a id="orge7b30b7"></a>

## Psalms 134:21

Blessed be the Lord out of Sion, who dwelleth in Jerusalem. 


<a id="org530783f"></a>

# Psalms 135


<a id="org0e7e656"></a>

## Psalms 135:1

Alleluia. Praise the Lord, for he is good: for his mercy endureth for ever.


<a id="orgdcecf9f"></a>

## Psalms 135:2

Praise ye the God of gods: for his mercy endureth for ever.


<a id="org5ffa525"></a>

## Psalms 135:3

Praise ye the Lord of lords: for his mercy endureth for ever.


<a id="org0f16768"></a>

## Psalms 135:4

Who alone doth great wonders: for his mercy endureth for ever.


<a id="orgbd453e9"></a>

## Psalms 135:5

Who made the heavens in understanding: for his mercy endureth for ever.


<a id="orgd89c8ee"></a>

## Psalms 135:6

Who established the earth above the waters: for his mercy endureth for ever.


<a id="org8d3a00a"></a>

## Psalms 135:7

Who made the great lights: for his mercy endureth for ever.


<a id="org4abf0d0"></a>

## Psalms 135:8

The sun to rule the day: for his mercy endureth for ever.


<a id="org11d7625"></a>

## Psalms 135:9

The moon and the stars to rule the night: for his mercy endureth for ever.


<a id="org3e3fb61"></a>

## Psalms 135:10

Who smote Egypt with their firstborn: for his mercy endureth for ever.


<a id="org8a0ea19"></a>

## Psalms 135:11

Who brought out Israel from among them: for his mercy endureth for ever.


<a id="org74a025f"></a>

## Psalms 135:12

With a mighty hand and with a stretched out arm: for his mercy endureth for ever.


<a id="org42f029f"></a>

## Psalms 135:13

Who divided the Red Sea into parts: for his mercy endureth for ever.


<a id="org001dd5d"></a>

## Psalms 135:14

And brought out Israel through the midst thereof: for his mercy endureth for ever.


<a id="org4284699"></a>

## Psalms 135:15

And overthrew Pharao and his host in the Red Sea: for his mercy endureth for ever.


<a id="orge7e18b5"></a>

## Psalms 135:16

Who led his people through the desert: for his mercy endureth for ever.


<a id="orgf206798"></a>

## Psalms 135:17

Who smote great kings: for his mercy endureth for ever.


<a id="org1f9b7e6"></a>

## Psalms 135:18

And slew strong kings: for his mercy endureth for ever.


<a id="orge064ff1"></a>

## Psalms 135:19

Sehon king of the Amorrhites: for his mercy endureth for ever.


<a id="org19560b1"></a>

## Psalms 135:20

And Og king of Basan: for his mercy endureth for ever.


<a id="org43766e0"></a>

## Psalms 135:21

<a id="orgd43e2b6"></a>

## Psalms 135:22

<a id="org5559247"></a>

<a id="org955f37b"></a>

## Psalms 135:24

<a id="org5db5b4a"></a>

## Psalms 135:25

<a id="orgd7d9ec9"></a>

<a id="orga1abf5b"></a>

# Psalms 136


<a id="org20a1ef2"></a>

## Psalms 136:1

Upon the rivers of Babylon, there we sat and wept: when we remembered Sion:


<a id="orgc7ea38c"></a>

## Psalms 136:2

On the willows in the midst thereof we hung up our instruments.


<a id="org8a2902f"></a>

## Psalms 136:3

For there they that led us into captivity required of us the words of songs. And they that carried us away, said: Sing ye to us a hymn of the songs of Sion.


<a id="orgbd7f717"></a>

## Psalms 136:4

How shall we sing the song of the Lord in a strange land?


<a id="orgd4c7566"></a>

## Psalms 136:5

If I forget thee, O Jerusalem, let my right hand be forgotten.


<a id="org29b2447"></a>

## Psalms 136:6

Let my tongue cleave to my jaws, if I do not remember thee: If I make not Jerusalem the beginning of my joy.


<a id="org831f082"></a>

## Psalms 136:7

Remember, O Lord, the children of Edom, in the day of Jerusalem: Who say: Rase it, rase it, even to the foundation thereof.


<a id="org28c79a8"></a>

## Psalms 136:8

O daughter of Babylon, miserable: blessed shall he be who shall repay thee thy payment which thou hast paid us.


<a id="orgb7ceeca"></a>

## Psalms 136:9

Blessed be he that shall take and dash thy little ones against the rock. 


<a id="org6ed4f91"></a>

# Psalms 137


<a id="org2e2676c"></a>

## Psalms 137:1

For David himself. I will praise thee, O Lord, with my whole heart: for thou hast heard the words of my mouth. I will sing praise to thee in the sight of the angels:


<a id="org08eb2de"></a>

## Psalms 137:2

I will worship towards thy holy temple, and I will give glory to thy name. For thy mercy, and for thy truth: for thou hast magnified thy holy name above all.


<a id="org982731f"></a>

## Psalms 137:3

In what day soever I shall call upon thee, hear me: thou shalt multiply strength in my soul.


<a id="orgc903be8"></a>

## Psalms 137:4

May all the kings of the earth give glory to thee: for they have heard all the words of thy mouth.


<a id="org1638114"></a>

## Psalms 137:5

And let them sing in the ways of the Lord: for great is the glory of the Lord.


<a id="org38cadc8"></a>

## Psalms 137:6

For the Lord is high, and looketh on the low: and the high he knoweth afar off.


<a id="org35170f7"></a>

## Psalms 137:7

If I shall walk in the midst of tribulation, thou wilt quicken me: and thou hast stretched forth thy hand against the wrath of my enemies: and thy right hand hath saved me.


<a id="org91d7063"></a>

## Psalms 137:8

The Lord will repay for me: thy mercy, O Lord, endureth for ever: O despise not the works of thy hands. 


<a id="org2f4f750"></a>

# Psalms 138


<a id="orgb349d02"></a>

## Psalms 138:1

Unto the end, a psalm of David. Lord, thou hast proved me, and known me:


<a id="org4778b2b"></a>

## Psalms 138:2

Thou hast known my sitting down, and my rising up.


<a id="org25ed544"></a>

## Psalms 138:3

Thou hast understood my thoughts afar off: my path and my line thou hast searched out.


<a id="orgb95f50d"></a>

## Psalms 138:4

And thou hast foreseen all my ways: for there is no speech in my tongue.


<a id="org8a303d8"></a>

## Psalms 138:5

Behold, O Lord, thou hast known all things, the last and those of old: thou hast formed me, and hast laid thy hand upon me.


<a id="orgab1c33e"></a>

## Psalms 138:6

Thy knowledge is become wonderful to me: it is high, and I cannot reach to it.


<a id="org52527d3"></a>

## Psalms 138:7

Whither shall I go from thy spirit? or whither shall I flee from thy face?


<a id="org03a05c6"></a>

## Psalms 138:8

If I ascend into heaven, thou art there: if I descend into hell, thou art present.


<a id="orgabbe6a9"></a>

## Psalms 138:9

If I take my wings early in the morning, and dwell in the uttermost parts of the sea:


<a id="orge957f65"></a>

## Psalms 138:10

Even there also shall thy hand lead me: and thy right hand shall hold me.


<a id="org9305e3d"></a>

## Psalms 138:11

And I said: Perhaps darkness shall cover me: and night shall be my light in my pleasures.


<a id="org6a606b2"></a>

## Psalms 138:12

But darkness shall not be dark to thee, and night shall be light all the day: the darkness thereof, and the light thereof are alike to thee.


<a id="org735d306"></a>

## Psalms 138:13

For thou hast possessed my reins: thou hast protected me from my mother&rsquo;s womb.


<a id="org41fac3d"></a>

## Psalms 138:14

I will praise thee, for thou art fearfully magnified: wonderful are thy works, and my soul knoweth right well.


<a id="org5efaf60"></a>

## Psalms 138:15

My bone is not hidden from thee, which thou hast made in secret: and my substance in the lower parts of the earth.


<a id="orged2ecc9"></a>

## Psalms 138:16

Thy eyes did see my imperfect being, and in thy book all shall be written: days shall be formed, and no one in them.


<a id="org6064215"></a>

## Psalms 138:17

But to me thy friends, O God, are made exceedingly honourable: their principality is exceedingly strengthened.


<a id="org1bd6fe8"></a>

## Psalms 138:18

I will number them, and they shall be multiplied above the sand, I rose up and am still with thee.


<a id="org20d479c"></a>

## Psalms 138:19

If thou wilt kill the wicked, O God: ye men of blood, depart from me:


<a id="org916c50c"></a>

## Psalms 138:20

Because you say in thought: They shall receive thy cities in vain.


<a id="orgf646aab"></a>

## Psalms 138:21

Have I not hated them, O Lord, that hated thee: and pined away because of thy enemies?


<a id="orgb023ebd"></a>

## Psalms 138:22

I have hated them with a perfect hatred: and they are become enemies to me.


<a id="org950283d"></a>

## Psalms 138:23

Prove me, O God, and know my heart: examine me, and know my paths.


<a id="org5f474b1"></a>

## Psalms 138:24

And see if there be in me the way of iniquity: and lead me in the eternal way. 


<a id="orgac56744"></a>

# Psalms 139


<a id="org86cee73"></a>

## Psalms 139:1

Unto the end, a psalm of David.


<a id="org856f69a"></a>

## Psalms 139:2

Deliver me, O Lord, from the evil man: rescue me from the unjust man.


<a id="org0e90dd4"></a>

## Psalms 139:3

Who have devised iniquities in their hearts: all the day long they designed battles.


<a id="orgfd84200"></a>

## Psalms 139:4

They have sharpened their tongues like a serpent: the venom of asps is under their lips.


<a id="org49a20dd"></a>

## Psalms 139:5

Keep me, O Lord, from the hand of the wicked: and from unjust men deliver me. Who have proposed to supplant my steps:


<a id="org3dd00ed"></a>

## Psalms 139:6

The proud have hidden a net for me. And they have stretched out cords for a snare: they have laid for me a stumblingblock by the wayside.


<a id="org7508041"></a>

## Psalms 139:7

I said to the Lord: Thou art my God: hear, O Lord, the voice of my supplication.


<a id="orge9bdf37"></a>

## Psalms 139:8

O Lord, Lord, the strength of my salvation: thou hast overshadowed my head in the day of battle.


<a id="org4f33059"></a>

## Psalms 139:9

Give me not up, O Lord, from my desire to the wicked: they have plotted against me; do not thou forsake me, lest they should triumph.


<a id="org919ab15"></a>

## Psalms 139:10

The head of them compassing me about: the labour of their lips shall overwhelm them.


<a id="org1ed5ba2"></a>

## Psalms 139:11

Burning coals shall fall upon them; thou wilt cast them down into the fire: in miseries they shall not be able to stand.


<a id="orgd791fb8"></a>

## Psalms 139:12

A man full of tongue shall not be established in the earth: evil shall catch the unjust man unto destruction.


<a id="orgb96073e"></a>

## Psalms 139:13

I know that the Lord will do justice to the needy, and will revenge the poor.


<a id="orgf23bfed"></a>

## Psalms 139:14

But as for the just, they shall give glory to thy name: and the upright shall dwell with thy countenance. 


<a id="orgdc5436b"></a>

# Psalms 140


<a id="orge4e97a8"></a>

## Psalms 140:1

I have cried to thee, O Lord, hear me: hearken to my voice, when I cry to thee.


<a id="orgf2728d2"></a>

## Psalms 140:2

Let my prayer be directed as incense in thy sight; the lifting up of my hands, as evening sacrifice.


<a id="orgf8aa913"></a>

## Psalms 140:3

Set a watch, O Lord, before my mouth: and a door round about my lips.


<a id="org3d2e146"></a>

## Psalms 140:4

Incline not my heart to evil words; to make excuses in sins. With men that work iniquity: and I will not communicate with the choicest of them.


<a id="org181ff3f"></a>

## Psalms 140:5

The just man shall correct me in mercy, and shall reprove me: but let not the oil of the sinner fatten my head. For my prayer shall still be against the things with which they are well pleased:


<a id="org4159cb0"></a>

## Psalms 140:6

Their judges falling upon the rock have been swallowed up. They shall hear my words, for they have prevailed:


<a id="org4bdc594"></a>

## Psalms 140:7

As when the thickness of the earth is broken up upon the ground: Our bones are scattered by the side of hell.


<a id="org537be76"></a>

## Psalms 140:8

But to thee, O Lord, Lord, are my eyes: in thee have I put my trust, take not away my soul.


<a id="org536b92b"></a>

## Psalms 140:9

Keep me from the snare, which they have laid for me, and from the stumblingblocks of them that work iniquity.


<a id="orgaa76c7c"></a>

## Psalms 140:10

The wicked shall fall in his net: I am alone until I pass. 


<a id="org60e148d"></a>

# Psalms 141


<a id="org2cb00a6"></a>

## Psalms 141:1

Of understanding for David, A prayer when he was in the cave.


<a id="orgd70d9ca"></a>

## Psalms 141:2

I cried to the Lord with my voice: with my voice I made supplication to the Lord.


<a id="orga428431"></a>

## Psalms 141:3

In his sight I pour out my prayer, and before him I declare my trouble:


<a id="org52d369a"></a>

## Psalms 141:4

When my spirit failed me, then thou knewest my paths. In this way wherein I walked, they have hidden a snare for me.


<a id="org5ae12d3"></a>

## Psalms 141:5

I looked on my right hand, and beheld, and there was no one that would know me. Flight hath failed me: and there is no one that hath regard to my soul.


<a id="org7aae46a"></a>

## Psalms 141:6

I cried to thee, O Lord: I said: Thou art my hope, my portion in the land of the living.


<a id="org146ef30"></a>

## Psalms 141:7

Attend to my supplication: for I am brought very low. Deliver me from my persecutors; for they are stronger than I.


<a id="orge4f18aa"></a>

## Psalms 141:8

Bring my soul out of prison, that I may praise thy name: the just wait for me, until thou reward me. 


<a id="org578d107"></a>

# Psalms 142


<a id="org5ec96bb"></a>

## Psalms 142:1

A psalm of David, when his son Absalom pursued him. Hear, O Lord, my prayer: give ear to my supplication in thy truth: hear me in thy justice.


<a id="orgf972610"></a>

## Psalms 142:2

And enter not into judgment with thy servant: for in thy sight no man living shall be justified.


<a id="org948f766"></a>

## Psalms 142:3

For the enemy hath persecuted my soul: he hath brought down my life to the earth. He hath made me to dwell in darkness as those that have been dead of old:


<a id="orgddabab1"></a>

## Psalms 142:4

And my spirit is in anguish within me: my heart within me is troubled.


<a id="orgc8ce667"></a>

## Psalms 142:5

I remembered the days of old, I meditated on all thy works: I meditated upon the works of thy hands.


<a id="org8948ca3"></a>

## Psalms 142:6

I stretched forth my hands to thee: my soul is as earth without water unto thee.


<a id="org03bbc19"></a>

## Psalms 142:7

Hear me speedily, O Lord: my spirit hath fainted away. Turn not away thy face from me, lest I be like unto them that go down into the pit.


<a id="org4225cef"></a>

## Psalms 142:8

Cause me to hear thy mercy in the morning; for in thee have I hoped. Make the way known to me, wherein I should walk: for I have lifted up my soul to thee.


<a id="org5b184c5"></a>

## Psalms 142:9

Deliver me from my enemies, O Lord, to thee have I fled:


<a id="org509b573"></a>

## Psalms 142:10

Teach me to do thy will, for thou art my God. Thy good spirit shall lead me into the right land:


<a id="org6e21ecd"></a>

## Psalms 142:11

for thy name&rsquo;s sake, O Lord, thou wilt quicken me in thy justice. Thou wilt bring my soul out of trouble:


<a id="orgcd964d2"></a>

## Psalms 142:12

And in thy mercy thou wilt destroy my enemies. And thou wilt cut off all them that afflict my soul: for I am thy servant. 


<a id="orgf774738"></a>

# Psalms 143


<a id="org8a936b9"></a>

## Psalms 143:1

Blessed be the Lord my God, who teacheth my hands to fight, and my fingers to war.


<a id="org43ab0f5"></a>

## Psalms 143:2

My mercy, and my refuge: my support, and my deliverer: My protector, and I have hoped in him: who subdueth my people under me.


<a id="org0077d3f"></a>

## Psalms 143:3

Lord, what is man, that thou art made known to him? or the son of man, that thou makest account of him?


<a id="org0a0bf11"></a>

## Psalms 143:4

Man is like to vanity: his days pass away like a shadow.


<a id="orgb62a357"></a>

## Psalms 143:5

Lord, bow down thy heavens and descend: touch the mountains, and they shall smoke.


<a id="orgadf6902"></a>

## Psalms 143:6

Send forth lightning, and thou shalt scatter them: shoot out thy arrows, and thou shalt trouble them.


<a id="org7c14dc8"></a>

## Psalms 143:7

Put forth thy hand from on high, take me out, and deliver me from many waters: from the hand of strange children:


<a id="orgd90525b"></a>

## Psalms 143:8

Whose mouth hath spoken vanity: and their right hand is the right hand of iniquity.


<a id="orgd95259d"></a>

## Psalms 143:9

To thee, O God, I will sing a new canticle: on the psaltery and an instrument of ten strings I will sing praises to thee.


<a id="orge1fcfbc"></a>

## Psalms 143:10

Who givest salvation to kings: who hast redeemed thy servant David from the malicious sword:


<a id="org0f4cf95"></a>

## Psalms 143:11

Deliver me, And rescue me out of the hand of strange children; whose mouth hath spoken vanity: and their right hand is the right hand of iniquity:


<a id="orge891b2f"></a>

## Psalms 143:12

Whose sons are as new plants in their youth: Their daughters decked out, adorned round about after the similitude of a temple:


<a id="org2216cd4"></a>

## Psalms 143:13

Their storehouses full, flowing out of this into that. Their sheep fruitful in young, abounding in their goings forth:


<a id="org949ec45"></a>

## Psalms 143:14

Their oxen fat. There is no breach of wall, nor passage, nor crying out in their streets.


<a id="org824a10a"></a>

## Psalms 143:15

They have called the people happy, that hath these things: but happy is that people whose God is the Lord. 


<a id="org2d7d352"></a>

# Psalms 144


<a id="org4a271a1"></a>

## Psalms 144:1

Praise, for David himself. I will extol thee, O God my king: and I will bless thy name for ever; yea, for ever and ever.


<a id="orgd38d989"></a>

## Psalms 144:2

Every day will I bless thee: and I will praise thy name for ever; yea, for ever and ever.


<a id="orgd991912"></a>

## Psalms 144:3

Great is the Lord, and greatly to be praised: and of his greatness there is no end.


<a id="org35547af"></a>

## Psalms 144:4

Generation and generation shall praise thy works: and they shall declare thy power.


<a id="orgd9152b9"></a>

## Psalms 144:5

They shall speak of the magnificence of the glory of thy holiness: and shall tell thy wondrous works.


<a id="org4bc0244"></a>

## Psalms 144:6

And they shall speak of the might of thy terrible acts: and shall declare thy greatness.


<a id="orgafb31d2"></a>

## Psalms 144:7

They shall publish the memory of the abundance of thy sweetness: and shall rejoice in thy justice.


<a id="orgd84ef9d"></a>

## Psalms 144:8

The Lord is gracious and merciful: patient and plenteous in mercy.


<a id="org4a2e621"></a>

## Psalms 144:9

The Lord is sweet to all: and his tender mercies are over all his works.


<a id="orgd0e6004"></a>

## Psalms 144:10

Let all thy works, O Lord, praise thee: and let thy saints bless thee.


<a id="orgaff5481"></a>

## Psalms 144:11

They shall speak of the glory of thy kingdom: and shall tell of thy power:


<a id="org2fecc6d"></a>

## Psalms 144:12

To make thy might known to the sons of men: and the glory of the magnificence of thy kingdom.


<a id="org637f41a"></a>

## Psalms 144:13

Thy kingdom is a kingdom of all ages: and thy dominion endureth throughout all generations. The Lord is faithful in all his words: and holy in all his works.


<a id="orgb2a095c"></a>

## Psalms 144:14

The Lord lifteth up all that fall: and setteth up all that are cast down.


<a id="org4ddc76e"></a>

## Psalms 144:15

The eyes of all hope in thee, O Lord: and thou givest them meat in due season.


<a id="orgdc26b94"></a>

## Psalms 144:16

Thou openest thy hand, and fillest with blessing every living creature.


<a id="org87e1ade"></a>

## Psalms 144:17

The Lord is just in all his ways: and holy in all his works.


<a id="orgd9b45bb"></a>

## Psalms 144:18

The Lord is nigh unto all them that call upon him: to all that call upon him in truth.


<a id="org713c89a"></a>

## Psalms 144:19

He will do the will of them that fear him: and he will hear their prayer, and save them.


<a id="orge06daed"></a>

## Psalms 144:20

The Lord keepeth all them that love him; but all the wicked he will destroy.


<a id="orgd4ea585"></a>

## Psalms 144:21

My mouth shall speak the praise of the Lord: and let all flesh bless his holy name forever; yea, for ever and ever. 


<a id="org2db9f17"></a>

# Psalms 145


<a id="org796833f"></a>

## Psalms 145:1

Alleluia, of Aggeus and Zacharias.


<a id="org460649c"></a>

## Psalms 145:2

Praise the Lord, O my soul, in my life I will praise the Lord: I will sing to my God as long as I shall be. Put not your trust in princes:


<a id="orgdc5a89c"></a>

## Psalms 145:3

In the children of men, in whom there is no salvation.


<a id="orgfca0f41"></a>

## Psalms 145:4

His spirit shall go forth, and he shall return into his earth: in that day all their thoughts shall perish.


<a id="orgcf426fd"></a>

## Psalms 145:5

Blessed is he who hath the God of Jacob for his helper, whose hope is in the Lord his God:


<a id="orgac76de3"></a>

## Psalms 145:6

Who made heaven and earth, the sea, and all things that are in them.


<a id="org379c7f6"></a>

## Psalms 145:7

Who keepeth truth for ever: who executeth judgment for them that suffer wrong: who giveth food to the hungry. The Lord looseth them that are fettered:


<a id="org13d2282"></a>

## Psalms 145:8

The Lord enlighteneth the blind. The Lord lifteth up them that are cast down: the Lord loveth the just.


<a id="orgd3c07ce"></a>

## Psalms 145:9

The Lord keepeth the strangers, he will support the fatherless and the widow: and the ways of sinners he will destroy.


<a id="orgd61c6d8"></a>

## Psalms 145:10

The Lord shall reign for ever: thy God, O Sion, unto generation and generation. 


<a id="org4104be0"></a>

# Psalms 146


<a id="orgbdf13dc"></a>

## Psalms 146:1

Alleluia. Praise ye the Lord, because psalm is good: to our God be joyful and comely praise.


<a id="org3c59b05"></a>

## Psalms 146:2

The Lord buildeth up Jerusalem: he will gather together the dispersed of Israel.


<a id="org8282ba8"></a>

## Psalms 146:3

Who healeth the broken of heart, and bindeth up their bruises.


<a id="org9cfeb57"></a>

## Psalms 146:4

Who telleth the number of the stars: and calleth them all by their names.


<a id="orgb9ab4ce"></a>

## Psalms 146:5

Great is our Lord, and great is his power: and of his wisdom there is no number.


<a id="orgdc97c8a"></a>

## Psalms 146:6

The Lord lifteth up the meek, and bringeth the wicked down even to the ground.


<a id="org8408ef1"></a>

## Psalms 146:7

Sing ye to the Lord with praise: sing to our God upon the harp.


<a id="orge7cf472"></a>

## Psalms 146:8

Who covereth the heaven with clouds, and prepareth rain for the earth. Who maketh grass to grow on the mountains, and herbs for the service of men.


<a id="org8957921"></a>

## Psalms 146:9

Who giveth to beasts their food: and to the young ravens that call upon him.


<a id="orgfab20c7"></a>

## Psalms 146:10

He shall not delight in the strength of the horse: nor take pleasure in the legs of a man.


<a id="orgb36afe2"></a>

## Psalms 146:11

The Lord taketh pleasure in them that fear him: and in them that hope in his mercy. 


<a id="org7488f71"></a>

# Psalms 147


<a id="org42e7186"></a>

## Psalms 147:1

Praise the Lord, O Jerusalem: praise thy God, O Sion.


<a id="orgba7196e"></a>

## Psalms 147:2

Because he hath strengthened the bolts of thy gates, he hath blessed thy children within thee.


<a id="orgb6676a3"></a>

## Psalms 147:3

Who hath placed peace in thy borders: and filleth thee with the fat of corn.


<a id="orge90a9ce"></a>

## Psalms 147:4

Who sendeth forth his speech to the earth: his word runneth swiftly.


<a id="orgb63e571"></a>

## Psalms 147:5

Who giveth snow like wool: scattereth mists like ashes.


<a id="org551c5fe"></a>

## Psalms 147:6

He sendeth his crystal like morsels: who shall stand before the face of his cold?


<a id="org4ec4af8"></a>

## Psalms 147:7

He shall send out his word, and shall melt them: his wind shall blow, and the waters shall run.


<a id="org9ee6677"></a>

## Psalms 147:8

Who declareth his word to Jacob: his justices and his judgments to Israel.


<a id="org1349f6f"></a>

## Psalms 147:9

He hath not done in like manner to every nation: and his judgments he hath not made manifest to them. Alleluia. 


<a id="org841668b"></a>

# Psalms 148


<a id="orgb35ee4f"></a>

## Psalms 148:1

Praise ye the Lord from the heavens: praise ye him in the high places.


<a id="org8eb88d9"></a>

## Psalms 148:2

Praise ye him, all his angels, praise ye him, all his hosts.


<a id="org74c5976"></a>

## Psalms 148:3

Praise ye him, O sun and moon: praise him, all ye stars and light.


<a id="org01d73b7"></a>

## Psalms 148:4

Praise him, ye heavens of heavens: and let all the waters that are above the heavens


<a id="orga259606"></a>

## Psalms 148:5

Praise the name of the Lord. For he spoke, and they were made: he commanded, and they were created.


<a id="org81bdc35"></a>

## Psalms 148:6

He hath established them for ever, and for ages of ages: he hath made a decree, and it shall not pass away.


<a id="orgfb85a5e"></a>

## Psalms 148:7

Praise the Lord from the earth, ye dragons, and all ye deeps:


<a id="orgfc56dc1"></a>

## Psalms 148:8

Fire, hail, snow, ice, stormy winds, which fulfil his word:


<a id="orgc0e7abb"></a>

## Psalms 148:9

Mountains and all hills, fruitful trees and all cedars:


<a id="org02e8cd1"></a>

## Psalms 148:10

Beasts and all cattle: serpents and feathered fowls:


<a id="orge6a16b1"></a>

## Psalms 148:11

Kings of the earth and all people: princes and all judges of the earth:


<a id="org2559676"></a>

## Psalms 148:12

Young men and maidens: let the old with the younger, praise the name of the Lord:


<a id="org2056d29"></a>

## Psalms 148:13

For his name alone is exalted.


<a id="org76833a9"></a>

## Psalms 148:14

The praise of him is above heaven and earth: and he hath exalted the horn of his people. A hymn to all his saints to the children of Israel, a people approaching to him. Alleluia. 


<a id="org8004cf4"></a>

# Psalms 149


<a id="org89afbda"></a>

## Psalms 149:1

Sing ye to the Lord a new canticle: let his praise be in the church of the saints.


<a id="org37f9cbb"></a>

## Psalms 149:2

Let Israel rejoice in him that made him: and let the children of Sion be joyful in their king.


<a id="org3bfc936"></a>

## Psalms 149:3

Let them praise his name in choir: let them sing to him with the timbrel and the psaltery.


<a id="org1d5c684"></a>

## Psalms 149:4

For the Lord is well pleased with his people: and he will exalt the meek unto salvation.


<a id="org0eee22c"></a>

## Psalms 149:5

The saints shall rejoice in glory: they shall be joyful in their beds.


<a id="org1ca65bc"></a>

## Psalms 149:6

The high praises of God shall be in their mouth: and two-edged swords in their hands:


<a id="org97a9e16"></a>

## Psalms 149:7

To execute vengeance upon the nations, chastisements among the people:


<a id="orga6cb134"></a>

## Psalms 149:8

To bind their kings with fetters, and their nobles with manacles of iron.


<a id="org02427a3"></a>

## Psalms 149:9

To execute upon them the judgment that is written: this glory is to all his saints. Alleluia. 


<a id="orgc9fd7b2"></a>

# Psalms 150


<a id="org9130139"></a>

## Psalms 150:1

Praise ye the Lord in his holy places: praise ye him in the firmament of his power.


<a id="org56e13f3"></a>

## Psalms 150:2

Praise ye him for his mighty acts: praise ye him according to the multitude of his greatness.


<a id="org3e02e46"></a>

## Psalms 150:3

Praise him with the sound of trumpet: praise him with psaltery and harp.


<a id="org726b057"></a>

## Psalms 150:4

Praise him with timbrel and choir: praise him with strings and organs.


<a id="org04454b7"></a>

## Psalms 150:5

Praise him on high sounding cymbals: praise him on cymbals of joy: let every spirit praise the Lord. Alleluia.
